Parliamentary elections were held in [[Serbia]] on 17 December 2023 to elect members of the [[National Assembly (Serbia)|National Assembly]]. While they were initially scheduled to be held by 30 April 2026, [[Aleksandar Vučić]], the president of Serbia, called a [[snap election]] in November 2023. In addition to the parliamentary elections, the [[2023 Vojvodina provincial election|Vojvodina provincial election]] and [[2023 Serbian local elections|local elections]] were held in 65 cities and municipalities, including the capital, [[2023 Belgrade City Assembly election|Belgrade]].

The [[Serbian Progressive Party]] (SNS) came to power after the [[2012 Serbian parliamentary election|2012 election]] when it formed a coalition government with the [[Socialist Party of Serbia]]. In the [[2022 Serbian general election|2022 parliamentary election]], SNS lost its [[parliamentary majority]] while opposition parties returned to the National Assembly. The [[United for the Victory of Serbia]] alliance, which placed second, was dissolved shortly after the election. [[Ana Brnabić]], who has been the [[Prime Minister of Serbia|prime minister]] since 2017, and her [[Third cabinet of Ana Brnabić|third cabinet]] were inaugurated in October 2022. Her cabinet saw several changes in 2023; [[Branko Ružić (politician)|Branko Ružić]] resigned and [[Rade Basta]] was dismissed. Brnabić's cabinet has also been involved in the [[North Kosovo crisis (2022–present)|North Kosovo crisis]] and was faced with [[2023 Serbian protests|anti-government protests]] from May to November 2023, which were triggered after the [[Belgrade school shooting]] and a [[Mladenovac and Smederevo shootings|mass murder near Mladenovac and Smederevo]].

Opposition parties organising the protests formed the [[Serbia Against Violence (coalition)|Serbia Against Violence]] coalition in October. The campaign was met with an increase in political tensions, [[Political polarization|polarisation]], and [[voter intimidation]]. Candidates campaigned on issues such as fighting against crime and corruption, decreasing inflation, and the [[Ohrid Agreement (2023)|Ohrid Agreement]]. Despite not being a candidate and no longer being president of SNS, Vučić mainly represented SNS during the campaign. The Republic Electoral Commission proclaimed 18 electoral lists for the parliamentary election.

Monitoring and non-governmental organisations reported that the election day was marked with [[electoral fraud]], mostly in the [[Belgrade]] region. [[ODIHR]] concluded that the elections were well organised, but that SNS had a systematic advantage in the election and abused public funds. The election resulted into SNS regaining its parliamentary majority, despite [[Opinion polling for the 2023 Serbian parliamentary election|opinion polls]] predicting a decrease of support, and SPS suffering from its worst result since the [[2007 Serbian parliamentary election|2007 election]]. The [[We – Voice from the People]] of conspiracy theorist [[Branimir Nestorović]] also unexpectedly gained representation in the National Assembly. [[2023 Serbian election protests|Mass protests]] were held in December, with SPN and other organisers calling for the annulment of election results. [[Miloš Vučević]] of SNS later formed [[Cabinet of Miloš Vučević|his cabinet]] in May 2024.{{TOC limit|3}}

== Background ==
A [[populist]] coalition, led by the [[Serbian Progressive Party]] (SNS), came to power after the [[2012 Serbian parliamentary election|2012 election]], along with the [[Socialist Party of Serbia]] (SPS).<ref>{{Cite web |date=10 May 2012 |title=Izbori 2012: Rezultati i postizborna trgovina |trans-title=2012 elections: Results and post-election trade === North Kosovo crisis ===
{{further|North Kosovo crisis (2022–2024)|Banjska attack}}
[[File:North Kosovo crisis 2022 barricades.jpg|thumb|alt=Two trucks roadblocking in North Kosovo|Tensions between Serbia and Kosovo escalated in July 2022]]
Beginning in July 2022, tensions between Serbia and [[Kosovo]] heightened, firstly due to the expiration of the eleven-year validity period for car documents.<ref>{{Cite web |date=29 July 2022 |title=Građani Srbije koji dolaze na Kosovo dobiće "dokument za ulazak i izlazak" |trans-title=Citizens of Serbia who come to Kosovo will receive "entry and exit documents" |url=https://n1info.rs/vesti/gradjani-srbije-koji-dolaze-na-kosovo-dobice-dokument-za-ulazak-i-izlazak/ |url-status=live October 2023 |website=[[N1 (TV channel)|N1]] |language=sr}}</ref><ref name=":20">{{Cite news |date=1 September 2022 |title=Kosovo pushes ahead with car licensing rule resisted by Serbs |url=https://www.reuters.com/world/europe/kosovo-pushes-ahead-with-car-licensing-rule-resisted-by-ethnic-serbs-2022-09-01/ |url-status=live |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20221028002846/https://www.reuters.com/world/europe/kosovo-pushes-ahead-with-car-licensing-rule-resisted-by-ethnic-serbs-2022-09-01/ |archive-date=28 October 2022 |access-date=14 October 2023 |work=[[Reuters]]}}</ref> After negotiations with the diplomatic representatives of the [[European Union]] in August, an agreement on car documents was reached.<ref>{{Cite news |date=27 August 2022 |title=Serbia-Kosovo ID document row settled, says EU |url=https://www.bbc.com/news/world-europe-62702819 |url-status=live |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20220830031211/https://www.bbc.com/news/world-europe-62702819 |archive-date=30 August 2022 |access-date=14 October 2023 |work=[[BBC News]]}}</ref> The agreement went into effect on 1 September, with the deadline for obtaining new car documents set for 31 October 2022.<ref name=":20" /> A proposed agreement to normalise tensions between the two countries, later-informally known as the [[Ohrid Agreement (2023)|Ohrid Agreement]], was sent to Serbia and Kosovo by diplomats {{Ill|Jens Plötner|de|Jens Plötner}} and [[Emmanuel Bonne]], and was leaked in September 2022.<ref>{{Cite web |date=18 September 2022 |title=Novi plan Šolca i Makrona za Kosovo i Srbiju: Realnost ili spisak želja |trans-title=The new plan of Scholz and Macron for |access-date=14 October 2023 |website=[[Vreme]] |language=sr}}</ref> Its existence was confirmed by Serbia and Kosovo a month later.<ref>{{Cite web |last1=Isufi |first1=Perparim |last2=Dragojlo |first2=Saša |date=10 October 2022 |title=Belgrade, Pristina Confirm German-French Proposal for Kosovo Deal |url=https://balkaninsight.com/2022/10/10/belgrade-pristina-confirm-german-french-proposal-for-kosovo-deal/ |url-status=live |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20221213003615/https://balkaninsight.com/2022/10/10/belgrade-pristina-confirm-german-french-proposal-for-kosovo-deal/ |archive-date=13 December 2022 |access-date=13 December 2022 |website=[[Balkan Insight]]}}</ref> Shortly before the deadline for the car documents expired, [[Albin Kurti]], the prime minister of Kosovo, announced that a phased implementation would instead be implemented up to 21 April 2023.<ref>{{Cite web |date=28 October 2022 |title=Kosovo expands timeline for Serbs to comply with car plates |url=https://apnews.com/article/nato-europe-serbia-kosovo-pristina-e3e0e8e04998fed2701d4af504202c56 |url-status=live |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20230111141029/https://apnews.com/article/nato-europe-serbia-kosovo-pristina-e3e0e8e04998fed2701d4af504202c56 |archive-date=11 January 2023 |access-date=13 December 2022 |website=[[Associated Press]]}}</ref> In protest to the announcement, hundreds of Kosovo Serb police officers, mayors, and [[Serb List (Kosovo)|Serb List]] politicians resigned from === 2023 protests ===
{{further|2023 Serbian protests}}
[[File:Srbija protiv nasilja, 19. maj 7 (cropped).jpg|thumb|alt=Demonstrators protesting in the Kneza Miloša Street on 19 May 2023|Demonstrators on 19 May 2023]]
In May 2023, the [[Belgrade school shooting]] and a [[Mladenovac and Smederevo shootings|mass murder near Mladenovac and Smederevo]] occurred.<ref>{{Cite news |date=3 May 2023 |title=Belgrade shooting: Teen made 'kill list' for Serbia school attack |url=https://www.bbc.com/news/world-europe-65468404 |url-status=live |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20230503091248/https://www.bbc.com/news/world-europe-65468404 |archive-date=3 May 2023 |access-date=17 May 2023 |work=[[BBC News]] |language=en-GB}}</ref><ref>{{Cite web |last=Dragojlo |first=Saša |date=5 May 2023 |title=Second Mass Shooting in Two Days Stuns Serbia, Killing Eight |url=https://balkaninsight.com/2023/05/05/second-mass-shooting-in-two-days-stuns-serbia-killing-eight/ |url-status=live |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231025172604/https://balkaninsight.com/2023/05/05/second-mass-shooting-in-two-days-stuns-serbia-killing-eight/ |archive-date=25 October 2023 |access-date=17 May 2023 |website=[[Balkan Insight]]}}</ref> The government responded by adopting measures such as stricter regulations on gun ownership and hiring 1,200 police officers to schools.<ref name="bbcnews1">{{Cite news |last1=Bubalo |first1=Mattea |last2=Gozzi |first2=Laura |date=5 May 2023 |title=Second mass shooting in Serbia leaves eight dead |url=https://www.bbc.com/news/world-europe-65490418 |url-status=live |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20230505033713/https://www.bbc.com/news/world-europe-65490418 |archive-date=5 May 2023 |access-date=17 May 2023 |work=[[BBC News]]}}</ref><ref>{{Cite news |date=5 May 2023 |title=Factbox: How countries have legislated after mass shootings |url=https://www.reuters.com/world/how-countries-have-legislated-after-mass-shootings-2023-05-05/ |url-status=live |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231025172555/https://www.reuters.com/world/how-countries-have-legislated-after-mass-shootings-2023-05-05/ |archive-date=25 October 2023 |access-date=17 May 2023 |work=[[Reuters]]}}</ref> The response was also criticised, particularly due to the statement of [[Branko Ružić (politician)|Branko Ružić]], the minister of education, who said that "a cancerous, pernicious influence of the Internet, video games, and so-called Western values, is evident" (''evidentan je kancerogen, poguban uticaj interneta video igrica, takozvanih zapadnih vrednosti'') in the shooting, and Brnabić, who said that the "system did not fail" (''sistem nije zakazao'') when responding to the claims that the government could have stopped the shootings.<ref>{{Cite web |date=3 May 2023 |title=Ružić: Poguban uticaj zapadnih vrednosti |trans-title=Ružić: The pernicious influence of Western values |url=https://www.nedeljnik.rs/ruzic-poguban-uticaj-zapadnih-vrednosti/ |website=[[Nedeljnik]] |language=sr}}</ref><ref>{{Cite web |date=4 May 2023 |title=Brnabić o tragediji u školi "Vladislav Ribnikar": Sistem nije zakazao |trans-title=Brnabić on the tragedy at the "Vladislav Ribnikar" school: The system did not fail |url=https://n1info.rs/vesti/brnabic-o-tragediji-u-os-vladislav-ribnikar-sistem-nije-zakazao/ |url-status=live In response to the shootings, and a day before the protests began, Ružić announced his resignation.<ref>{{Cite web |date=7 May 2023 |title=Branko Ružić podneo ostavku |trans-title=Branko Ružić resigned |url=https://n1info.rs/vesti/branko-ruzic-podneo-ostavku/ |url-status=live |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20230507163722/https://n1info.rs/vesti/branko-ruzic-podneo-ostavku/ |archive-date=7 May 2023 |access-date=25 July 2023 |website=[[N1 (TV channel)|N1]] |language=sr}}</ref> [[Đorđe Milićević]] was appointed as acting minister and was succeeded by [[Slavica Đukić Dejanović]] in late July 2023.<ref name="milicevicvd">{{Cite web |last=Pašić |first=Danijela |date=31 May 2023 |title=Đorđe Milićević umesto Ružića – imenovan vršilac dužnosti ministra prosvete |trans-title=Đorđe Milićević instead of Ružić – appointed acting minister of education |url=https://n1info.rs/vesti/djordje-milicevic-umesto-ruzica-imenovan-vrsilac-duznosti-ministra-prosvete/ |url-status=live |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20230605030435/https://n1info.rs/vesti/djordje-milicevic-umesto-ruzica-imenovan-vrsilac-duznosti-ministra-prosvete/ |archive-date=5 June 2023 |access-date=25 July 2023 |website=[[N1 (TV channel)|N1]] |language=sr}}</ref><ref name="dejanovic">{{Cite web |date=25 July 2023 |title=Slavica Đukić Dejanović i zvanično novi ministar prosvete |trans-title=Slavica Đukić Dejanović is officially the new minister of education |url=https://www.danas.rs/vesti/politika/skupstina-srbije-izglasala-slavicu-djukic-dejanovic-za-ministarku-prosvete/ |url-status=live |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20230725131628/https://www.danas.rs/vesti/politika/skupstina-srbije-izglasala-slavicu-djukic-dejanovic-za-ministarku-prosvete/ |archive-date=25 July 2023 |access-date=25 July 2023 |website=[[Danas (newspaper)|Danas]] |language=sr}}</ref> As one of the demands of the protests, organisers initiated a motion in the National Assembly to dismiss minister [[Bratislav Gašić]] in early July 2023, however, the motion was unsuccessful.<ref>{{Cite web |last=Milenković |first=Mirjana |date=5 July 2023 |title=Za nepoverenje Gašiću glasalo 37 poslanika, nije smenjen |trans-title=37 deputies voted for no confidence in Gašić, he was not dismissed |url=https://www.danas.rs/vesti/politika/skupstina-srbije-za-nepoverenje-gasicu-glasalo-37-poslanika-nije-smenjen/ |url-status=live |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20230725194140/https://www.danas.rs/vesti/politika/skupstina-srbije-za-nepoverenje-gasicu-glasalo-37-poslanika-nije-smenjen/ |archive-date=25 July 2023 |access-date=25 July 2023 |website=[[Danas (newspaper)|Danas]] |language=sr}}</ref>

== Electoral system ==
{{Politics of Serbia}}
The 250 members of the [[National Assembly (Serbia)|National Assembly]] are elected by [[closed-list]] [[proportional representation]] from a single nationwide [[constituency]].<ref name=":02">{{cite web |date=2016 |title=Electoral system of Serbia |url=http://www.ipu.org/parline-e/reports/2355_B.htm |url-status=live |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20160306025850/http://www.ipu.org/parline-e/reports/2355_B.htm |archive-date=6 March 2016 |access-date=2 June 2022 |website=[[Inter-Parliamentary Union]]}}</ref><ref name=":0">{{Cite web |title=Izbori i izborni sistem |trans-title=Elections and the electoral system |url=http://www.parlament.gov.rs/narodna-skupstina-/uloga-i-nacin-rada/izbori-i-izborni-sistem.906.html |url-status=live |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20230611193855/http://www.parlament.gov.rs/narodna-skupstina-/uloga-i-nacin-rada/izbori-i-izborni-sistem.906.html |archive-date=11 June 2023 |access-date=29 May 2023 |website=[[National Assembly of Serbia]] |language=sr}}</ref> Eligible voters vote for [[electoral list]]s, on which the candidates of the accepted lists are present. A maximum of 250 candidates could be present on a single electoral list. An electoral list could be submitted by a registered political party, a coalition of political parties, or a citizens' group (''grupa građana'').<ref name=":0" /> To submit an electoral list, at least 10,000 valid signatures must be collected, though [[Minority group|ethnic minority]] parties only need to collect 5,000 signatures to qualify on ballot.<ref name=":0" /><ref name=":5">{{Cite web |last=Milovančević |first=Vojislav |date=29 October 2021 |title=Detalji sporazuma Vučića i opozicije iz Skupštine |trans-title=Details of the agreement between Vučić and the opposition from the Assembly |url=https://nova.rs/vesti/politika/ekskluzivno-detalji-sporazuma-vucica-i-opozicije-iz-skupstine/ |url-status=live |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20211029113154/https://nova.rs/vesti/politika/ekskluzivno-detalji-sporazuma-vucica-i-opozicije-iz-skupstine/ |archive-date=29 October 2021 |access-date=2 June 2022 |website=[[NOVA portal]] |language=sr}}</ref> At least 40% of candidates on electoral lists must be female.<ref>{{cite web |date=8 February 2022 |title=Cenzus tri odsto, na listama 40 procenata žena |trans-title=Three percent threshold, 40 percent of women on the lists |url=https://www.rts.rs/page/stories/sr/story/9/politika/3844903/cenzus-tri-odsto-na-listama-40-procenata-zena.html |url-status=live |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20220128233232/https://www.rts.rs/page/stories/sr/story/9/politika/3844903/cenzus-tri-odsto-na-listama-40-procenata-zena.html |archive-date=28 January 2022 |access-date=2 June 2022 |website=[[Radio Television of Serbia]] |language=sr}}</ref> The electoral list is submitted by its chosen representative or representatives. An electoral list could be declined, after which those who had submitted an electoral list can fix the deficiencies in a span of 48 hours, or rejected, if the person is not authorised to nominate candidates. The name and date of the election, names of the electoral lists and its representatives, and information on how to vote are only present on the voting ballot.<ref name=":3">{{Cite web |date=7 February 2022 |title=Zakon o izboru narodnih poslanika |trans-title=Law on Election of People's Deputies |url=https://www.pravno-informacioni-sistem.rs/SlGlasnikPortal/eli/rep/sgrs/skupstina/zakon/2022/14/2 |url-status=live |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20230529120900/https://www.pravno-informacioni-sistem.rs/SlGlasnikPortal/eli/rep/sgrs/skupstina/zakon/2022/14/2 |archive-date=29 May 2023 |access-date=29 May 2023 |website=Pravno-informacioni sistem |language=sr}}</ref>

The [[Republic Electoral Commission (Serbia)|Republic Electoral Commission]] (RIK), local election commissions, and polling boards oversee the election.<ref name=":3" /> Seats are allocated using the [[d'Hondt method]] with an electoral threshold of 3% of all votes cast, although the threshold is waived for ethnic minority parties.<ref name=":02" /><ref>{{Cite news |date=8 February 2020 |title=Skupština Srbije: Izborni cenzus spušten na tri posto |trans-title=Assembly of Serbia: Electoral threshold lowered to three percent |url=https://balkans.aljazeera.net/news/balkan/2020/2/8/skupstina-srbije-izborni-cenzus-spusten-na-tri-posto |access-date=26 September 2024 |work=[[Al Jazeera Balkans]] |language=bs}}</ref> The seats are distributed by dividing the total number of votes received by the electoral list participating in the distribution of seats by each number from one to 250. If two or more electoral lists receive the same quotients on the basis of which the seat is distributed, the electoral list that received the greater number of votes has the priority.<ref name=":3" /> Parliamentary seats are awarded to candidates from electoral lists according to their order, starting with the first candidate from an electoral list.<ref name=":0" />

A parliamentary election is called by the president of Serbia, who also has to announce its date and dissolve the National Assembly in the process.<ref name=":0" /><ref name=":3" /> According to law, the next parliamentary election was supposed to take place by 30 April 2026.<ref name=":4">{{Cite web |title=Serbia: National Assembly |url=https://data.ipu.org/node/151/elections?chamber_id=13558 |url-status=live |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20221231175720/https://data.ipu.org/node/151/elections?chamber_id=13558 |archive-date=31 December 2022 |access-date=31 December 2022 |website=[[Inter-Parliamentary Union]]}}</ref> It is possible for a snap election to take place.<ref>{{Cite web |title=O izborima za narodne poslanike |trans-title=About elections for deputies |url=https://www.rik.parlament.gov.rs/tekst/sr/77/o-izborima-za-narodne-poslanike.php |url-status=live |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20230529120900/https://www.rik.parlament.gov.rs/tekst/sr/77/o-izborima-za-narodne-poslanike.php |archive-date=29 May 2023 |access-date=29 May 2023 |website=[[Republic Electoral Commission]] |language=sr}}</ref> To vote, a person has to be a citizen and resident of Serbia and at least 18 years old.<ref name=":4" /> For those who live abroad, they are able to vote at diplomatic missions.<ref name=":02" /> At least five days before the election, citizens are notified about the election; citizens receive information about the day and time of the election and the address of the polling station where they can vote.<ref name=":0" /> [[Election silence]] begins two days before the voting day and it lasts until the closure of all polling stations.<ref name=":30">{{Cite web |date=1 November 2023 |title=Počinje izborna trka, predaja lista najkasnije 20 dana pre izbora |trans-title=The election race begins, the list is submitted no later than 20 days before the election |url=https://www.rtv.rs/sr_lat/politika/pocinje-izborna-trka-predaja-lista-najkasnije-20-dana-pre-izbora_1489448.html |url-status=live |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231101114020/https://www.rtv.rs/sr_lat/politika/pocinje-izborna-trka-predaja-lista-najkasnije-20-dana-pre-izbora_1489448.html |archive-date=1 November 2023 |access-date=1 November 2023 |website=[[Radio Television of Vojvodina]] |language=sr}}</ref> During the election day, eligible voters could vote from 07:00 ([[UTC+01:00]]) to 20:00, though if the polling station is opened later than 07:00, voting is then extended by the amount of time for which the opening of the polling station was delayed.<ref name=":3" /><ref name=":33">{{Cite web |date=4 November 2023 |title=RIK odredio rokove za izborne radnje: Rok za podnošenje lista 26. novembar, izborna tišina počinje 14. decembra |trans-title=The RIK has set deadlines for election activities: The deadline for submitting lists is 26 November, the election silence begins on 14 December |url=https://nova.rs/vesti/politika/rik-odredio-rokove-za-izborne-radnje-rok-za-podnosenje-lista-26-novembar-izborna-tisina-pocinje-14-decembra/ |url-status=live |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231106141419/https://nova.rs/vesti/politika/rik-odredio-rokove-za-izborne-radnje-rok-za-podnosenje-lista-26-novembar-izborna-tisina-pocinje-14-decembra/ |archive-date=6 November 2023 |access-date=6 November 2023 |website=[[NOVA portal]] |language=sr}}</ref> Voters who are not able to vote at polling stations due to being sick, old, or invalid have to inform their election commission before 11:00 so that they could vote on the election day from their home after 11:00.<ref name=":33" />

=== Election date ===
In April 2023, newspaper ''[[Danas (newspaper)|Danas]]'' reported that the parliamentary elections, [[2023 Serbian local elections|local elections]], the [[2023 Vojvodina provincial election|Vojvodina provincial elections]], and the [[2023 Belgrade City Assembly election|Belgrade City Assembly elections]] could be held as early as in November 2023.<ref>{{Cite web |date=10 April 2023 |title=Vučić raspisuje izbore za novembar? |trans-title=Vučić to call elections for November? |url=https://www.danas.rs/vesti/politika/vucic-raspisuje-izbore-za-novembar/ |url-status=live (newspaper)|Danas]] |language=sr}}</ref> Shortly after the beginning of the 2023 protests, Vučić hinted that snap elections could take place before September 2023.<ref>{{Cite web |date=14 May 2023 Newspaper ''[[Nova (Serbia)|Nova]]'' and news portal ''[[N1 (TV channel)|N1]]'' reported in September 2023 that the government considered 19 December 2023 as the date for local, provincial, and parliamentary elections.<ref>{{Cite web |last=Savić |first=Danilo |date=4 September 2023 |title=Vučić rekao partnerima da se spremaju za izbore posle Nikoljdana, na beogradske za sada ne sme 2023 |website=[[N1 (TV channel)|N1]] |language=sr}}</ref> For the election to take place on 17 December, the government of Serbia had to formally propose to dissolve the National Assembly between 18 October and 2 November. The president of Serbia then had 72 hours to decide whether to dissolve the National Assembly or not.<ref name=":26">{{Cite web |date=16 October 2023 |title=Šta i kad mora da se uradi da bi se izbori October 2023 |website=[[Vreme]] |language=sr}}</ref> The government of Serbia sent Vučić the proposal to dissolve the National Assembly and organise local elections in 65 cities and municipalities on 30 October.<ref>{{Cite web |date=30 October 2023 |title=Vlada uputila predlog Vučiću za raspuštanje Skupštine i raspisivanje izbora |trans-title=The government submitted a proposal to Vučić for the |access-date=30 October 2023 |website=[[N1 (TV channel)|N1]] |language=sr}}</ref> On 1 November, Vučić dissolved the National Assembly and called the elections for 17 December.<ref>{{Cite web |date=1 November 2023 |title=Vučić raspisao vanredne parlamentarne izbore za 17. decembar |trans-title=Vučić announced snap parliamentary elections for 17 December |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231101090933/https://n1info.rs/vesti/vucic-raspisao-vanredne-parlamentarne-izbore-za-17-decembar/ |archive-date=1 November 2023 |access-date=1 November 2023 |website=[[N1 (TV channel)|N1]] |language=sr}}</ref> The official campaign period lasted 46 days.<ref>{{Cite web |date=1 November 2023 |title=Počinje izborna trka, predaja lista najkasnije 20 dana pre 2023 |access-date=1 November 2023 |website=[[Tačno d.o.o.|Tanjug]] |language=sr}}</ref> Ognjen Radonjić, a professor at the [[Faculty of Philosophy, University of Belgrade|Faculty of Philosophy]], and Dragan Popović, the director of the Centre for Practical Politics, argued that the Banjska attack was one of the main reasons why Vučić announced early elections.<ref>{{Cite news |last=Karabeg |first=Omer |date=15 October 2023 |title=Može li Vučić da izgubi Beograd na decembarskim izborima? |trans-title=Can Vučić lose Belgrade in the December elections? |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231022223944/https://www.slobodnaevropa.org/a/most-izbori-srbija-vucic-beograd/32637426.html |archive-date=22 October 2023 |access-date=22 October 2023 |work=[[Radio Free Europe]] |language=sr}}</ref> The [[Assembly of Vojvodina]] also dissolved itself on 16 November, also setting the provincial election date for 17 December.<ref>{{Cite web |date=16 November 2023 |title=Počela sednica Skupštine Vojvodine: Prvo raspuštanje, pa izbori |trans-title=The session of the Assembly of Vojvodina has begun: First the dissolution, then the elections |url=https://www.021.rs/story/Novi-Sad/Vesti/358597/Pocela-sednica-Skupstine-Vojvodine-Prvo-raspustanje-pa-izbori.html |access-date=16 November 2023 |website=021.rs |language=sr |archive-date=16 November 2023 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231116102814/https://www.021.rs/story/Novi-Sad/Vesti/358597/Pocela-sednica-Skupstine-Vojvodine-Prvo-raspustanje-pa-izbori.html |url-status=live }}</ref>

The 2023 parliamentary election was the first parliamentary election to be held in the [[winter]] season since the [[2007 Serbian parliamentary election|2007 parliamentary election]], which was held on 21 January.<ref>{{Cite web |date=2 June 2016 |title=Spisak izbora i referenduma |trans-title=List of elections and referendums |url=https://www.vreme.com/projekat/spisak-izbora-i-referenduma/ |url-status=live |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20230812155947/https://www.vreme.com/projekat/spisak-izbora-i-referenduma/ |archive-date=12 August 2023 |access-date=21 October 2023 |website=[[Vreme]] |language=sr}}</ref> Dejan Bursać, a teaching associate at the [[Institute for Political Studies in Belgrade|Institute for Political Studies]], argued that ruling parties "avoid the winter for voting because the voters are more dissatisfied, the turnout cannot be easily controlled because of the weather, and the costs to the people are increased" (''izbegavaju zimu za glasanje jer su glasači nezadovoljniji, a ne može se ni izlaznot lako kontrolisati zbog vremena i uz to su povećani troškovi ljudima'').<ref name=":06">{{Cite web |last=Valtner |first=Lidija |date=17 October 2023 |title=Ko će se bolje snaći u prvoj zimskoj kampanji, vlast ili opozicija? |trans-title=Who will do better in the first winter campaign, the government or the opposition? |url=https://www.danas.rs/vesti/politika/ko-ce-se-bolje-snaci-u-prvoj-zimskoj-kampanji-vlast-ili-opozicija/ |url-status=live |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231018033120/https://www.danas.rs/vesti/politika/ko-ce-se-bolje-snaci-u-prvoj-zimskoj-kampanji-vlast-ili-opozicija/ |archive-date=18 October 2023 |access-date=21 October 2023 |website=[[Danas (newspaper)|Danas]] |language=sr}}</ref> Ivana Petronijević Terzić, a Demostat journalist, has also listed increased inflation, higher bills due to heating, and worse weather conditions as one of the reasons, but also said that these reasons would be a problem in a democratic society.<ref name=":06"/> In preparations for the elections, RIK began acquiring election equipment, including ballot boxes, [[UV lamps]], and finger sprays, on 13 October.<ref>{{Cite web |last=Latković |first=Nataša |date=17 October 2023 |title=Počele pripreme za izbore: RIK nabavlja glasačke kutije, UV lampe, sprejeve, ali bez tendera |trans-title=Preparations for the elections have begun: RIK is obtaining ballot boxes, UV lamps, sprays, but without a tender |url=https://nova.rs/vesti/politika/pocele-pripreme-za-izbore-rik-nabavlja-glasacke-kutije-uv-lampe-sprejeve-ali-bez-tendera/ |url-status=live |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231101092425/https://nova.rs/vesti/politika/pocele-pripreme-za-izbore-rik-nabavlja-glasacke-kutije-uv-lampe-sprejeve-ali-bez-tendera/ |archive-date=1 November 2023 |access-date=22 October 2023 |website=[[NOVA portal]] |language=sr}}</ref>

=== Election conditions ===
A group of opposition parties, led by the [[Forward to Europe]] (PE) and [[Green–Left Front]] (ZLF) parliamentary groups, sent a joint letter to [[Organization for Security and Co-operation in Europe]] (OSCE) and other election observers in Serbia in September 2023, with the request to declare the status of election conditions for the upcoming elections. PE and ZLF alleged that the conditions had worsened since the 2022 parliamentary election and said that the organisations should contemplate about rating the elections as not free and undemocratic if the [[Office for Democratic Institutions and Human Rights]] (ODIHR) advices were not implemented.<ref name=":28">{{Cite web |date=8 October 2023 |title=Izborni uslovi se pogoršali: Pet opozicionih stranaka uputilo pismo međunarodnim posmatračima izbora |trans-title="Election conditions have worsened": Five opposition parties sent a letter to international election observers |url=https://n1info.rs/vesti/izborni-uslovi-se-pogorsali-pet-opozicionih-stranaka-uputilo-pismo-medjunarodnim-posmatracima-izbora/ |url-status=live |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231029045049/https://n1info.rs/vesti/izborni-uslovi-se-pogorsali-pet-opozicionih-stranaka-uputilo-pismo-medjunarodnim-posmatracima-izbora/ |archive-date=29 October 2023 |access-date=23 October 2023 |website=[[N1 (TV channel)|N1]] |language=sr}}</ref> In an ''Insajder'' interview, political scientist {{Ill|Cvijetin Milivojević|sr|Cvijetin Milivojević}} also claimed that the conditions were worse in comparison with the previous election, but added that due to the short campaign timespan it would be impractical to resolve election conditions.<ref>{{Cite web |date=2023-09-29 |title=Milivojević u Markeru: Izborni uslovi za opoziciju sada možda i gori nego pre |trans-title=Milivojević in Marker: Election conditions for the opposition may be worse now than before |url=https://insajder.net/teme/milivojevic-u-markeru-izborni-uslovi-za-opoziciju-sada-mozda-i-gori-nego-pre-video |url-status=live |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231029045050/https://insajder.net/teme/milivojevic-u-markeru-izborni-uslovi-za-opoziciju-sada-mozda-i-gori-nego-pre-video |archive-date=29 October 2023 |access-date=2023-10-23 |website=[[Insajder]] |language=sr}}</ref> Bursać and Jovana Đurbabić from non-governmental and monitoring organisation {{Ill|CRTA (organisation)|lt=CRTA|sr|Crta (organizacija)}} listed "unequal access to the media, campaign of party officials, and control of the elections at the polling stations" (''nejednak pristup medijima, funkcionerska kampanja i kontrola samih izbora na biračkom mestu'') as the three main problems of the election conditions in Serbia.<ref>{{Cite web |last=Miljuš |first=Stefan |date=19 September 2023 |title=Ključni izazovi predstojećih izbora u Srbiji: Mediji, funkcionerska kampanja i kontrola birališta |trans-title=Key challenges of the upcoming elections in Serbia: Media, campaign of party officials, and polling station control |url=https://www.glasamerike.net/a/srbija-izbori-problemi-mediji-kampanja-sns-opozicija/7274783.html |url-status=live |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231029045050/https://www.glasamerike.net/a/srbija-izbori-problemi-mediji-kampanja-sns-opozicija/7274783.html |archive-date=29 October 2023 |access-date=23 October 2023 |website=[[Voice of America]] |language=sr}}</ref>

After PE and ZLF, Brnabić also called OSCE and ODIHR in October 2023 to monitor the elections, while accusing opposition parties of wanting foreign interference in the elections and trying to form an insight that elections in Serbia are not free and undemocratic.<ref>{{Cite news |date=9 October 2023 |title=Premijerka Srbije pozvala OEBS na izbore |trans-title=The Prime Minister of Serbia invites OSCE to the elections |url=https://www.slobodnaevropa.org/a/izvori-srbija-oebs-brnabic-pismo/32629805.html |url-status=live |work=[[Radio Free Europe]] |language=sr}}</ref><ref>{{Cite web |date=10 October 2023 |title=Ana Brnabić: Opozicija instrumentalizuje OEBS |trans-title=Ana Brnabić: The opposition is instrumentalising the OSCE |url=https://www.vreme.com/vesti/izborni-uslovi-po-premijerki-kad-vlast-zove-oebs-to-je-ozbiljno-kad-opozicija-onda-nije/ |url-status=live |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231029050554/https://www.vreme.com/vesti/izborni-uslovi-po-premijerki-kad-vlast-zove-oebs-to-je-ozbiljno-kad-opozicija-onda-nije/ |archive-date=29 October The Committee for Culture and Information of the National Assembly amended the ban on campaign of party officials, extending it to 30 days, as part of the proposed changes to the Law on Public Information and Media which the National Assembly adopted on 26 October.<ref>{{Cite web |date=25 October 2023 |title=Zabrana funkcionerske kampanje se produžava na mesec dana |trans-title=The campaign === Political parties ===
{{see also|List of political parties in Serbia}}

The table below lists political parties and coalitions elected to the National Assembly after the 2022 parliamentary election. Out of 19 electoral lists, only 7 crossed the 3% threshold while 5 minority electoral lists crossed the waived electoral threshold.<ref name=":22">{{cite book |last1=Kovačević |first1=Miladin postponed until 5 July, due to the repeated voting in [[Veliki Trnovac]], where a seat in the National Assembly was battled between SPS and the [[Albanian Coalition of Preševo Valley]] (KSLP), led by the [[Party for Democratic Action]].<ref>{{Cite web |date=5 July 2022 |title=RIK objavio konačne rezultate parlamentarnih izbora |trans-title=RIK publishes final results of the parliamentary elections === Pre-election composition ===
The [[13th National Assembly of Serbia|thirteenth convocation of the National Assembly]] held its first session on 1 August 2022, at which the 13th parliamentary composition was formalised.<ref>{{Cite news |date=1 August 2022 |title=Srbija dobila novi saziv parlamenta |trans-title=Serbia receives a new convocation of the parliament |url=https://www.slobodnaevropa.org/a/srbija-skupstina-konstituirajuca-sjednica/31968953.html |url-status=live |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231002153716/https://www.slobodnaevropa.org/a/srbija-skupstina-konstituirajuca-sjednica/31968953.html |archive-date=2 October 2023 |access-date=4 June 2023 |work=[[Radio Free Europe]] |language=sr}}</ref><ref name=":7">{{Cite web |last=Janković |first=Marija |date=1 August 2022 |title=Ko je ko u Skupštini Srbije |trans-title=Who is who in the Serbian Parliament |url=https://www.bbc.com/serbian/lat/srbija-62377118 |url-status=live |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20220812001534/https://www.bbc.com/serbian/lat/srbija-62377118 |archive-date=12 August 2022 |access-date=4 June 2023 |website=[[BBC News]] |language=sr}}</ref> [[Vladimir Orlić]] of SNS was elected [[President of the National Assembly of Serbia|president of the National Assembly]] on 2 August, while [[Sandra Božić]] (SNS), [[Snežana Paunović]] (SPS), [[Elvira Kovács]] ([[Alliance of Vojvodina Hungarians]], VMSZ), [[Usame Zukorlić]] ([[Justice and Reconciliation Party]], SPP), [[Božidar Delić]] ([[National Democratic Alternative (Serbia)|National Democratic Alternative]], NADA), [[Borko Stefanović]] (SPP), and [[Zoran Lutovac]] (DS) were elected vice-presidents.<ref>{{Cite news |date=3 August 2022 |title=Vladimir Orlić izabran za predsednika Narodne skupštine Srbije |trans-title=Vladimir Orlić has been elected as the president of the National Assembly of Serbia |url=https://www.slobodnaevropa.org/a/vladimir-orlic-izabran-za-predsednika-skup%C5%A1tine-srbije/31971011.html |url-status=live |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231016094748/https://www.slobodnaevropa.org/a/vladimir-orlic-izabran-za-predsednika-skup%C5%A1tine-srbije/31971011.html |archive-date=16 October 2023 |access-date=14 October 2023 |work=[[Radio Free Europe]] |language=sr}}</ref> Delić died shortly after taking office and was replaced by [[Vojislav Mihailović]] in November 2022.<ref>{{Cite web |last=Radovanović |first=Vojin |date=23 August 2022 |title=Preminuo Božidar Delić, potpredsednik Skupštine i bivši komandat 549. motorizovane brigade |trans-title=Božidar Delić, vice president of the Assembly and former commander of the 549th Motorized Brigade, passed away |url=https://www.danas.rs/vesti/politika/umro-bozidar-delic-potpredsednik-skupstine-i-bivsi-komandat-549-motorizovane-brigade/ |url-status=live |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231016094749/https://www.danas.rs/vesti/politika/umro-bozidar-delic-potpredsednik-skupstine-i-bivsi-komandat-549-motorizovane-brigade/ |archive-date=16 October 2023 |access-date=14 October 2023 |website=[[Danas (newspaper)|Danas]] |language=sr}}</ref><ref>{{Cite web |date=10 November 2022 |title=Vojislav Mihailović izabran za potpredsednika Narodne skupštine |trans-title=Vojislav Mihailović has been elected vice-president of the National Assembly |url=https://www.rts.rs/lat/vesti/politika/5015684/vojislav-mihailovic-izabran-za-potpredsednika-narodne-skupstine.html |url-status=live |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231016094749/https://www.rts.rs/lat/vesti/politika/5015684/vojislav-mihailovic-izabran-za-potpredsednika-narodne-skupstine.html |archive-date=16 October 2023 |access-date=14 October 2023 |website=[[Radio Television of Serbia]] |language=sr}}</ref> The composition of the National Assembly changed since the first session in August 2022; for example, the [[European Regions (Serbia)|European Regions]], a parliamentary group composed of minority interest parties, briefly existed until October 2022.<ref>{{Cite web |date=1 August 2022 |title=Ko je ko u Skupštini Srbije |trans-title=Who is who in the Parliament |url=https://www.bbc.com/serbian/lat/srbija-62377118 |url-status=live |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20220812001534/https://www.bbc.com/serbian/lat/srbija-62377118 |archive-date=12 August 2022 |access-date=14 October 2023 |website=[[BBC News]] |language=sr}}</ref><ref>{{Cite web |title=Evropski regioni – Vojvodina, Sandžak, Preševska dolina |trans-title=European Regions – Vojvodina, Sandžak, Preševo Valley |url=https://otvoreniparlament.rs/poslanicki-klub/410 |access-date=14 October 2023 |website=Otvoreni Parlament |language=sr |archive-date=16 October 2023 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231016094751/https://otvoreniparlament.rs/poslanicki-klub/410 |url-status=live }}</ref> The last session of the thirteenth convocation was held from 23 to 26 October.<ref>{{Cite web |date=23 October 2023 |title=Počela prva i najverovatnije poslednja sednica ovog saziva Skupštine Srbije: Na dnevnom redu 60 tačaka |trans-title=The first and probably the last session of this convocation of the Serbian Parliament has begun: 60 items on the agenda |url=https://www.danas.rs/vesti/politika/pocela-prva-i-najverovatnije-poslednja-sednica-ovog-saziva-skupstine-srbije-na-dnevnom-redu-60-tacaka/ |url-status=live |archive-date=24 October 2023 |access-date=26 October 2023 |website=[[Danas (newspaper)|Danas]] |language=sr}}</ref><ref>{{Cite web |date=26 October 2023 |title=Završena sednica Skupštine Srbije, == Pre-election activities ==
=== Government parties ===
Vučić hinted at a potential formation of a bloc or a movement in September 2022, which he later revealed in March 2023 to be the [[People's Movement for the State]] (NPZD).<ref name=":14">{{Cite web |last=Vlaović |first=G. |date=12 September 2022 |title=Vučić gasi Srpsku naprednu stranku i formira "Moju Srbiju"? |trans-title=Vučić to shut down the Serbian Progressive Party and form "My Serbia"? |url=https://www.danas.rs/vesti/politika/vucic-gasi-srpsku-naprednu-stranku-i-formira-moju-srbiju/ |url-status=live |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20221205020215/https://www.danas.rs/vesti/politika/vucic-gasi-srpsku-naprednu-stranku-i-formira-moju-srbiju/ |archive-date=5 December 2022 |access-date=2 June 2023 |website=[[Danas (newspaper)|Danas]] |language=sr}}</ref><ref>{{Cite web |date=8 March 2023 |title=Novosti: Vučić formira Narodni pokret za državu i kreće u obilazak Srbije |trans-title=Novosti: Vučić to form the People's Movement for the State and to embark on a tour of Serbia |url=https://n1info.rs/vesti/novosti-vucic-zapocinje-formiranje-narodnog-pokreta-za-drzavu/ |url-status=live |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20230309131506/https://n1info.rs/vesti/novosti-vucic-zapocinje-formiranje-narodnog-pokreta-za-drzavu/ |archive-date=9 March 2023 |access-date=11 March 2023 |website=[[N1 (TV channel)|N1]] |language=sr}}</ref> He said that NPZD would act as a "supra-party movement" (''nadstranački pokret'') and that SNS would not be dissolved.<ref>{{Cite web |last=Stojković |first=Anđelija |date=9 March 2023 |title=Niko neće ukinuti SNS |trans-title=No one will abolish SNS |url=http://fonet.rs/politika/36276320/niko-nece-ukinuti-sns.html |access-date=2 June 2023 |website=FoNet portal |language=sr}}</ref> Vučević confirmed that SNS would take part in the movement.<ref name=":10">{{Cite web |date=20 April 2023 |title=Vučić najavio povlačenje sa čela SNS-a 27. maja, formiranje Narodnog pokreta za Srbiju na Vidovdan |trans-title=Vučić announces his resignation from the leadership of SNS on 27 May, the formation of the People's Movement for Serbia on Vidovdan |url=https://www.danas.rs/vesti/politika/vucic-najavio-povlacenje-sa-cela-sns-a-27-maja-formiranje-narodnog-pokreta-za-srbiju-na-vidovdan/ |url-status=live |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20230601214021/http://www.danas.rs/vesti/politika/vucic-najavio-povlacenje-sa-cela-sns-a-27-maja-formiranje-narodnog-pokreta-za-srbiju-na-vidovdan/ |archive-date=1 June 2023 |access-date=2 June 2023 |website=[[Danas (newspaper)|Danas]] |language=sr}}</ref> Initially announced to be formalised in May 2023, the date was subsequently moved towards autumn 2023.<ref name=":102">{{Cite web |date=20 April 2023 |title=Vučić najavio povlačenje sa čela SNS-a 27. maja, formiranje Narodnog pokreta za Srbiju na Vidovdan |trans-title=Vučić announced his resignation from the leadership of SNS on 27 May, the formation of the People's Movement for Serbia on Vidovdan |url=https://www.danas.rs/vesti/politika/vucic-najavio-povlacenje-sa-cela-sns-a-27-maja-formiranje-narodnog-pokreta-za-srbiju-na-vidovdan/ |url-status=live |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20230420210504/https://www.danas.rs/vesti/politika/vucic-najavio-povlacenje-sa-cela-sns-a-27-maja-formiranje-narodnog-pokreta-za-srbiju-na-vidovdan/ |archive-date=20 April 2023 |access-date=21 April 2023 |website=[[Danas (newspaper)|Danas]] |language=sr}}</ref><ref>{{Cite web |date=11 August 2023 |title=Vučević: Ne kasnimo sa novim pokretom za državu, videćete kako ćemo ga formirati |trans-title=Vučević: We are not late with the new movement for the state, you will see how we will form it |url=https://www.021.rs/story/Info/Srbija/349502/Vucevic-Ne-kasnimo-sa-novim-pokretom-za-drzavu-videcete-kako-cemo-ga-formirati.html |access-date=12 August 2023 |website=021.rs |language=sr |archive-date=12 August 2023 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20230812011005/https://www.021.rs/story/Info/Srbija/349502/Vucevic-Ne-kasnimo-sa-novim-pokretom-za-drzavu-videcete-kako-cemo-ga-formirati.html |url-status=live }}</ref> Political commentators pointed out that SPS was divided on the issue of joining NPZD and that as a result, the formalisation of NPZD was delayed.<ref name=":18">{{Cite web |last=Kojić |first=Nikola |date=1 October 2023 |title=Zašto ni Vučić više ne pominje Narodni pokret za državu |trans-title=Why even Vučić no longer mentions the People's Movement for the State |url=https://n1info.rs/vesti/vucic-narodni-pokret-za-drzavu/ |url-status=live |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231006131009/https://n1info.rs/vesti/vucic-narodni-pokret-za-drzavu/ |archive-date=6 October 2023 |access-date=8 October 2023 |website=[[N1 (TV channel)|N1]] |language=sr}}</ref> [[Predrag J. Marković]], one of the vice-presidents of SPS, said that the identity of SPS would cease to exist if it had joined the movement.<ref>{{Cite web |date=8 June 2023 |title=Predrag Marković protiv utapanja SPS u Vučićev Narodni pokret za državu |trans-title=Predrag Marković against submerging the SPS in Vučić's People's Movement for the State |access-date=26 June 2023 |website=[[NOVA portal]] |language=sr}}</ref> Considering that NPZD was not mentioned at the main board session of SNS in October 2023, analyst [[Đorđe Vukadinović]] of === Opposition parties ===
After the dissolution of the UZPS coalition, SSP, [[Movement of Free Citizens (Serbia)|Movement of Free Citizens]], [[Movement for Reversal]], and [[United Trade Unions of Serbia "Sloga"|United Trade Unions of Serbia Sloga]], formed the Ujedinjeni parliamentary group in the National Assembly in August 2022.<ref name=":1" /><ref>{{Cite web |date=24 May 2022 |title=SSP, PSG, Pokret za preokret i May 2022 |access-date=2 June 2022 |website=[[Danas (newspaper)|Danas]] |language=sr}}</ref> Ujedinjeni changed its name to Forward to Europe in July 2023.<ref>{{Cite web |last=Đurić |first=Vanja |date=19 July 2023 |title=Poslanička grupa "Ujedinjeni" menja naziv |trans-title=Parliamentary group "United" is changing its name |url=https://n1info.rs/vesti/poslanicka-grupa-ujedinjeni-menja-naziv/ |website=[[N1 (TV channel)|N1]] |language=sr}}</ref> [[Zdravko Ponoš]], the presidential candidate of the UZPS coalition, left Narodna after the 2022 elections.<ref>{{Cite web |date=5 April 2022 |title=Zdravko Ponoš napustio Narodnu stranku |trans-title=Zdravko Ponoš left the People's Party |url=https://www.politika.rs/sr/clanak/504075/Zdravko-Ponos-napustio-Narodnu-stranku |url-status=live ==== Election alliances ====
[[File:Dogovor za pobedu (cropped).jpg|thumb|upright=1.3|alt=Borislav Novaković, Biljana Đorđević, Đorđe Pavićević, Robert Kozma, Zoran Lutovac, Dragan Rakić, Marinika Tepić, Radomir Lazović, Nebojša Zelenović, Pavle Grbović, Srđan Milivojević, Miroslav Aleksić, Đorđe Miketić, Borko Stefanović, Željko Veselinović, and Janko Veselinović at a press conference inside the National Assembly of Serbia in September 2023|Opposition parties organising the Serbia Against Violence protests (representatives pictured) formed a joint coalition in October 2023]]
In an interview for newspaper ''Nova'' in August 2023, [[Marinika Tepić]], one of the vice-presidents of SSP, stated that the creation of an electoral alliance of political parties that organise the Serbia Against Violence protests is possible. "During this one year of work in the National Assembly, and especially in these last three months during the protests, we, [opposition parties], managed to build trust stronger than ever before" (''Tokom ovih godinu dana rada u Narodnoj skupštini, a naročito u poslednja tri meseca tokom protesta, uspeli da izgradimo poverenje snažno kao nikad do sad''), Tepić said.<ref name=":15">{{Cite web |last=Savić |first=Danilo |date=18 August 2023 |title=Intervju Marinika Tepić: Uskoro predstavljamo novi plan protesta, verujem u zajedničku izbornu listu organizatora "Srbija protiv nasilja" |trans-title=Interview Marinika Tepić: We will soon present a new protest plan, I believe in the joint electoral list of the "Serbia Against Violence" organisers |url=https://nova.rs/vesti/politika/intervju-marinika-tepic-uskoro-predstavljamo-novi-plan-protesta-verujem-u-zajednicku-izbornu-listu-organizatora-srbija-protiv-nasilja/ |url-status=live |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20230821114939/https://nova.rs/vesti/politika/intervju-marinika-tepic-uskoro-predstavljamo-novi-plan-protesta-verujem-u-zajednicku-izbornu-listu-organizatora-srbija-protiv-nasilja/ |archive-date=21 August 2023 |access-date=21 August 2023 |website=[[NOVA portal]] |language=sr}}</ref> It was noted that DS, SRCE, Together, and ZLF opposition parties intensively cooperated with each other, as early as April 2023.<ref name=":16">{{Cite web |last=Radovanović |first=Vojin |date=18 August 2023 |title=Crnogorski scenario ili jedna kolona: Kako će opozicija izaći na naredne izbore? |trans-title=The Montenegrin scenario or one column: How will the opposition come out in the next elections? |url=https://www.danas.rs/vesti/politika/crnogorski-scenario-ili-jedna-kolona-kako-ce-opozicija-izaci-na-naredne-izbore/ |url-status=live |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20230821114938/https://www.danas.rs/vesti/politika/crnogorski-scenario-ili-jedna-kolona-kako-ce-opozicija-izaci-na-naredne-izbore/ |archive-date=21 August 2023 |access-date=21 August 2023 |website=[[Danas (newspaper)|Danas]] |language=sr}}</ref><ref>{{Cite web |last=Živić |first=Miona |date=1 April 2023 |title=Tribina u kafani: "Koliko se vidi Leskovac iz Beograda? |access-date=21 August 2023 |website=[[Danas (newspaper)|Danas]] |language=sr}}</ref> Lazović has, however, opposed the creation of a single coalition of all opposition parties, stating that it could == Electoral lists ==
With the dissolution of the National Assembly and a call for elections to be held on 17 December, the deadline to submit electoral lists was set for 26 November.<ref>{{Cite web |date=2 November 2023 |title=Dimitrijević (RIK): Od danas prijem izbornih lista, podnose se do 26. novembra |trans-title=Dimitrijević (RIK): From today electoral lists will be accepted, they must be submitted by 26 November |url=https://beta.rs/content/193443-dimitrijevic-rik-od-danas-prijem-izbornih-lista-podnose-se-do-26-novembra |url-status=live |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231102092206/https://beta.rs/content/193443-dimitrijevic-rik-od-danas-prijem-izbornih-lista-podnose-se-do-26-novembra |archive-date=2 November 2023 |access-date=2 November 2023 |website=[[Novinska agencija Beta]] |language=sr}}</ref> The collective electoral list was published by RIK on 1 December, with 2,818 candidates listed in total.<ref>{{Cite web |date=1 December 2023 |title=Utvrđena zbirna izborna lista za parlamentarne izbore |trans-title=The collective electoral list for the parliamentary elections was published |url=https://n1info.rs/vesti/izbori-2023/utvrdjena-zbirna-izborna-lista-za-parlamentarne-izbore/ |url-status=live |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231202010520/https://n1info.rs/vesti/izbori-2023/utvrdjena-zbirna-izborna-lista-za-parlamentarne-izbore/ |archive-date=2 December 2023 |access-date=1 December 2023 |website=[[N1 (TV channel)|N1]] |language=sr}}</ref> The following table includes electoral lists that were confirmed by RIK and that took part in the 2023 parliamentary election.<ref>{{Cite news |date=14 November 2023 |title=Ko je sve na listama za poslanike republičke skupštine |trans-title=Who is on the lists for representatives of the republican assembly |url=https://www.bbc.com/serbian/lat/svet-67379555 |url-status=live |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231126112158/https://www.bbc.com/serbian/lat/svet-67379555 |archive-date=26 November 2023 |access-date=26 November 2023 |work=[[BBC News]] |language=sr}}</ref> The electoral lists of PEP, which submitted its electoral list under two Bunjevci minority parties, and [[Pavle Bihali]] of [[Leviathan Movement|Levijatan]]-led Russian Minority Alliance were rejected by RIK due to not having enough valid signatures.<ref>{{Cite web |date=28 November 2023 |title=Odbijena lista Pavla Bihalija: Nije ni upisan u birački spisak |trans-title=The list of Pavle Bihali has been rejected: He is not even on the voter's list |access-date=28 November 2023 |website=[[N1 (TV channel)|N1]] |language=sr}}</ref><ref name="RIK_ALBANCI2">{{Cite web |date=28 November 2023 |title=RIK odbila da proglasi listu "Dosta! == Campaign ==
Croatian daily newspaper ''[[Večernji list]]'' described the 2023 election as "the most uncertain election since 2012".<ref>{{Cite web |last=Zovko |first=Hrvoje |date=21 November 2023 |title=Vučićeva kritična, 12. godina vlasti: Srbija za mjesec dana izlazi na izvanredne izbore |url=https://www.vecernji.hr/vijesti/vuciceva-kriticna-12-godina-vlasti-srbija-za-mjesec-dana-izlazi-na-izvanredne-izbore-1725535 |url-access=subscription |url-status=live |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231121214608/https://www.vecernji.hr/vijesti/vuciceva-kriticna-12-godina-vlasti-srbija-za-mjesec-dana-izlazi-na-izvanredne-izbore-1725535 |archive-date=21 November 2023 |access-date=21 November 2023 |website=[[Večernji list]] |language=hr}}</ref> Political scientist and journalist Aleksandar Ivković argued that the campaign was unprincipled, listing graffitis, posters, music videos, and tabloid media content that were perpetrated against opposition parties.<ref name=":42">{{Cite web |last=Savić |first=Danilo |date=27 October 2023 |title=Čeka nas najprljavija kampanja ikad: Neće biti pošteđeni ni opozicija, ni aktivisti, ni njihove porodice |trans-title=The dirtiest campaign ever awaits us: Neither the opposition, nor the activists, nor their families will be spared |url=https://nova.rs/vesti/politika/ceka-nas-najprljavija-kampanja-ikad-nece-biti-postedjeni-ni-opozicija-ni-aktivisti-ni-njihove-porodice/ |url-status=live |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231029150116/https://nova.rs/vesti/politika/ceka-nas-najprljavija-kampanja-ikad-nece-biti-postedjeni-ni-opozicija-ni-aktivisti-ni-njihove-porodice/ |archive-date=29 October 2023 |access-date=29 October 2023 |website=[[NOVA portal]] |language=sr}}</ref> Political scientist Boban Stojanović estimated that the political friction did not decrease and that "political violence will be seen until the end of the election campaign" (''političko nasilje biće prisutno do kraja kampanje'').<ref>{{Cite web |date=13 November 2023 |title=Stojanović za Insajder: Tenzije se ne smanjuju, političko nasilje biće prisutno do kraja kampanje |trans-title=Stojanović for Insider: Tensions are not decreasing, political violence will be present until the end of the campaign |url=https://www.danas.rs/vesti/politika/izbori-2023/stojanovic-za-insajder-tenzije-se-ne-smanjuju-politicko-nasilje-bice-prisutno-do-kraja-kampanje/ |url-status=live |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231114215036/https://www.danas.rs/vesti/politika/izbori-2023/stojanovic-za-insajder-tenzije-se-ne-smanjuju-politicko-nasilje-bice-prisutno-do-kraja-kampanje/ |archive-date=14 November 2023 |access-date=15 November 2023 |website=[[Danas (newspaper)|Danas]] |language=sr}}</ref> Stojanović said that the election was more uncertain than the 2022 election.<ref>{{Cite web |date=25 November 2023 |title=Stojanović: Predstojeći izbori neizvesniji nego prethodni, posebno kada je reč o Beogradu |trans-title=Stojanović: The upcoming elections are more uncertain than the previous ones, especially when it comes to Belgrade |url=https://www.danas.rs/vesti/politika/izbori-2023/boban-stojanovic-izbori/ |url-status=live |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231125154852/https://www.danas.rs/vesti/politika/izbori-2023/boban-stojanovic-izbori/ |archive-date=25 November 2023 |access-date=25 November 2023 |website=[[Danas (newspaper)|Danas]] |language=sr}}</ref>

During their visit in Serbia, PACE representatives concluded that the campaign was met with [[Political polarization|polarisation]] and intimidation from the government.<ref>{{Cite web |date=27 November 2023 |title=Savet Evrope: U Srbiji veoma polarizovana kampanja sa nezabeleženim nivoom zastrašivanja |trans-title=Council of Europe: In Serbia, a very polarised campaign with an unprecedented level of intimidation |url=https://www.danas.rs/vesti/politika/izbori-2023/savet-evrope-u-srbiji-veoma-polarizovana-kampanja-sa-nezabelezenim-nivoom-zastrasivanja/ |url-status=live |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231127181812/https://www.danas.rs/vesti/politika/izbori-2023/savet-evrope-u-srbiji-veoma-polarizovana-kampanja-sa-nezabelezenim-nivoom-zastrasivanja/ |archive-date=27 November 2023 |access-date=27 November 2023 |website=[[Danas (newspaper)|Danas]] |language=sr}}</ref> Raša Nedeljkov from CRTA expected a rigorous and unfair campaign with bigotry as its cornerstone; he listed the targeting of political opponents, media representatives, civil society organisations, and election observers as examples.<ref>{{Cite web |date=1 November 2023 |title=Nedeljkov: Možemo da očekujemo prljavu kampanju, već vidimo targetiranje protivnika, medija... |trans-title=Nedeljkov: We can expect a dirty campaign, we are already seeing the targeting of opponents, the media... |url=https://n1info.rs/vesti/izbori-2023/nedeljkov-mozemo-da-ocekujemo-prljavu-kampanju-vec-vidimo-targetiranje-protivnika-medija/ |url-status=live |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231101191524/https://n1info.rs/vesti/izbori-2023/nedeljkov-mozemo-da-ocekujemo-prljavu-kampanju-vec-vidimo-targetiranje-protivnika-medija/ |archive-date=1 November 2023 |access-date=2 November 2023 |website=[[N1 (TV channel)|N1]] |language=sr}}</ref> CRTA claimed that [[voter intimidation]] increased during the campaign period.<ref>{{Cite web |date=4 November 2023 |title=CRTA: Politički pritisci na građane su svakodnevni, a tokom izbora se pojačavaju |trans-title=CRTA: Political pressures on citizens are daily, and during elections they intensify |url=https://beta.rs/content/193563-crta-politicki-pritisci-na-gradane-su-svakodnevni-a-tokom-izbora-se-pojacavaju |url-status=live |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231106140110/https://beta.rs/content/193563-crta-politicki-pritisci-na-gradane-su-svakodnevni-a-tokom-izbora-se-pojacavaju |archive-date=6 November 2023 |access-date=6 November 2023 |website=[[Novinska agencija Beta]] |language=sr}}</ref> During the first three weeks of the election campaign, CRTA reported in its analysis that "inequality, suspicions, and threats" (''neravnopravnost, sumnje i pretnje'') were seen, claiming that government parties had significant advantage due to the abuse of public institutions.<ref>{{Cite web |date=23 November 2023 |title=CRTA: Neravnopravnost, sumnje i pretnje obeležile prvih 20 dana kampanje |trans-title=CRTA: Inequality, doubts and threats marked the first 20 days of the campaign |url=https://n1info.rs/vesti/izbori-2023/crta-neravnopravnost-sumnje-i-pretnje-obelezile-prvih-20-dana-kampanje/ |url-status=live |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231123215137/https://n1info.rs/vesti/izbori-2023/crta-neravnopravnost-sumnje-i-pretnje-obelezile-prvih-20-dana-kampanje/ |archive-date=23 November 2023 |access-date=23 November 2023 |website=[[N1 (TV channel)|N1]] |language=sr}}</ref> Amidst the campaign, the Centre for Investigative Journalism of Serbia (CINS) also released a report in which it was revealed that during the campaign period a youth organisation operating a call centre was tasked with intimidating voters. CINS also reported that the call centre also possessed a database of voters, with voters sorted in groups based on whether they are a member of SNS, a SNS voter, or a non-SNS voter.<ref name=":43">{{Cite web |last1=Milosavljević |first1=Ivana |last2=Ćurčić |first2=Teodora |last3=Kostić |first3=Vladimir |date=29 November 2023 |title=CINS u kol centru SNS-a: Agencija za hostese, kupovina glasova i milioni u kešu |trans-title=CINS in the SNS call centre: An agency for hostesses, buying voters, and millions in pockets |url=https://www.cins.rs/cins-u-kol-centru-sns-a-agencija-za-hostese-kupovina-glasova-i-milioni-u-kesu/ |url-status=live |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231129095736/https://www.cins.rs/cins-u-kol-centru-sns-a-agencija-za-hostese-kupovina-glasova-i-milioni-u-kesu/ |archive-date=29 November 2023 |access-date=29 November 2023 |website=Centar za istraživačko novinarstvo Srbije |language=sr}}</ref>

An informal organisation of high school students launched a campaign in October 2023 named "It's Up To You Too" (''I ti se pitaš''), aimed at first-time voters in the 2023 parliamentary election.<ref>{{Cite web |last=Ranković |first=Dunja |date=30 October 2023 |title=Kampanja "I ti se pitaš": Mladi koji prvi put izlaze na glasanje organizuju probne izbore |trans-title="It's Up To You Too" campaign: Young people who go out to vote for the first time organise trial elections |url=https://n1info.rs/vesti/kampanja-i-ti-se-pitas-mladi-koji-prvi-put-izlaze-na-glasanje-organizuju-probne-izbore/ |url-status=live |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231031012011/https://n1info.rs/vesti/kampanja-i-ti-se-pitas-mladi-koji-prvi-put-izlaze-na-glasanje-organizuju-probne-izbore/ |archive-date=31 October 2023 |access-date=31 October 2023 |website=[[N1 (TV channel)|N1]] |language=sr}}</ref> The Civic Initiatives, a non-governmental organisation, also launched a campaign with activists, professors, and public figures to boost the turnout and the number of controllers (members of polling stations) in the 2023 election.<ref>{{Cite web |last=Lukač |first=Davor |date=2 November 2023 |title=Kampanja "Dokle više" |trans-title="How Much More" Campaign |url=http://fonet.rs/drustvo/36385791/kampanja-dokle-vise.html |access-date=3 November 2023 |website=FoNet portal |language=sr |archive-date=3 November 2023 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231103211132/https://fonet.rs/drustvo/36385791/kampanja-dokle-vise.html |url-status=live }}</ref> A group of public figures, including actors [[Svetlana Bojković]], [[Dragan Bjelogrlić]], former [[Serbian Academy of Sciences and Arts]] president [[Vladimir S. Kostić]], legal scholar and judge [[Miodrag Majić]], and former University of Belgrade rector [[Ivanka Popović]], formed the initiative [[ProGlas]] on 7 November 2023 to boost the electoral turnout for the 2023 election and "stop the explosion of crime and corruption in society" (''zaustave eksploziju kriminala i korupcije u društvu'').<ref>{{Cite web |date=7 November 2023 |title=Grupa intelektualaca predstavila ProGlas, pozivaju građane da se ohrabre i menjaju Srbiju |trans-title=A group of intellectuals presented ProGlas, calling on citizens to be encouraged and change Serbia |url=https://beta.rs/content/193754-grupa-intelektualaca-predstavila-proglas-pozivaju-gradane-da-se-ohrabre-i-menjaju-srbiju |url-status=live |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231107130733/https://beta.rs/content/193754-grupa-intelektualaca-predstavila-proglas-pozivaju-gradane-da-se-ohrabre-i-menjaju-srbiju |archive-date=7 November 2023 |access-date=7 November 2023 |website=[[Novinska agencija Beta]] |language=sr}}</ref> The ProGlas initiative received than more 100,000 signatures of support by 15 November.<ref>{{Cite web |date=15 November 2023 |title="ProGlas" potpisalo više od 100.000 ljudi |trans-title="ProGlas" has been signed by more than 100,000 people |url=https://n1info.rs/vesti/izbori-2023/proglas-potpisalo-vise-od-100-000-ljudi/ |url-status=live |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231115121800/https://n1info.rs/vesti/izbori-2023/proglas-potpisalo-vise-od-100-000-ljudi/ |archive-date=15 November 2023 |access-date=15 November 2023 |website=[[N1 (TV channel)|N1]] |language=sr}}</ref> Regarding ProGlas, political scientist Duško Radosavljević said that "if we will remember this campaign for something, it will be because of the attempt by professional and respected people to ask for a new understanding of politics. For me, that is a force that provides a real chance for Serbia to be better" (''Ako ćemo po nečemu pamtiti ovu kampanju, to će biti taj pokušaj stručnih i uglednih ljudi da zatraže novo poimanje politike. To je za mene neka sila koja pruža realnu šansu da Srbija bude bolja'').<ref>{{Cite web |last=Petrović |first=Ivica |date=16 December 2023 |title=Vučić je svuda, ali SNS ipak može da izgubi izbore |trans-title=Vučić is everywhere, but SNS can still lose the elections |url=https://www.dw.com/sr/vu%C4%8Di%C4%87-je-svuda-ali-sns-ipak-mo%C5%BEe-da-izgubi-izbore/a-67742691 |url-status=live |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231216154604/https://www.dw.com/sr/vu%C4%8Di%C4%87-je-svuda-ali-sns-ipak-mo%C5%BEe-da-izgubi-izbore/a-67742691 |archive-date=16 December 2023 |access-date=16 December 2023 |website=[[Deutsche Welle]] |language=sr}}</ref>

The 2023 parliamentary election campaign also saw the increase of usage of the social media platform [[TikTok]] among politicians.<ref name=":44">{{Cite web |last=Reves |first=Aleksandra |date=29 November 2023 |title=Eksperti u sadržaju bez sadržaja: Kako se političari (ne)obraćaju mladima u kampanji? |trans-title=Content experts without content: How do politicians (not) address young people in the campaign? |url=https://www.021.rs/story/Info/Srbija/359821/Eksperti-u-sadrzaju-bez-sadrzaja-Kako-se-politicari-neobracaju-mladima-u-kampanji.html |access-date=30 November 2023 |website=021.rs |language=sr |archive-date=29 November 2023 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231129181454/https://www.021.rs/story/Info/Srbija/359821/Eksperti-u-sadrzaju-bez-sadrzaja-Kako-se-politicari-neobracaju-mladima-u-kampanji.html |url-status=live }}</ref><ref>{{Cite web |date=1 December 2023 |title=Koji je cilj poruka političara na TikToku: Privlačenje novih birača ili guranje mladih u apstinenciju? |trans-title=What is the goal of politicians' messages on TikTok: Attracting new voters or pushing young people into abstinence? |url=https://n1info.rs/vesti/izbori-2023/koji-je-cilj-poruka-politicara-na-tiktoku-privlacenje-novih-biraca-ili-guranje-mladih-u-apstinenciju/ |url-status=live |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231203114945/https://n1info.rs/vesti/izbori-2023/koji-je-cilj-poruka-politicara-na-tiktoku-privlacenje-novih-biraca-ili-guranje-mladih-u-apstinenciju/ |archive-date=3 December 2023 |access-date=1 December 2023 |website=[[N1 (TV channel)|N1]] |language=sr}}</ref> Vučić, Tadić, Tepić, SPS president [[Ivica Dačić]], and finance minister [[Siniša Mali]] all joined the platform in November 2023, to present themselves to younger voters.<ref name=":44" /><ref>{{Cite web |date=22 November 2023 |title=TikTok kao poligon za promociju: Gosti Euronews centra o tome šta političari rade na mrežama i kakav je efekat na birače |trans-title=TikTok as a training ground for promotion: Euronews center guests on what politicians are doing on the networks and what effect it has on voters |url=https://www.euronews.rs/srbija/politika/105850/tiktok-kao-poligon-za-promociju-gosti-euronews-centra-o-tome-sta-politicari-rade-na-mrezama-i-kakav-je-efekat-na-birace/vest |url-status=live |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231203114944/https://www.euronews.rs/srbija/politika/105850/tiktok-kao-poligon-za-promociju-gosti-euronews-centra-o-tome-sta-politicari-rade-na-mrezama-i-kakav-je-efekat-na-birace/vest |archive-date=3 December 2023 |access-date=30 November 2023 |website=[[Euronews]] |language=sr}}</ref> Jelena Kleut, a professor at the [[Faculty of Philosophy, University of Belgrade|Faculty of Philosophy of the University of Belgrade]], said that "knowing the Serbian Progressive Party, this move is based on data suggesting that the TikTok electorate might be interested in going to the polls in the election" (''Znajući Srpsku naprednu stranku, taj potez je zasnovan na nekim podacima koji govore da bi biračko telo koje se nalazi na TikTok-u moglo da bude zainteresovano da na ovim izborima izađe na glasanje'').<ref name=":44" />

=== Issues ===
Shortly before the election was called, Bursać predicted that the campaign would be filled with issues such as the ongoing tensions with Kosovo, jeopardised foreign policy positions due to the tensions with Kosovo, rising prices, and the mass shootings that occurred in May 2023.<ref name=":06" /> Vojislav Mihailović of CRTA said that opposition parties should put local politics, economy, corruption, crime and violence, as its main topics while campaigning, while he noted that respondents in opinion polls that CRTA conducted were mostly concerned about the economy.<ref>{{Cite web |date=13 October 2023 |title=Mihailović o izbornoj kampanji SNS: Neće biti čistija, a da li će biti prljavija – videćemo |trans-title=Mihailović on the SNS election campaign: It will not be cleaner, but we will see if it will be dirtier |url=https://n1info.rs/vesti/mihailovic-o-izbornoj-kampanji-sns-nece-biti-cistija-a-da-li-ce-biti-prljavija-videcemo/ |url-status=live |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231019043147/https://n1info.rs/vesti/mihailovic-o-izbornoj-kampanji-sns-nece-biti-cistija-a-da-li-ce-biti-prljavija-videcemo/ |archive-date=19 October 2023 |access-date=22 October 2023 |website=[[N1 (TV channel)|N1]] |language=sr}}</ref>

Journalists Bojan Bilbija (of ''[[Politika]]''), Zoran Panović (of Demostat), and Miloš Garić (''Kosovo Online'' editor-in-chief), jointly agreed that economic issues and the North Kosovo crisis would be the main issues of the elections.<ref>{{Cite web |date=6 October 2023 |title=Koje teme će biti dominantne uoči predstojećih izbora, kad god oni bili? |trans-title=Which topics will be dominant in the run-up to the upcoming elections, whenever they are? |url=https://www.rtv.rs/sr_lat/vojvodina/novi-sad/koje-teme-ce-biti-dominantne-uoci-predstojecih-izbora-kad-god-oni-bili_1481309.html |url-status=live |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231011220845/https://www.rtv.rs/sr_lat/vojvodina/novi-sad/koje-teme-ce-biti-dominantne-uoci-predstojecih-izbora-kad-god-oni-bili_1481309.html |archive-date=11 October 2023 |access-date=22 October 2023 |website=[[Radio Television of Vojvodina]] |language=sr}}</ref> Vladimir Pejić, the director of Agency Faktor Plus, listed the North Kosovo crisis, economic issues, and the fight against crime and corruption as the main issues of the election.<ref>{{Cite web |date=30 September 2023 |title=Pejić: Kosovo će biti jedna od tri dominantne teme na izborima |trans-title=Pejić: Kosovo will be one of the three dominant topics in the elections |url=https://www.blic.rs/vesti/politika/pejic-kosovo-ce-biti-jedna-od-tri-dominantne-teme-na-izborima-u-srbiji/260wmkf |url-status=live |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231101094201/https://www.blic.rs/vesti/politika/pejic-kosovo-ce-biti-jedna-od-tri-dominantne-teme-na-izborima-u-srbiji/260wmkf |archive-date=1 November 2023 |access-date=22 October 2023 |website=[[Blic]] |language=sr}}</ref> Milivojević and political consultant Nikola Tomić named Kosovo as the main issue for the upcoming elections.<ref>{{Cite web |date=5 October 2023 |title=Kosovo bi mogla biti glavna tema izbora: "Opozicija se decenijama ravna prema najjačem u vlasti umesto prema građanima" |trans-title=Kosovo could be the main topic of the election: "For decades, the opposition has been aligning itself with the strongest in power instead of the citizens." |url=https://www.euronews.rs/srbija/politika/101528/kosovo-bi-mogla-biti-glavna-tema-izbora-opozicija-se-decenijama-ravna-prema-najjacem-u-vlasti-umesto-prema-gradanima/vest |url-status=live |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231101092659/https://www.euronews.rs/srbija/politika/101528/kosovo-bi-mogla-biti-glavna-tema-izbora-opozicija-se-decenijama-ravna-prema-najjacem-u-vlasti-umesto-prema-gradanima/vest |archive-date=1 November 2023 |access-date=22 October 2023 |website=[[Euronews]] |language=sr}}</ref> Klačar named living standards, inflation and prices, Kosovo, foreign policy positions, and European Union membership as main issues,<ref>{{Cite web |date=20 October 2023 |title=Klačar: Usvajanjem medijskih zakona se ne mogu očekivati velike promene do kraja godine |trans-title=Klačar: With the adoption of media laws, no major changes can be expected until the end of the year |url=https://www.rtv.rs/sr_lat/politika/klacar-usvajanjem-medijskih-zakona-se-ne-mogu-ocekivati-velike-promene-do-kraja-godine_1486084.html |url-status=live |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231021144120/https://www.rtv.rs/sr_lat/politika/klacar-usvajanjem-medijskih-zakona-se-ne-mogu-ocekivati-velike-promene-do-kraja-godine_1486084.html |archive-date=21 October 2023 |access-date=23 October 2023 |website=[[Radio Television of Vojvodina]] |language=sr}}</ref> while Stojanović listed living standards, inflation, and Kosovo as main topics, also claiming that "there will also be enormous pressure on SNS voters, on public sector employees, and blackmailing".<ref>{{Cite web |last=Antonijević |first=Milena |date=7 November 2023 |title=Serbia's election campaigns all highlight Kosovo and inflation |url=https://www.euractiv.com/section/politics/news/serbias-election-campaigns-all-highlight-kosovo-and-inflation/ |url-status=live |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231107070843/https://www.euractiv.com/section/politics/news/serbias-election-campaigns-all-highlight-kosovo-and-inflation/ |archive-date=7 November 2023 |access-date=7 November 2023 |website=[[Euractiv]]}}</ref>

=== Party campaigns ===
According to the preliminary report of the Agency for the Prevention of Corruption from 14 December, SNS spent {{Currency|4500000|EUR}} during the campaign period, while SPS spent {{Currency|1600000|EUR}} and VMSZ spent around {{Currency|100000|EUR}}. From the opposition, Serbia on the West alliance spent more than {{Currency|200000|EUR}}, SPN spent {{Currency|82000|EUR}}, Narodna spent {{Currency|46000|EUR}}, [[We – Voice from the People]] spent {{Currency|4490|EUR}}, and SRS spent {{Currency|1500|EUR}}. From minority parties, the [[Russian Party (Serbia)|Russian Party]] spent {{Currency|162000|EUR}}.<ref name=":46">{{Cite news |last1=Janković |first1=Jelena |last2=Katić |first2=Miloš |date=14 December 2023 |title=Najskuplju kampanju u Srbiji vodi Vučićeva partija |trans-title=The most expensive campaign in Serbia is run by Vučić's party |url=https://www.slobodnaevropa.org/a/srbija-izbori-kampanja-troskovi/32730436.html |url-status=live |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231214104948/https://www.slobodnaevropa.org/a/srbija-izbori-kampanja-troskovi/32730436.html |archive-date=14 December 2023 |access-date=14 December 2023 |work=[[Radio Free Europe]] |language=sr}}</ref>

Vučević announced that SNS would begin its campaign in late October, after the 15-year anniversary of the founding assembly of SNS.<ref>{{Cite web |date=10 November 2023 |title=Vučеvić najavio sеdnicu GO SNS: Na proslavi 15 godina strankе ulazimo u izbornu kampanju |trans-title=Vučević announced the session of the main board of SNS: On the celebration of the 15 years of the party, we will enter the |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231016183558/https://www.blic.rs/vesti/politika/vucevic-najavio-sednicu-go-sns-na-proslavi-15-godina-stranke-ulazimo-u-izbornu/6zse8y0 |archive-date=16 October 2023 |access-date=21 October 2023 |website=[[Blic]] |language=sr}}</ref> Despite this, SNS organised gatherings with its supporters before the 15-year celebration to promote the party for the upcoming elections.<ref>{{Cite web |last=Savić |first=Danilo |date=17 October 2023 |title=Velika mrsna SNS kampanja: Živeo predsednik, a sad dajte pečenje da se "ne ladi" |trans-title=A big fat SNS campaign: Long live the president, now give the roast so that it "does not get cold" |url=https://nova.rs/vesti/politika/ziveo-predsednik-a-sad-dajte-pecenje-da-se-ne-ladi-naprednjaci-pod-satrama-okupljaju-narod-i-traze-glasove/ |url-status=live |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231022224359/https://nova.rs/vesti/politika/ziveo-predsednik-a-sad-dajte-pecenje-da-se-ne-ladi-naprednjaci-pod-satrama-okupljaju-narod-i-traze-glasove/ |archive-date=22 October 2023 |access-date=21 October 2023 |website=[[NOVA portal]] |language=sr}}</ref> SNS was endorsed by its former party president Vučić, who also announced that [[Tomislav Nikolić]], former president of Serbia and president of SNS, would participate in its campaign.<ref>{{Cite web |date=21 October 2023 |title=Vučić na proslavi SNS u Šapcu: Predstojeći izbori najvažniji |url=https://n1info.rs/vesti/foto-video-vucic-na-proslavi-sns-u-sapcu-predstojeci-izbori-najvazniji-do-sada/ |url-status=live |access-date=23 October 2023 |website=[[N1 (TV channel)|N1]] |language=sr}}</ref><ref>{{Cite web |date=24 October 2023 |title=Kako je Vučić ucenjivao svog političkog oca kog sad potura glasačima: |archive-date=27 October 2023 |access-date=24 October 2023 |website=[[NOVA portal]] |language=sr}}</ref> SNS began collecting signatures for its electoral list on 1 November.<ref>{{Cite web |date=1 November 2023 |title=SNS počela prikupljanje potpisa podrške za predaju izbornih lista |trans-title=SNS started collecting signatures of support for the submission of election lists
