submitted its list to RIK a day later, with 92,637 signatures in total.<ref>{{Cite web |date=2 November 2023 |title=SNS prva predala RIK-u izbornu listu uz 92.637 potpisa podrške |trans-title=SNS was the first to submit the election list to the RIK with 92,637 signatures of support |url=https://www.tanjug.rs/izbori-2023/vesti/57305/sns-prva-predala-rik-u-izbornu-listu-uz-92637-potpisa-podrske/vest |access-date=2 November 2023 |website=[[Tačno d.o.o.|Tanjug]] |language=sr}}</ref> RIK confirmed its list on 3 November with 88,083 valid signatures collected.<ref name="RIK_SNS" />

[[Stefan Krkobabić]], the leader of [[PUPS – Solidarity and Justice|Party of United Pensioners of Serbia]] (PUPS) in the National Assembly, expressed his support for SNS during the campaign, while announcing that PUPS would campaign on introducing a guaranteed [[social pension]].<ref>{{Cite web |date=15 October 2023 |title=Stefan Krkobabić: PUPS će insistirati na socijalnim penzijama |trans-title=Stefan Krkobabić: PUPS will insist on social pensions |url=https://beta.rs/content/192301-stefan-krkobabic-pups-ce-insistirati-na-socijalnim-penzijama |url-status=live |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20231020163622/https://beta.rs/content/192301-stefan-krkobabic-pups-ce-insistirati-na-socijalnim-penzijama |archive-date=20 October 2023 |access-date=22 October 2023 |website=[[Novinska agencija Beta]] |language=sr}}</ref> The [[Strength of Serbia Movement]], a SNS ally since 2010,<ref>{{Cite web |date=16 November 2010 |title=Opozicija se okuplja oko Srpske napredne stranke |trans-title=Opposition is gathering around the Serbian Progressive Party |url=https://boom93.rs/arhiva/info-arhiva/srbija/opozicija-se-okuplja-oko-srpske-napredne-stranke/ |access-date=2 September 2022 |website=Boom93 |language=sr |archive-date=2 February 2022 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20220202002617/https://boom93.rs/arhiva/info-arhiva/srbija/opozicija-se-okuplja-oko-srpske-napredne-stranke/ |url-status=live }}</ref> announced that they would not contest the 2023 parliamentary election; the [[Serbian Renewal Movement]] of [[Vuk Drašković]] did not sign a cooperation agreement with SNS for the 2023 election, though two of its candidates still contested the election on the SNS electoral list.<ref>{{Cite web |date=7 November 2023 |title=Zašto Karićev PSS nije na listi SNS prvi put od 2012. godine |trans-title=Why Karić's PSS is not on the SNS list for the first time since 2012 |url=https://n1info.rs/vesti/izbori-2023/zasto-karicev-pss-nije-na-listi-sns-prvi-put-od-2012-godine/ |access-date=7 November 2023 |website=[[N1 (TV channel)|N1]] |language=sr}}</ref> Individuals who were formerly critical of SNS and Vučić, including [[Tatjana Macura]], formerly aligned with DJB, [[Radoslav Milojičić]], formerly aligned with DS, and [[Dejan Bulatović]], formerly aligned with SSP, were announced as candidates on the SNS electoral list.<ref>{{Cite web |date=5 November 2023 |title=Macura, Kena, Bulatović: Vučića zvali šonjom i izdajnikom Kosova – novi SNS lavovi za svoj prelet krive sve od Đilasa do Danasa |trans-title=Macura, Kena, Bulatović: They called Vučić a coward and a traitor of Kosovo – the new SNS lions blame everyone from Đilas to Danas for their switch |url=https://www.danas.rs/vesti/politika/izbori-2023/macura-kena-milojicic-vucica-zvali-sonjom-i-izdajnikom-kosova-novi-sns-lavovi-za-svoj-prelet-krive-sve-od-djilasa-do-danasa/ |access-date=7 November 2023 |website=[[Danas (newspaper)|Danas]] |language=sr}}</ref>

Despite no longer being the president of SNS, but still serving as president of Serbia, Vučić was its main representative in the election campaign.<ref>{{Cite web |last=Latković |first=Nataša |date=29 October 2023 |title=Predsednik Srbije u "ful gasu": Vučić nezaustavljivo troši naše pare da bi sačuvao vlast |trans-title=The President of Serbia in "full throttle": Vučić unstoppably spends our money to preserve power |url=https://nova.rs/vesti/politika/predsednik-srbije-u-ful-gasu-vucic-nezaustavljivo-trosi-nase-pare-da-bi-sacuvao-vlast/ |access-date=29 October 2023 |website=[[NOVA portal]] |language=sr}}</ref><ref>{{Cite web |last=Gajić |first=Petar |date=11 November 2023 |title=Predsednik svih građana, a u kampanji SNS-a: Vučić opet isto, samo ne izlazi iz frižidera |trans-title=President of all citizens, but in the SNS campaign: Vučić is doing the same again, only he doesn't come out of the fridge |url=https://n1info.rs/vesti/izbori-2023/predsednik-svih-gradjana-a-u-kampanji-sns-a-vucic-opet-isto-samo-ne-izlazi-iz-frizidera/ |access-date=13 November 2023 |website=[[N1 (TV channel)|N1]] |language=sr}}</ref> He was not a candidate in any elections in 2023.<ref>{{Cite web |last=Kaiser |first=Markus |date=15 December 2023 |title=Election in the shadow of an all-powerful president |url=https://www.freiheit.org/de/westliche-balkanlaender/election-shadow-all-powerful-president |access-date=16 December 2023 |website=[[Friedrich Naumann Foundation]]}}</ref> During the campaign, Vučić strongly criticised the opposition, alleging that a vote for them is "a vote for the president of the Party of Freedom and Justice, [[Dragan Đilas]], a vote for the independence of Kosovo, and for the introduction of sanctions to Russia" (''svaki glas za opoziciju glas za predsednika Stranke slobode i pravde Dragana Đilasa, glas za nezavisnost Kosova i za uvođenje sankcija [Rusiji]''),<ref name=":54">{{Cite web |last=Stojković |first=Anđelija |date=30 October 2023 |title=Opozicija jednako Đilas |trans-title=Opposition equals Đilas |url=http://fonet.rs/politika/36384332/opozicija-jednako-djilas.html |access-date=1 November 2023 |website=FoNet portal |language=sr}}</ref> and that Đilas controlled the entire opposition.<ref>{{Cite web |date=12 November 2023 |title=Weekly Campaign Overview: SNS holds first three rallies, focuses on salaries and infrastructure |url=https://serbiaelects.europeanwesternbalkans.com/2023/11/12/weekly-campaign-overview-6-12-november-sns-holds-first-three-rallies-focuses-on-salaries-and-infrastructure/ |access-date=13 November 2023 |website=[[European Western Balkans]]}}</ref> He portrayed the election as "between the past [...] and the future" (''između "prošlosti"'' [...] ''i "budućnosti''), while alleging with Vučević that there was a plan to overthrow SNS from power.<ref>{{Cite web |date=18 October 2023 |title=Vučić: Đukanović priča gluposti, ZSO budućnost za Kurtija, priznaćemo volju naroda nakon izbora |trans-title=Vučić: Đukanović is talking nonsense, ZSO is the future for Kurti, we will recognise the will of the people after the elections |url=https://beta.rs/content/192483-vucic-dukanovic-prica-gluposti-zso-buducnost-za-kurtija-priznacemo-volju-naroda-nakon-izbora |access-date=22 October 2023 |website=[[Novinska agencija Beta]] |language=sr}}</ref><ref>{{Cite web |date=22 October 2023 |title=Vučić na Pinku započeo kampanju: Postoji plan stranih službi za svrgavanje SNS |trans-title=Vučić started a campaign on Pink: There is a plan of foreign governments to overthrow the SNS |url=https://n1info.rs/vesti/vucic-na-pinku-plan-stranih-sluzbi-za-rusenje-sns/ |access-date=23 October 2023 |website=[[N1 (TV channel)|N1]] |language=sr}}</ref><ref>{{Cite web |date=24 October 2023 |title=Vučević: Apelovao sam da se poveća izborni cenzus, ali to nije prihvaćeno |trans-title=Vučević: I appealed to increase the electoral threshold, but it was not accepted |url=https://n1info.rs/vesti/vucevic-apelovao-sam-da-se-poveca-izborni-cenzus-ali-to-nije-prihvaceno/ |access-date=24 October 2023 |website=[[N1 (TV channel)|N1]] |language=sr}}</ref> Brnabić and Minister [[Aleksandar Martinović]] claimed that the opposition wanted to create disorder and incite a civil war, respectively.<ref>{{Cite web |date=10 November 2023 |title=Ministar Martinović: Opozicija želi da izazove građanski rat |trans-title=Minister Martinović: The opposition wants to provoke a civil war |url=https://www.danas.rs/vesti/politika/izbori-2023/ministar-martinovic-opozicija-zeli-da-izazove-gradjanski-rat/ |access-date=10 November 2023 |website=[[Danas (newspaper)|Danas]] |language=sr}}</ref><ref>{{Cite web |last=Milenković |first=M. R. |date=11 November 2023 |title=Ne sprema opozicija haos i demonstracije posle izbora, već se vlast plaši novog 5. oktobra: Izjava Ane Brnabić je klasična priča "o lopovu koji viče držte lopova" |trans-title=The opposition is not preparing chaos and demonstrations after the elections, but the government is afraid of a new 5 October: Ana Brnabić's statement is a classic story "about a thief who shouts, catch the thief" |url=https://www.danas.rs/vesti/politika/izbori-2023/izjava-ane-brnabic-haos/ |access-date=11 November 2023 |website=[[Danas (newspaper)|Danas]] |language=sr}}</ref> These statements were criticised by CRTA, and opposition politicians such as Lazović, Obradović, and Jovanović.<ref>{{Cite web |date=11 November 2023 |title=CRTA: Omogućite građanima da izađu na izbore bez straha od "haosa i građanskog rata" |trans-title=CRTA: Let citizens to go to the polls without fear of "chaos and civil war" |url=https://n1info.rs/vesti/izbori-2023/crta-omogucite-gradjanima-da-izadju-na-izbore-bez-straha-od-haosa-i-gradjanskog-rata/ |access-date=13 November 2023 |website=N1 |language=sr}}</ref><ref>{{Cite web |last=Tatalović |first=Žaklina |date=12 November 2023 |title=Vlast zastrašuje građane: Martinović pominje čak i građanski rat, opozicija – čuvamo volju naroda |trans-title=The government intimidates the citizens: Martinović even mentions the civil war, the opposition – we protect the will of the people |url=https://n1info.rs/vesti/izbori-2023/vlast-zastrasuje-gradjane-martinovic-pominje-cak-i-gradjanski-rat-opozicija-cuvamo-volju-naroda/ |access-date=13 November 2023 |website=N1 |language=sr}}</ref>

SNS campaigned on populist messages. Vučić announced on 29 October that the government of Serbia would by 1 December payout {{Currency|10,000|RSD}} to beneficiaries of social assistance, of which there are 170,000 in Serbia, to blind, demented, and elderly persons, of which there are 51,000, and that students would receive discounts on train and plane tickets.<ref>{{Cite web |date=29 October 2023 |title=Penzionerima i studentima popust za vozne i avio-karte, po 10.000 dinara korisnicima socijalne pomoći do 1. decembra |trans-title=Pensioners and students discount for train and plane tickets, 10,000 dinars each for beneficiaries of social assistance until 1 December |url=https://www.euronews.rs/biznis/biznis-vesti/103503/penzionerima-i-studentima-popust-za-vozne-i-avio-karte-po-10000-dinara-korisnicima-socijalne-pomoci-do-1-decembra/vest |access-date=29 October 2023 |website=[[Euronews]] |language=sr}}</ref> Despite the government denying that this decision would influence the voters, Nemanja Nenadić, from non-profit organisation [[Transparency Serbia]], listed the payouts and discounts as "one of the ways to subtly influence the will of the citizens, to make them think that the government makes concessions to them" (''jedan od načina da se malo suptilnije utiče na volju građana, da pomisle kako im vlast čini ustupke'').<ref>{{Cite news |last=Bogdanović |first=Nevena |date=30 October 2023 |title=Srbija na pragu novih izbora: Koliko će koštati vanredno glasanje? |trans-title=Serbia on the threshold of new elections: How much will the snap vote cost? |url=https://www.slobodnaevropa.org/a/izbori-srbija-kampanja-troskovi/32660328.html |access-date=1 November 2023 |work=[[Radio Free Europe]] |language=sr}}</ref> In response to Vučić's campaign, DS submitted a report to the Anti-Corruption Agency, alleging that Vučić allegedly abused power to boost SNS in the elections. The Bureau of Social Research (BIRODI) also claimed that Vučić violated Article 40 of the Law on Prevention of Corruption.<ref name=":62">{{Cite web |last=Kojić |first=Nikola |date=31 October 2023 |title=Deo opozicije podnosi prijavu protiv Aleksandra Vučića |trans-title=Part of the opposition files a report against Aleksandar Vučić |url=https://n1info.rs/vesti/opozicija-podnosi-prijavu-protiv-aleksandra-vucica/ |access-date=1 November 2023 |website=[[N1 (TV channel)|N1]] |language=sr}}</ref> Zoran Čvorović, a professor at the [[University of Belgrade Faculty of Law|Faculty of Law]], argued that as president of Serbia, Vučić violated the constitution due to him being listed as the representatives of all SNS-led lists in the 2023 elections.<ref>{{Cite web |date=2 November 2023 |title=Profesor Čvorović za BETU: Vučić prekršio Ustav, Srbija je u stanju ličnog režima |trans-title=Professor Čvorović for Beta: Vučić violated the Constitution, Serbia is in a state of personal regime |url=https://beta.rs/content/193468-profesor-cvorovic-za-betu-vucic-prekrsio-ustav-srbija-je-u-stanju-licnog-rezima |access-date=3 November 2023 |website=[[Novinska agencija Beta]] |language=sr}}</ref> RIK rejected all 15 citizens' complaints related to Vučić being listed in the name of the SNS-led electoral list, despite not taking part in the elections, saying that "Vučić has agreed on paper for his name to be mentioned on the electoral list" (''Vučić pismeno saglasio da svoje ima da jednoj listi'').<ref>{{Cite web |date=6 November 2023 |title=RIK odbacio prigovore da Vučić nije smeo da stavi svoje ime na izbornu listu |trans-title=RIK rejected complaints that Vučić was not allowed to put his name on the electoral list |url=https://nova.rs/vesti/politika/rik-odbacio-prigovore-da-vucic-nije-smeo-da-stavi-svoje-ime-na-izbornu-listu/ |access-date=7 November 2023 |website=[[NOVA portal]] |language=sr}}</ref> The government of Serbia introduced more populist measures in late November, such as {{Currency|10,000|RSD}} payouts to high school students.<ref>{{Cite web |date=1 December 2023 |title=I škole u predizbornoj kampanji: Uvukli profesore u populističke mere Vlade o podeli 10.000 dinara |trans-title=And schools are in the pre-election campaign too: Teachers were drawn into the government's populist measures on the distribution of 10,000 dinars |url=https://n1info.rs/vesti/i-skole-u-predizbornoj-kampanji-uvukli-profesore-u-populisticke-mere-vlade-o-podeli-10-000-dinara/ |access-date=1 December 2023 |website=[[N1 (TV channel)|N1]] |language=sr}}</ref>

Orlić and [[Nevena Đurić]], vice-presidents of SNS, campaigned in [[Ruma]], where they pledged citizens more investments in infrastructure, education, and technology.<ref>{{Cite web |last=Janković |first=Miloš |date=8 November 2023 |title=Orlić i Đurić posetili Rumu |trans-title=Orlić and Đurić visited Ruma |url=http://fonet.rs/izbori-2023/36388185/orlic-i-djuric-posetili-rumu.html |access-date=8 November 2023 |website=FoNet portal |language=sr}}</ref> Another campaign meeting was held on 9 November in [[Pirot]], featuring Vučić, Brnabić, Vučević, Stamatović, and PUPS leader [[Milan Krkobabić]] as speakers.<ref>{{Cite web |date=9 November 2023 |title=Predsednik države opet na partijskom predizbornom mitingu SNS |trans-title=The President of Serbia again at a SNS pre-election party rally |url=https://n1info.rs/vesti/izbori-2023/vucic-na-mitingu-sns-u-pirotu-hocu-da-za-cetiri-godine-prosecna-plata-bude-veca-od-1-000-evra/ |access-date=9 November 2023 |website=[[N1 (TV channel)|N1]] |language=sr}}</ref> SNS also campaigned on improving the status of women and introducing more [[mammogram]]s in Serbian hospitals.<ref>{{Cite web |date=11 November 2023 |title=Kako naprednjaci, Vučević i Pilja, u kampanji love glasove žena? |trans-title=How do the Progressives, Vučević and Pilja, hunt women's votes in the campaign? |url=https://www.danas.rs/vesti/politika/izbori-2023/kako-naprednjaci-vucevic-i-pilja-u-kampanji-love-glasove-zena/ |access-date=13 November 2023 |website=[[Danas (newspaper)|Danas]] |language=sr}}</ref><ref>{{Cite web |date=11 November 2023 |title=Vučević u Novom Sadu, Beški i Selenči |trans-title=Vučević in Novi Sad, Beška and Selenča |url=https://www.rtv.rs/sr_lat/izbori-2023/parlamentarni-izbori/vucevic-u-novom-sadu-beski-i-selenci_1492509.html |access-date=13 November 2023 |website=[[Radio Television of Vojvodina]] |language=sr}}</ref> The party has also expressed its support for the accession of Serbia to the European Union.<ref name=":45">{{Cite news |last=Cvetković |first=Ljudmila |date=1 December 2023 |title=Ko se takmiči na parlamentarnim izborima u Srbiji? |trans-title=Who is competing in the parliamentary elections in Serbia? |url=https://www.slobodnaevropa.org/a/srbija-parlamentarni-izbori-kandidati/32707104.html |access-date=2 December 2023 |work=[[Radio Free Europe]] |language=sr}}</ref> Nikolić made his first public appearance since 2017 at the SNS convention in Belgrade on 2 December.<ref>{{Cite web |date=3 December 2023 |title="Nikolić na mitingu SNS – da kompenzuje 'izdaju Kosova'": Kakva nam je predizborna kampanja |trans-title="Nikolić at the SNS meeting – to compensate for the 'betrayal of Kosovo'": How is the pre-election campaign |url=https://n1info.rs/vesti/izbori-2023/nikolic-na-mitingu-sns-da-kompenzuje-izdaju-kosova-kakva-nam-je-predizborna-kampanja/ |access-date=3 December 2023 |website=[[N1 (TV channel)|N1]] |language=sr}}</ref> SNS held its last convention in Novi Sad on 13 December.<ref>{{Cite web |last=Pavkov |first=Ksenija |date=13 December 2023 |title=Završni miting Srpske napredne stranke održan u Novom Sadu |trans-title=The final meeting of the Serbian Progressive Party was held in Novi Sad |url=https://n1info.rs/vesti/izbori-2023/zavrsni-miting-srpske-napredne-stranke-odrzan-u-novom-sadu/ |access-date=14 December 2023 |website=[[N1 (TV channel)|N1]] |language=sr}}</ref>

==== Socialist Party of Serbia ====
SPS, JS, and Zeleni signed a cooperation agreement on 1 November, announcing that they would contest the elections together under the same electoral list name, "Ivica Dačić – Prime Minister of Serbia", that they contested with in the 2022 parliamentary election.<ref name=":112">{{Cite web |date=1 November 2023 |title=Socijalistička partija Srbije, Jedinstvena Srbija i Zeleni Srbije potpisali koalicioni sporazum |trans-title=The Socialist Party of Serbia, United Serbia and the Greens of Serbia signed a coalition agreement |url=https://beta.rs/content/193420-socijalisticka-parija-srbije-jedinstvena-srbija-i-zeleni-srbije-potpisali-koalicioni-sporazum |access-date=1 November 2023 |website=[[Novinska agencija Beta]] |language=sr}}</ref> The SPS-led coalition submitted its list to RIK on 2 November, with more than 20,000 signatures.<ref>{{Cite web |date=2 November 2023 |title=SNS prva predala izborne liste; Tadić: SDS prihvata da bude na listi "Srbija protiv nasilja" |trans-title=SNS submitted its list first; Tadić: SDS accepts to be on the "Serbia Against Violence" list |url=https://rts.rs/lat/vesti/izbori-2023/5302210/sns-prva-predala-izborne-liste-tadic-sds-prihvata-da-bude-na-listi-srbija-protiv-nasilja.html |access-date=3 November 2023 |website=[[Radio Television of Serbia]] |language=sr}}</ref> RIK confirmed their list on 4 November with 19,618 valid signatures in total.<ref name="RIK_SPS"/> Boban Stojanović argued that RIK should have rejected the SPS electoral list due to a number of signatures of support being certified by notaries who are not listed in the notaries database.<ref>{{Cite web |date=7 November 2023 |title=Boban Stojanović: RIK je morao da poništi listu SPS-a za parlamentarne izbore zbog nepravilnosti |trans-title=Boban Stojanović: RIK had to cancel the SPS list for the parliamentary elections due to irregularities |url=https://beta.rs/content/193723-boban-stojanovic-rik-je-morao-da-ponisti-listu-sps-a-za-parlamentarne-izbore-zbog-nepravilnosti |access-date=7 November 2023 |website=[[Novinska agencija Beta]] |language=sr}}</ref>

Despite being a coalition government partner with SNS since 2012, SPS official [[Dušan Bajatović]] was a target of attacks in articles published by pro-government media.<ref>{{Cite web |last=Milenković |first=M. R. |date=15 November 2023 |title=Opozicioni status je najveća noćna mora Ivice Dačića: Naprednjaci gađajući Bajatovića, ciljaju lidera SPS |trans-title=The opposition status is Ivica Dačić's biggest nightmare: Progressives, targeting Bajatović, also targeting SPS leader |url=https://www.danas.rs/vesti/politika/izbori-2023/sns-dacic-bajatovic/ |access-date=15 November 2023 |website=[[Danas (newspaper)|Danas]] |language=sr}}</ref> During the campaign period, SPS presented themselves as "guarantees of political stability" (''garant političke stabilnosti'') while also expressing support for youth rights and youth activism.<ref>{{Cite web |date=12 November 2023 |title=Dačić: SPS je garant političke stabilnosti |trans-title=Dačić: SPS is the guarantee to political stability |url=https://www.euronews.rs/srbija/politika/104825/dacic-sps-je-garant-politicke-stabilnosti/vest |access-date=13 November 2023 |website=[[Euronews]] |language=sr}}</ref><ref>{{Cite web |date=17 November 2023 |title=Ivica Dačić: Potreban nam je omladinski aktivizam |trans-title=Ivica Dačić: We need youth activism |url=https://www.tanjug.rs/izbori-2023/vesti/59904/ivica-dacic-potreban-nam-je-omladinski-aktivizam/vest |access-date=17 November 2023 |website=[[Tačno d.o.o.|Tanjug]] |language=sr}}</ref> Dačić also to portrayed the coalition as socialist; while campaigning in [[Ljubovija]], Dačić said that their voters would automatically also vote for "patriotism and socialism" (''patriotizam i socijalizam'').<ref>{{Cite web |date=18 November 2023 |title=Predizbirna konvencija liste Ivica Dačića-Premijer Srbije u Ljuboviji |trans-title=Pre-election convention of the list of Ivica Dačić – Prime Minister of Serbia in Ljubovija |url=https://www.rtv.rs/sr_lat/izbori-2023/parlamentarni-izbori/predizbirna-konvencija-liste-ivica-dacica-premijer-srbije-u-ljuboviji_1494442.html |access-date=18 November 2023 |website=[[Radio Television of Vojvodina]] |language=sr}}</ref> While campaigning in [[Mrčajevci]], Dačić also said that the SPS coalition supports free education, free universal health care, and social funds.<ref>{{Cite web |date=21 November 2023 |title=Dačić: Verujem u socijalističke principe i jednake mogućnosti |trans-title=Dačić: I believe in socialist principles and equal opportunities |url=https://www.danas.rs/vesti/politika/izbori-2023/dacic-verujem-u-socijalisticke-principe-i-jednake-mogucnosti/ |access-date=21 November 2023 |website=[[Danas (newspaper)|Danas]] |language=sr}}</ref> Dačić also reflected on his opinions about Milošević during the campaign, saying that "Milošević was an example of how to love and defend your country" (''Milošević bio primer kako se zemlja voli i brani'').<ref>{{Cite web |date=23 November 2023 |title=Dačić: Milošević bio primer kako se zemlja voli i brani, ne štedeći ni sopstveni život |trans-title=Dačić: Milošević was an example of how to love and defend the country, not even sparing one's own life |url=https://n1info.rs/vesti/izbori-2023/dacic-milosevic-bio-primer-kako-se-zemlja-voli-i-brani-ne-stedeci-ni-sopstveni-zivot/ |access-date=23 November 2023 |website=[[N1 (TV channel)|N1]] |language=sr}}</ref> The SPS coalition also expressed its support for the accession of Serbia to the European Union.<ref name=":45" />

==== Serbia Against Violence ====
[[File:Serbia Against Violence convention in Belgrade, 12 December 2023 (4) (cropped).jpg|thumb|alt=Serbia Against Violence convention in Belgrade on 12 December 2023|SPN campaigned on increasing pensions, salaries, and investing in education and universal health care]]
Members of the SPN coalition, with the addition of Romanian Party and the Civic Democratic Party, signed a cooperation agreement on 3 November, saying that the "fight against crime and corruption, stopping inflation and the impoverishment of citizens, restoring pensions reduced in 2014, and the importance of security, especially for the youngest" (''borbe protiv kriminala i korupcije, zaustavljanja inflacije ii osiromašenja gradjana, vraćanje penzija smanjenih 2014. godine i značaj bezbednosti, posebno za najmlađe'') would be their main issues during the campaign.<ref>{{Cite web |date=3 November 2023 |title=Stranke i pokreti oko liste Srbija protiv nasilja potpisali koalicioni sporazum |trans-title=Parties and movements around the Serbia Against Violence list signed a coalition agreement |url=https://beta.rs/content/193523-stranke-i-pokreti-oko-liste-srbija-protiv-nasilja-potpisali-koalicioni-sporazum |access-date=3 November 2023 |website=[[Novinska agencija Beta]] |language=sr}}</ref> SPN submitted its list to RIK on 8 November.<ref>{{Cite web |date=8 November 2023 |title=Izborna koalicija Srbija protiv nasilja predala listu |trans-title=Electoral alliance Serbia Against Violence submitted its list |url=https://n1info.rs/vesti/izbori-2023/izborna-koalicija-srbija-protiv-nasilja-predaje-listu-rik-u/ |access-date=8 November 2023 |website=[[N1 (TV channel)|N1]] |language=sr}}</ref> Their electoral list was confirmed by RIK on 9 November.<ref name="RIK_SPN" /> While the negotiations were still ongoing, Lutovac listed [[Gordana Matković]], a minister under the governments of [[Zoran Đinđić]] and [[Zoran Živković (politician)|Zoran Živković]], and {{Ill|Ivan Vujačić|sr|Ivan Vujačić}}, former leader of DS in the National Assembly, as two potential candidates for the position of prime minister.<ref>{{Cite web |date=18 October 2023 |title=Lutovac: Nema kamena spoticanja u proevropskoj opoziciji, Matković ili Vujačić za premijera |trans-title=Lutovac: There are no stumbling blocks in the pro-European opposition, Matković or Vujačić for prime minister |url=https://beta.rs/content/192468-lutovac-nema-kamena-spoticanja-u-proevropskoj-opoziciji-matkovic-ili-vujacic-za-premijera |access-date=21 October 2023 |website=[[Novinska agencija Beta]] |language=sr}}</ref> SPN, however, decided to present Tepić and Aleksić as their two main representatives.<ref name=":39" />

Before and during the official campaign period, politicians affiliated with SPN, including Tepić, Aleksić, Ćuta, and [[Srđan Milivojević]], a DS member of the National Assembly, were featured on propaganda flyers that were spread in Novi Sad and Belgrade, depicting them in a negative matter.<ref name=":210">{{Cite web |last=Savić |first=Danilo |date=20 October 2023 |title=Izbori nisu ni raspisani, a naprednjaci već krenuli u napad na lidere opozicije: U kampanju opasnog targetiranja uključili su se visoki funkcioneri SNS |trans-title=The elections have not even been announced, and the Progressives have already started attacking the leaders of the opposition: high-ranking SNS officials joined the campaign of dangerous targeting |url=https://nova.rs/vesti/politika/izbori-nisu-ni-raspisani-a-naprednjaci-vec-krenuli-u-napad-na-lidere-opozicije-u-kampanju-opasnog-targetiranja-ukljucili-su-se-visoki-funkcioneri-sns/ |access-date=22 October 2023 |website=[[NOVA portal]] |language=sr}}</ref><ref>{{Cite web |date=21 October 2023 |title=U poštanskim sandučićima leci protiv Milivojevića i Jovanovića |trans-title=In mailboxes, flyers against Milivojević and Jovanović |url=https://n1info.rs/vesti/u-postanskim-sanducicima-leci-portiv-srdjana-milivojevica-i-aleksandra-jovanovica/ |access-date=22 October 2023 |website=[[N1 (TV channel)|N1]] |language=sr}}</ref> [[Pavle Grbović]], the president of PSG, was also featured on posters that depicted him as an [[Ustaša]].<ref>{{Cite web |date=22 October 2023 |title=Novo targetiranje lidera opozicije: Oblepljeno više od 200 plakata na Zvezdari |trans-title=New targeting of opposition leaders: More than 200 posters pasted on Zvezdara |url=https://nova.rs/vesti/politika/novo-targetiranje-lidera-opozicije-oblepljeno-vise-od-200-plakata-na-zvezdari-foto/ |access-date=23 October 2023 |website=[[NOVA portal]] |language=sr}}</ref> The posters that featured Grbović were promoted by [[Đorđe Dabić]], a SNS state secretary.<ref name=":210" /> Aleksić accused Vučić of being behind these ideas, while Grbović filed complaints about the posters.<ref>{{Cite web |date=19 October 2023 |title=Aleksić o uvredljivim flajerima: Vučić reciklira stare laži o meni iz straha od gubitka vlasti |trans-title=Aleksić on the offensive flyers: Vučić recycles old lies about me for fear of losing power |url=https://www.danas.rs/vesti/politika/miroslav-aleksic-uvredljivi-flajeri-aleksandar-vucic-reciklira-lazi/ |access-date=22 October 2023 |website=[[Danas (newspaper)|Danas]] |language=sr}}</ref><ref>{{Cite web |date=28 October 2023 |title=Grbović (PSG) podneo prijave zbog plakata na kojima je prikazan u ustaškoj uniformi |trans-title=Grbović (PSG) filed complaints because of posters showing him in Ustaša uniform |url=https://beta.rs/content/193149-grbovic-psg-podneo-prijave-zbog-plakata-na-kojima-je-prikazan-u-ustaskoj-uniformi |access-date=29 October 2023 |website=[[Novinska agencija Beta]] |language=sr}}</ref> [[Janko Veselinović (lawyer)|Janko Veselinović]], the leader of the [[Movement for Reversal]], was physically assaulted in Novi Sad on 12 November by a director of the public greenery company.<ref>{{Cite web |date=12 November 2023 |title=Veselinović: Fizički me napao direktor Gradskog zelenila u Novom Sadu |trans-title=Veselinović: I was physically attacked by the director of City Greenery in Novi Sad |url=https://n1info.rs/vesti/janko-veselinovic-fizicki-me-napao-direktor-zelenila-iz-novog-sada-tokom-kampanje/ |access-date=17 November 2023 |website=[[N1 (TV channel)|N1]] |language=sr}}</ref> Attacks on SSP offices on [[Zvezdara]], a Belgrade municipality, were conducted on 16 November.<ref>{{Cite web |date=16 November 2023 |title=Radikalske metode: Nalepnice "Tajkun Đilas" i grafiti "Đilas lopov" osvanuli na prostorijama SSP-a |trans-title=Radical methods: "Tycon Đilas" stickers and "Đilas the thief" graffiti appeared on the premises of the SSP |url=https://www.danas.rs/vesti/politika/izbori-2023/ssp-uvredljivi-grafiti-djilas/ |access-date=16 November 2023 |website=[[Danas (newspaper)|Danas]] |language=sr}}</ref>

SPN campaigned on returning "stolen pensions" (''otete penzije''), the pensions that were lowered by Vučić's government in 2014, and on environmental issues.<ref>{{Cite web |date=13 November 2023 |title=Grbović: Vratićemo penzionerima otete penzije |trans-title=Grbović: We will give back pensioners the pensions that were stolen from them |url=https://n1info.rs/vesti/izbori-2023/grbovic-vraticemo-penzionerima-otete-penzije/ |access-date=13 November 2023 |website=[[N1 (TV channel)|N1]] |language=sr}}</ref><ref name=":35">{{Cite web |date=16 November 2023 |title=Ćuta: Zaustavićemo pljačku države i vratiti otete penzije |trans-title=Ćuta: We will stop the looting of the state and return stolen pensions |url=https://n1info.rs/vesti/izbori-2023/cuta-zaustavicemo-pljacku-drzave-i-vratiti-otete-penzije/ |access-date=16 November 2023 |website=[[N1 (TV channel)|N1]] |language=sr}}</ref> Ćuta highlighted the issue of poverty and hunger.<ref name=":35" /> Lazović also said that SPN supported removing national broadcast frequency status for [[Nacionalna Televizija Happy|Happy]] and [[Pink (Serbia)|Pink]] television channels, lowering the inflation and prices, and investing in [[Universal health care|universal health care protection]].<ref name=":63">{{Cite web |last1=Jelovac |first1=Jelena |last2=Savić |first2=Danilo |date=16 November 2023 |title=Ovo je prvih 5 poteza koje bi opozicija povukla posle rušenja SNS sa vlasti |trans-title=These are the first 5 moves that the opposition would make after the overthrow of the SNS from power |url=https://nova.rs/vesti/politika/ovo-je-prvih-5-poteza-koje-bi-opozicija-povukla-posle-rusenja-sns-sa-vlasti/ |access-date=16 November 2023 |website=[[NOVA portal]] |language=sr}}</ref> Aleksić added that SPN would introduce [[progressive taxation]], while Đilas said that SPN would also increase salaries and invest in education.<ref name=":63" /><ref name=":55">{{Cite web |date=30 October 2023 |title=Povećanje plata u zdravstvu i prosveti, vraćanje penzija...: Đilas predstavio šta je plan SSP ako opozicija sruši |website=[[NOVA portal]] |language=sr}}</ref> Attended by several thousand supporters, SPN held its last campaign convention on 12 December in Belgrade.<ref>{{Cite web |last=Nešić |first=Nenad |date=12 December 2023 |title="Pobedićemo parizer dahije, u nedelju uzimamo sudbinu u ruke": Veliki miting opozicije u Beogradu |trans-title="We will defeat the Baloney dahias, on Sunday we will take our fate into our hands": Big meeting of the opposition in Belgrade |url=https://n1info.rs/vesti/izbori-2023/veliki-miting-opozicije-u-beogradu-obratice-se-11-lidera-planirana-i-setnja-do-rik/ |access-date=12 December 2023 |website=[[N1 (TV channel)|N1]] |language=sr}}</ref>

==== National Democratic Alternative ====
NADA began its official campaign on 28 October, listing corruption, nepotism, party employment, and rejecting Ohrid Agreement as one of its main issues for the election.<ref>{{Cite web |date=28 October 2023 |title=Koalicija NADA počela predizbornu kampanju: Borba protiv korupcije i nepotizma prioriteti |trans-title=Coalition NADA started election campaign: Fight against corruption and nepotism as priorities |url=https://beta.rs/content/193135-koalicija-nada-pocela-predizbornu-kampanju-borba-protiv-korupcije-i-nepotizma-prioriteti |access-date=29 October 2023 |website=[[Novinska agencija Beta]] |language=sr}}</ref> NADA submitted its list to RIK on 6 November and RIK confirmed it a day later.<ref name=":32" /><ref name="RIK_NADA" /> Shortly before the beginning of the official campaign period, Jovanović was featured on propaganda posters in October 2023, falsely depicting him as someone who released incumbent prime minister of Kosovo, Albin Kurti, from prison in 2001.<ref name=":210" /> Several NADA billboard posters were later torn down on 21 November; NADA accused the government of being behind the acts.<ref>{{Cite web |date=21 November 2023 |title=Koalicija NADA: Vlast uništava naše bilborde |trans-title=NADA coalition: The government is destroying our billboards |url=https://n1info.rs/vesti/izbori-2023/koalicija-nada-vlast-unistava-nase-bilborde/ |access-date=21 November 2023 |website=[[N1 (TV channel)|N1]] |language=sr}}</ref>

During the campaign period, Jovanović intensified his criticism of SNS while declining to criticise pro-European parties.<ref name=":110">{{Cite web |date=17 October 2023 |title=Miloš Jovanović objasnio zašto ne napada proevropsku opoziciju |trans-title=Miloš Jovanović explained why he does not attack the pro-European opposition |url=https://www.danas.rs/vesti/politika/jovanovic-novi-dss-napadi-opozicija/ |access-date=22 October 2023 |website=[[Danas (newspaper)|Danas]] |language=sr}}</ref> He has also called for greater cooperation between opposition parties to topple SNS from power.<ref>{{Cite web |date=22 November 2023 |title=Jovanović (Novi DSS): Saradnja cele opozicije jedini način da dođe do smene Vučićevog režima |trans-title=Jovanović (New DSS): Cooperation of the entire opposition is the only way to change the Vučić regime |url=https://www.danas.rs/vesti/politika/izbori-2023/jovanovic-novi-dss-saradnja-cele-opozicije-jedini-nacin-da-dodje-do-smene-vucicevog-rezima/ |access-date=23 November 2023 |website=[[Danas (newspaper)|Danas]] |language=sr}}</ref> Jovanović has called for electoral reform, pledging to "destroy the [[partocracy]] that SNS created" (''akaradna partijska država koju je stvorio SNS'').<ref name=":110" /> NADA supported the re-introduction of the [[First-past-the-post voting|first-past-the-post system]], and campaigned on further [[Regionalism (politics)|regionalisation]] and decentralisation of Serbia and giving cities and municipalities more power in regards to infrastructure and economy.<ref>{{Cite web |date=10 November 2023 |title=Jovanović: Koalicija NADA se zalaže za većinski izborni sistem |trans-title=Jovanović: The NADA coalition stands for a majoritarian electoral system |url=https://n1info.rs/vesti/izbori-2023/jovanovic-koalicija-nada-se-zalaze-za-vecinski-izborni-sistem/ |access-date=10 November 2023 |website=[[N1 (TV channel)|N1]] |language=sr}}</ref><ref>{{Cite web |date=12 November 2023 |title=Miloš Jovanović: Vratiti odgovornost u lokalne samouprave |trans-title=Miloš Jovanović: Return responsibility to local governments |url=https://www.danas.rs/vesti/politika/izbori-2023/milos-jovanovic-vratiti-odgovornost-u-lokalne-samouprave/ |access-date=13 November 2023 |website=[[Danas (newspaper)|Danas]] |language=sr}}</ref> NADA also called for the reform of healthcare and agriculture.<ref>{{Cite web |date=14 November 2023 |title=Koalicija NADA: Poljoprivreda da bude strateška grana privrede |trans-title=Coalition NADA: Agriculture must be a strategic branch of the economy |url=https://n1info.rs/vesti/izbori-2023/koalicija-nada-poljoprivreda-da-bude-strateska-grana-privrede/ |access-date=15 November 2023 |website=[[N1 (TV channel)|N1]] |language=sr}}</ref><ref>{{Cite web |date=18 November 2023 |title=NADA: Neophodne ozbiljne reforme u društvu, naročito zdravstvu |trans-title=NADA: Necessary serious reforms in society, especially health care |url=https://www.rtv.rs/sr_lat/izbori-2023/parlamentarni-izbori/nada-neophodne-ozbiljne-reforme-u-drustvu-narocito-zdravstvu_1494477.html |access-date=19 November 2023 |website=[[Radio Television of Vojvodina]] |language=sr}}</ref> Vojislav Mihailović of POKS also called for the restoration of the monarchy, saying that "Serbia should be a constitutional, parliamentary monarchy like organised European countries" (''da li Srbija treba da bude ustavna, parlamenta kraljevina poput uređenih evropskih zemlje'').<ref>{{Cite web |date=23 November 2023 |title=NADA: Otvoriti pitanje oblika vladavine i državnog uređenja |trans-title=NADA: To open the question of the form of government and state organisation |url=https://www.rtv.rs/sr_lat/izbori-2023/parlamentarni-izbori/nada-otvoriti-pitanje-oblika-vladavine-i-drzavnog-uredjenja_1495824.html |access-date=23 November 2023 |website=[[Radio Television of Vojvodina]] |language=sr}}</ref>

Regarding foreign policy, NADA campaigned on wanting "the best possible cooperation with the European Union" (''najbolju moguću saradnju sa Evropskom unijom'') in regards to trade, economy, and culture. It has, however, expressed its opposition to Serbia joining the European Union if "the condition set for Serbia is to recognise the secession of Kosovo" (''ako je za to uslov priznanje nezavisnosti Kosova'').<ref name=":40">{{Cite web |date=22 November 2023 |title=Koalicija NADA: EU važan partner, ali ne zalažemo se za članstvo ako je uslov priznanje nezavisnosti Kosova |trans-title=Coalition NADA: EU is an important partner, but we do not stand for membership if the condition is recognition of Kosovo's independence |url=https://n1info.rs/vesti/izbori-2023/koalicija-nada-eu-vazan-partner-ali-ne-zalazemo-se-za-clanstvo-ako-je-uslov-priznanje-nezavisnosti-kosova/ |access-date=23 November 2023 |website=[[N1 (TV channel)|N1]] |language=sr}}</ref> NADA held its last campaign convention on 10 December.<ref>{{Cite web |last=Savatović |first=Mladen |date=10 December 2023 |title=Završna konvencija koalicije NADA – uz "Marš na Drinu", ali i suze |trans-title=The final convention of the NADA coalition – with "March on the Drina", but also tears |url=https://n1info.rs/vesti/izbori-2023/koalicija-nada-u-beogradu-mi-smo-jedina-nacionalna-demokratska-alternativa-aktuelnom-rezimu/ |access-date=11 December 2023 |website=[[N1 (TV channel)|N1]] |language=sr}}</ref>

==== National Gathering ====
[[File:Milica Đurđević Stamenkovski and Boško Obradović at RIK, 4 November 2023.png|thumb|alt=Milica Đurđević Stamenkovski, Boško Obradović, and ten other Dveri and SSZ politicians giving a press conference at the Republic Electoral Commission on 4 November 2023|The SSZ–Dveri coalition campaigned on forging closer relations with [[BRICS]], instead of the European Union, and opposing the implementation of the [[Ohrid Agreement (2023)|Ohrid Agreement]]]]
SSZ and Dveri, the members of the NO coalition, signed another cooperation agreement on 1 November, announcing that they would officially contest the elections together. Obradović named preserving traditional values and Kosovo as part of Serbia, supporting Republika Srpska, Serbs in neighbouring regions, and [[Eco-nationalism|ecological patriotism]] as one of their main issues.<ref name=":31">{{Cite web |date=1 November 2023 |title=Zavetnici i Dveri potpisali koalicioni sporazum – zajednički nastupaju na izborima |trans-title=Oathkeepers and Dveri signed a coalition agreement – they participate in the elections together |url=https://n1info.rs/vesti/izbori-2023/zavetnici-i-dveri-potpisali-koalicioni-sporazum-zajednicki-nastupaju-na-izborima/ |access-date=2 November 2023 |website=[[N1 (TV channel)|N1]] |language=sr}}</ref> The coalition submitted its list on 4 November and it was accepted by RIK a day later.<ref name="NO_RIK" /><ref>{{Cite web |date=4 November 2023 |title=Zavetnici i Dveri predali izbornu listu – "Nacionalno okupljanje – državotvorna snaga"- za parlamentarne izbore |trans-title=Oathkeepers and Dveri handed over the electoral list – "National Gathering – State-Building Force" – for the parliamentary elections |url=https://www.rtv.rs/sr_lat/izbori-2023/parlamentarni-izbori/zavetnici-i-dveri-predali-izbornu-listu-nacionalno-okupljanje-drzavotvorna-snaga-za-parlamentarne-izbore_1490603.html |access-date=4 November 2023 |website=[[Radio Television of Vojvodina]] |language=sr}}</ref> At a press conference after they presented their electoral list, Đurđević Stamenkovski emphasised their opposition to the Ohrid Agreement and the European Union.<ref>{{Cite web |date=4 November 2023 |title='Nacionalno okupljanje' Dveri i Zavetnika predalo potpise RIK-u |trans-title='National Gathering' of Dveri and Oathkeepers delivered their signatures to RIK |url=https://beta.rs/content/193597-nacionalno-okupljanje-dveri-i-zavetnika-predalo-potpise-rik-u |access-date=6 November 2023 |website=[[Novinska agencija Beta]] |language=sr}}</ref> The far-right [[Alternative for Germany]] party, the Chetnik Ravna Gora Movement, and the clerical-fascist [[Obraz (organization)|Obraz]] organisation of Mladen Obradović, voiced their support for the SSZ–Dveri coalition.<ref name=":232">{{Cite web |date=17 November 2023 |title=Đurđević Stamenkovski: Mi želimo Evropu u kojoj će Srbija imati svoje mesto |trans-title=Đurđević Stamenkovski: We want a Europe in which Serbia will have its place |url=https://www.tanjug.rs/izbori-2023/vesti/59918/durdevic-stamenkovski-mi-zelimo-evropu-u-kojoj-ce-srbija-imati-svoje-mesto/vest |access-date=17 November 2023 |website=[[Tačno d.o.o.|Tanjug]] |language=sr}}</ref><ref>{{Cite web |date=20 November 2023 |title=Dveri i Ravnogorski pokret potpisali Sporazum o saradnji: "Plod višegodišnje uzajamne podrške" |trans-title=Dveri and the Ravna Gora movement signed a cooperation agreement: "The fruit of many years of mutual support" |url=https://n1info.rs/vesti/izbori-2023/dveri-i-ravnogorski-pokret-potpisali-sporazum-o-saradnji-plod-visegodisnje-uzajamne-podrske/ |access-date=20 November 2023 |website=[[N1 (TV channel)|N1]] |language=sr}}</ref><ref>{{Cite web |last=Radovanović |first=Vojin |date=24 November 2023 |title=Boško Obradović predstavio novu podršku "Nacionalnom okupljanju": Među njima Mladen Obradović i borci protiv obavezne vakcinacije |trans-title=Boško Obradović presented new support for the "National Gathering": Among them Mladen Obradović and fighters against mandatory vaccination |url=https://www.danas.rs/vesti/politika/izbori-2023/obradovic-izbori-koalicija/ |access-date=24 November 2023 |website=[[Danas (newspaper)|Danas]] |language=sr}}</ref>

During the campaign period, the SSZ–Dveri coalition representatives emphasised their support for greater incentives for domestic businessmen and farmers,<ref>{{Cite web |date=7 November 2023 |title=Boško Obradović: Povećati podsticaje za domaće privrednike i poljoprivrednike |trans-title=Boško Obradović: Increase incentives for domestic businessmen and farmers |url=https://www.rtv.rs/sr_lat/izbori-2023/parlamentarni-izbori/bosko-obradovic-povecati-podsticaje-za-domace-privrednike-i-poljoprivrednike_1491303.html |access-date=7 November 2023 |website=[[Radio Television of Vojvodina]] |language=sr}}</ref> the construction of student dormitories in Belgrade, Novi Sad, Niš and Kragujevac, giving free school books, and financial aid for "socially vulnerable families" (''socijalno ugrožene porodice'').<ref>{{Cite web |date=17 November 2023 |title=Dveri: Izgraditi bar po jedan novi studentski dom u Beogradu, Novom Sadu, Nišu i Kragujevcu |trans-title=Dveri: Construct at least one new student dormitory in Belgrade, Novi Sad, Niš, and Kragujevac |url=https://beta.rs/content/194445-dveri-izgraditi-bar-po-jedan-novi-studentski-dom-u-beogradu-novom-sadu-nisu-i-ragujevcu |access-date=17 November 2023 |website=[[Novinska agencija Beta]] |language=sr}}</ref><ref>{{Cite web |date=18 November 2023 |title=Obradović: Besplatni udžbenici za sve đake u Srbiji i novčana pomoć za ugrožene |trans-title=Obradović: Free textbooks for all students in Serbia and financial aid for the vulnerable |url=https://www.rtv.rs/sr_lat/izbori-2023/parlamentarni-izbori/obradovic-besplatni-udzbenici-za-sve-djake-u-srbiji-i-novcana-pomoc-za-ugrozene_1494475.html |access-date=18 November 2023 |website=[[Radio Television of Vojvodina]] |language=sr}}</ref> [[Ratko Ristić]], one of the representatives of the NO coalition, also said that one of their main issues is to "return Serbia's sovereignty, especially economic sovereignty" (''povratak suverenizma Srbije, posebno ekonomskog'') and that they would "pay special attention to the development of Serbian agriculture and the position of Serbian farmers" (''posebnu pažnju ćemo obratiti na razvoj srpske poljoprivrede i položaj srpskog seljaka'').<ref>{{Cite web |date=10 November 2023 |title=Ristić: Vratiti Srbiji ekonomski suverenizam |trans-title=Ristić: Serbia should get its economic sovereignty back |url=https://n1info.rs/vesti/izbori-2023/ristic-vratiti-srbiji-ekonomski-suverenizam/ |access-date=10 November 2023 |website=[[N1 (TV channel)|N1]] |language=sr}}</ref> Đurđević Stamenkovski also said that she wants Serbia to return "the proven traditional values in the education system".<ref>{{Cite web |date=21 November 2023 |title=Đurđević Stamenkovski: Potrebna hitna reforma prosvete |trans-title=Đurđević Stamenkovski: Urgent education reform is needed |url=https://www.rtv.rs/sr_lat/izbori-2023/parlamentarni-izbori/djurdjevic-stamenkovski-potrebna-hitna-reforma-prosvete_1495307.html |access-date=21 November 2023 |website=[[Radio Television of Vojvodina]] |language=sr}}</ref> Obradović alleged that the SSZ–Dveri coalition was a target of attacks and media censorship.<ref>{{Cite web |date=16 November 2023 |title=Dveri: Vlast zabranjuje Nacionalno okupljanje |trans-title=Dveri: The government is forbidding National Gathering |url=https://n1info.rs/vesti/izbori-2023/dveri-vlast-zabranjuje-nacionalno-okupljanje/ |access-date=16 November 2023 |website=[[N1 (TV channel)|N1]] |language=sr |last1=Beograd |first1=N1 }}</ref>

On foreign policy, the coalition expressed their support for retaining close relations with China, due to their positions towards Kosovo,<ref>{{Cite web |last=Čolić |first=Leposava |date=7 November 2023 |title=Podrška Kine Srbiji |trans-title=China's support to Serbia |url=http://fonet.rs/izbori-2023/36387726/podrska-kine-srbiji.html |access-date=8 November 2023 |website=FoNet portal |language=sr}}</ref> and that they would want Serbia to become a member of [[BRICS]] instead of the European Union.<ref>{{Cite web |date=14 November 2023 |title=Đurđević Stamenkovski: Evropska unija ima alternativu, a to je BRIKS |trans-title=Đurđević Stamenkovski: The European Union has an alternative, and that is BRICS |url=https://n1info.rs/vesti/izbori-2023/djurdjevic-stamenkovski-evropska-unija-ima-alternativu-a-to-je-briks/ |access-date=15 November 2023 |website=[[N1 (TV channel)|N1]] |language=sr}}</ref> Obradović alleged that regions such as [[Sandžak]], [[Vojvodina]], and parts of eastern Serbia would separate from Serbia if "Serbia gives up on Kosovo" (''ako se odrekne Kosova'').<ref>{{Cite web |date=16 November 2023 |title=Obradović: Srbija će ostati bez drugih delova teritorije ako se odrekne Kosova |trans-title=Obradović: Serbia will be left without other parts of the territory if it renounces Kosovo |url=https://n1info.rs/vesti/izbori-2023/obradovic-srbija-ce-ostati-bez-drugih-delova-teritorije-ako-se-odrekne-kosova/ |access-date=16 November 2023 |website=[[N1 (TV channel)|N1]] |language=sr}}</ref> Đurđević Stamenkovski, in an Insajder interview, did not reject cooperating with SNS after the elections if SNS rejects the Ohrid Agreement.<ref>{{Cite web |date=15 November 2023 |title=Đurđević: Postizborna saradnja moguća sa svima koji prihvate politiku Zavetnika o Kosovu |trans-title=Đurđević: Post-election cooperation is possible with everyone who accepts the policy of the Oathkeepers on Kosovo |url=https://www.danas.rs/vesti/politika/izbori-2023/djurdjevic-postizborna-saradnja-moguca-sa-svima-koji-prihvate-politiku-zavetnika-o-kosovu/ |access-date=16 November 2023 |website=[[Danas (newspaper)|Danas]] |language=sr}}</ref> NO held its last campaign convention on 10 December.<ref>{{Cite web |date=10 December 2023 |title=Održana Završna konvencija koalicije okupljene oko liste Nacionalnog okupljanja |trans-title=The final convention of the coalition gathered around the list of the National Gathering was held |url=https://www.tanjug.rs/izbori-2023/vesti/63835/odrzana-zavrsna-konvencija-koalicije-okupljene-oko-liste-nacionalnog-okupljanja/vest |access-date=11 December 2023 |website=[[Tačno d.o.o.|Tanjug]] |language=sr}}</ref>

==== Serbian Radical Party ====
SRS presented its electoral list to RIK on 3 November RIK confirmed it a day later.<ref>{{Cite web |date=3 November 2023 |title=Šešelj: SRS predala izbornu listu sa nešto više od 11.000 potpisa građana |trans-title=Šešelj: SRS handed over its electoral list to RIK with more than 11,000 signatures from citizens |url=https://www.danas.rs/vesti/politika/izbori-2023/seselj-srs-predala-izbornu-listu-sa-nesto-vise-od-11-000-potpisa-gradjana/ |access-date=6 November 2023 |website=[[Danas (newspaper)|Danas]] |language=sr}}</ref><ref>{{Cite web |date=4 November 2023 |title=Proglašena izborna lista "Dr Vojislav Šešelj – Srpska radikalna stranka'' |trans-title=Electoral list "Dr Vojislav Šešelj – Serbian Radical Party" has been proclaimed |url=https://www.euronews.rs/srbija/politika/104099/proglasena-izborna-lista-dr-vojislav-seselj-srpska-radikalna-stranka/vest |access-date=6 November 2023 |website=[[Euronews]] |language=sr}}</ref> SRS campaigned on issues such as health care reform, saying that Serbia should "use the experiences of foreign, Western European countries, as well as the USA, which has a more developed health system" (''da koristimo iskustva stranih, zapadnoevropskih zemalja, kao i SAD koje imaju razvijeniji zdravstveni sistem''),<ref>{{Cite web |date=8 November 2023 |title=Ristić (SRS) o zdravstvu: Da svako ko se razboli ima svog lekara na raspolaganju 24 sata dnevno |trans-title=Ristić (SRS) on healthcare: Everyone who gets sick should have a doctor available 24 hours a day |url=https://beta.rs/content/193808-ristic-srs-o-zdravstvu-da-svako-ko-se-razboli-ima-svog-lekara-na-raspolaganju-24-sata-dnevno |access-date=8 November 2023 |website=[[Novinska agencija Beta]] |language=sr}}</ref> advocating greater investments for domestic companies, and preventing bullying by creating "teams of parents, educators, and local municipal officers" (''timski rad roditelja dece, prosvetnih radnika i lokalne zajednice'').<ref>{{Cite web |date=9 November 2023 |title=A. Šešelj: SRS se zalaže za ulaganje u domaću privredu i članstvo u BRIKS-u |trans-title=A. Šešelj: SRS stands for investment in the domestic economy and membership in BRICS |url=https://beta.rs/content/193910-a-seselj-srs-se-zalaze-za-ulaganje-u-domacu-privredu-i-clanstvo-u-briks-u |access-date=9 November 2023 |website=[[Novinska agencija Beta]] |language=sr}}</ref><ref>{{Cite web |date=11 November 2023 |title=SRS: Vršnjačko nasilje suzbiti pedagoškim merama prevencije |trans-title=SRS: Suppress peer violence with pedagogical prevention measures |url=https://beta.rs/content/194023-srs-vrsnjacko-nasilje-suzbiti-pedagoskim-merama-prevencije |access-date=11 November 2023 |website=[[Novinska agencija Beta]] |language=sr}}</ref> [[Aleksandar Šešelj]] also said that SRS supported a ban on non-governmental organisations that support the recognition of Kosovo.<ref>{{Cite web |date=21 November 2023 |title=Aleksandar Šešelj: Zabranićemo sve nevladine organizacije koje promovišu nezavisno Kosovo |trans-title=Aleksandar Šešelj: We will ban all non-governmental organisations that promote an independent Kosovo |url=https://www.tanjug.rs/izbori-2023/vesti/60538/aleksandar-seselj-zabranicemo-sve-nevladine-organizacije-koje-promovisu-nezavisno-kosovo/vest |access-date=21 November 2023 |website=[[Tačno d.o.o.|Tanjug]] |language=sr}}</ref>

In an interview for [[Radio Television of Vojvodina]], Aleksandar Šešelj said that SRS would not join a pro-European government in case if SRS crosses the electoral threshold.<ref>{{Cite web |date=13 November 2023 |title=Šešelj: Ne bismo mogli da učestvujemo u vladi koja je proevropska |trans-title=Šešelj: We would not be able to participate in a pro-European government |url=https://www.rtv.rs/sr_lat/izbori-2023/parlamentarni-izbori/seselj-ne-bismo-mogli-da-ucestvujemo-u-vladi-koja-je-proevropska_1493001.html |access-date=15 November 2023 |website=[[Radio Television of Vojvodina]] |language=sr}}</ref> SRS has called for the abandonment of the process of accession of Serbia to the European Union and instead called on forging closer ties with Russia and becoming an applicant member of BRICS.<ref>{{Cite web |date=5 November 2023 |title=Srpska radikalna stranka: Srbija nije postigla rezultate u nacionalnom interesu na evropskom putu |trans-title=Serbian Radical Party: Serbia has not achieved results in the national interest on the European road |url=https://beta.rs/content/193631-srpska-radikalna-stranka-srbija-nije-postigla-rezultate-u-nacionalnom-interesu-na-evropskom-putu |access-date=6 November 2023 |website=[[Novinska agencija Beta]] |language=sr}}</ref> Vojislav Šešelj also met with the Palestinian ambassador in Serbia during the campaign; Vojislav Šešelj also criticised Israel, describing their actions towards [[State of Palestine|Palestine]] as [[Palestinian genocide accusation|genocidal]].<ref>{{Cite web |date=16 November 2023 |title=Poseta palestinskog ambasadora |trans-title=Visit of the Palestinian ambassador |url=http://fonet.rs/izbori-2023/36392140/poseta-palestinskog-ambasadora-.html |access-date=16 November 2023 |website=FoNet portal |language=sr}}</ref><ref>{{Cite web |date=16 November 2023 |title=Šešelj: Izrael uz podršku SAD sprovodi genocid nad Palestincima |trans-title=Šešelj: Israel with the support of the USA is carrying out genocide against the Palestinians |url=https://beta.rs/content/194384-seselj-izrael-uz-podrsku-sad-sprovodi-genocid-nad-palestincima |access-date=16 November 2023 |website=[[Novinska agencija Beta]] |language=sr}}</ref>

==== Alliance of Vojvodina Hungarians ====
VMSZ, led by acting president [[Bálint Pásztor]], submitted its list to RIK on 7 November. At a press conference after submitting the list, Pásztor said that VMSZ collected 11,355 signatures, more than twice the amount needed for minority parties, and that they would campaign on issues they listed in their electoral programme.<ref name="VMSZ_slogan" /> RIK confirmed their list on 8 November.<ref name="RIK_VMSZ"/> Pásztor expressed his support for continuing the cooperation between VMSZ and SNS.<ref>{{Cite web |date=14 November 2023 |title=Pastor: Savez vojvođanskih Mađara za nastavak saradnje sa SNS |trans-title=Pastor: Alliance of Vojvodina Hungarians for continued cooperation with SNS |url=https://www.rtv.rs/sr_lat/izbori-2023/parlamentarni-izbori/pastor-savez-vojvodjanskih-madjara-za-nastavak-saradnje-sa-sns_1493319.html |access-date=15 November 2023 |website=[[Radio Television of Vojvodina]] |language=sr}}</ref> VMSZ received support from the [[Democratic Party of Vojvodina Hungarians]] and Party of Hungarian Unity in late November.<ref>{{Cite web |date=22 November 2023 |title=Savez vojvođanskih Mađara na izbore ide uz podršku DSVM-a i SMJ-a |trans-title=The Alliance of Vojvodina Hungarians is going to the elections with the support of DSVM and SMJ |url=https://n1info.rs/vesti/izbori-2023/savez-vojvodjanskih-madjara-na-izbore-ide-uz-podrsku-dsvm-a-i-smj-a/ |access-date=23 November 2023 |website=[[N1 (TV channel)|N1]] |language=sr}}</ref>

==== United for Justice ====
SPP and DSHV formalised an electoral alliance under the name United for Justice (UZP) on 4 November.<ref>{{Cite web |date=4 November 2023 |title=SPP na parlamentarnim izborima sa listom "Usame Zukorlić – Ujedinjeni za pravdu – SPP-DSHV" |trans-title=SPP in the parliamentary elections with the list "Usame Zukorlić – United for Justice – SPP-DSHV" |url=https://www.b92.net/info/izbori2023/vesti.php?nav_id=2427180 |access-date=9 November 2023 |website=[[B92]] |language=sr}}</ref> UZP submitted its list to RIK on 9 November, with Zukorlić stating that the coalition would advocate for proportional representation of national communities in public institutions and balanced regional development.<ref>{{Cite web |date=9 November 2023 |title=Stranka pravde i pomirenja i Demokratski savez Hrvata u Vojvodini predali listu RIK |trans-title=The Party of Justice and Reconciliation and the Democratic Alliance of Croats in Vojvodina submitted the list to the RIK |url=https://n1info.rs/vesti/izbori-2023/stranka-pravde-i-pomirenja-i-demokratski-savez-hrvata-u-vojvodini-predali-listu-rik/ |access-date=9 November 2023 |website=[[N1 (TV channel)|N1]] |language=sr}}</ref> Their electoral list was accepted by RIK on 10 November.<ref name="RIK_UZP"/> UZP members expressed their support for remaining in the next government, saying "that members of our communities supported this move" (''pripadnici naših zajednica to pozdavili'').<ref>{{Cite web |date=14 November 2023 |title=Zukorlić i Žigmanov o zajedničkoj listi: Sinergijom do snažnijeg glasa nevećinskih zajednica |trans-title=Zukorlić and Žigmanov on the joint list: Synergy to a stronger voice of non-majority communities |url=https://n1info.rs/vesti/izbori-2023/zukorlic-i-zigmanov-o-zajednickoj-listi-sinergijom-do-snaznijeg-glasa-nevecinskih-zajednica/ |access-date=15 November 2023 |website=[[N1 (TV channel)|N1]] |language=sr}}</ref> Zukorlić has described UZP as a pro-European coalition and that "he believes that one day Serbia will nevertheless join the NATO alliance" (''veruje da će jednog dana Srbija "ipak pristupiti i NATO alijansi"'').<ref>{{Cite web |date=21 November 2023 |title=Zukorlić: Doći će dan za pomirenje Beograda i Prištine na principima pravde |trans-title=Zukorlić: The day will come for the reconciliation of Belgrade and Priština on the principles of justice |url=https://n1info.rs/vesti/izbori-2023/zukorlic-doci-ce-dan-za-pomirenje-beograda-i-pristine-na-principima-pravde/ |access-date=21 November 2023 |website=[[N1 (TV channel)|N1]] |language=sr}}</ref> DSHV received support from [[Andrej Plenković]], the prime minister of Croatia and leader of the [[Croatian Democratic Union]].<ref>{{Cite web |last=Ilić |first=Velimir |date=12 December 2023 |title=Podrška Žigmanovu |trans-title=Support to Žigmanov |url=http://fonet.rs/izbori-2023/36404539/podrska-zigmanovu.html |access-date=12 December 2023 |website=FoNet portal |language=sr}}</ref>

==== Party of Democratic Action of Sandžak ====
SDAS of [[Sulejman Ugljanin]] submitted its electoral list to RIK on 16 November, with RIK confirming it on the same day.<ref name="RIK_SDAS"/><ref name=":34">{{Cite web |date=15 November 2023 |title=SDA Sandžaka predala listu za parlamentarne izbore |trans-title=SDA of Sandžak submitted its electoral list for parliamentary elections |url=https://n1info.rs/vesti/izbori-2023/sda-sandzaka-predala-listu-za-parlamentarne-izbore/ |access-date=15 November 2023 |website=[[N1 (TV channel)|N1]] |language=sr}}</ref> Its main representative and ballot holder, [[Selma Kučević]], emphasised that SDAS supports decentralisation and regionalism as well as "authentically representing the Bosniak people as well as other citizens of Sandžak" (''autentični predstavnici bošnjačkog naroda ali i svih ostalih građana Sandžaka'').<ref name=":34" /> Ugljanin said that SDAS supported anti-corruption measures and government transparency.<ref>{{Cite web |date=21 November 2023 |title=Ugljanin: Borba protiv korupcije, kroz jačanje institucija i pravnog sistema važni za našu stranku |trans-title=Ugljanin: The fight against corruption, through the strengthening of institutions and the legal system, is important for our party |url=https://www.euronews.rs/srbija/politika/105687/ugljanin-borba-protiv-korupcije-kroz-jacanje-institucija-i-pravnog-sistema-vazni-za-nasu-stranku/vest |access-date=21 November 2023 |website=[[Euronews]] |language=sr}}</ref>

==== Coalition for Peace and Tolerance ====
A group of ethnic minority parties and organisations, including [[Vlach National Party]] (VNS), [[Hungarian Civic Alliance (Serbia)|Hungarian Civic Alliance]] (MPSZ), and [[Democratic Party of Macedonians]], held a meeting in April 2023, with the intention being on forming a coalition, named [[Coalition for Peace and Tolerance]], for the upcoming parliamentary, provincial, and local elections.<ref>{{Cite web |last=Mihajlović Jovanović |first=Suzana |date=28 April 2023 |title=Formira se Koalicija za mir i toleranciju |trans-title=The Coalition for Peace and Tolerance is being formed |url=https://www.ngportal.rs/formira-se-koalicija-za-mir-i-toleranciju/ |access-date=18 November 2023 |website=NG Portal |language=sr}}</ref> Shortly after the meeting, [[Jahja Fehratović]] left SPP.<ref>{{Cite web |last=Novosel |first=Slađana |date=5 May 2023 |title=Najbliži saradnik Zukorlića, Jahja Fehratović napustio SPP |trans-title=The closest associate of Zukorlić, Jahja Fehratović, left SPP |url=https://www.danas.rs/vesti/politika/najblizi-saradnik-zukorlica-jahja-fehratovic-napustio-spp/ |access-date=18 November 2023 |website=[[Danas (newspaper)|Danas]] |language=sr}}</ref> Later in October, Fehratović announced the formation of his political party, the For the Future and Development (ZBR). Fehratović said that ZBR would support traditional values, spirituality, and rule of law.<ref name=":36">{{Cite web |date=30 October 2023 |title=Fehratović osniva Stranku budućnosti i razvoja |trans-title=Fehratović founds the Party of the Future and Development |url=https://infolid.rs/politika/fehratovic-osniva-stranku-buducnosti-i-razvoja/ |access-date=18 November 2023 |website=Infolid |language=sr}}</ref>

Following the dissolution of the National Assembly, Fehratović's ZBR formed a coalition, named "Together for the Future and Development –  Coalition for Peace and Development" (KZMT), with VNS, MPSZ, [[Democratic Union of Croats]], Bosniak Civic Party, Party of Montenegrins, Civic Party of Greeks of Serbia, Vojvodina Movement, Tolerance of Serbia, Union of Yugoslavs, Union of Female Roma Network and Non-Roma Network of Serbia, and Union of Banat Romanians. Fehratović was also announced as the coalition's ballot holder.<ref name=":37">{{Cite web |last=Spalović |first=Dejan |date=10 November 2023 |title=Formirana manjinska izborna lista "Zajedno za budućnost i razvoj – koalicija za mir i toleranciju" |trans-title=Formed minority electoral list "Together for the Future and Development – Coalition for Peace and Tolerance" |url=https://www.politika.rs/sr/clanak/583405/Formirana-manjinska-izborna-lista-Zajedno-za-buducnost-i-razvoj-koalicija-za-mir-i-toleranciju |access-date=18 November 2023 |website=[[Politika]] |language=sr}}</ref> KZMT submitted its electoral list on 17 November.<ref>{{Cite AV media |url=https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=1bhU9WHxgMk |title=17.11.2023. Изборна листа ЗАЈЕДНО ЗА БУДУЦНОСТ И РАЗВОЈ – КОАЛИЦИЈА ЗА МИР И ТОЛЕРАНЦИЈУ |date=17 November 2023 |type=Videotape |language=sr |publisher=[[Republic Electoral Commission]] |trans-title=17.11.2023. Electoral list TOGETHER FOR THE FUTURE AND DEVELOPMENT – COALITION FOR PEACE AND TOLERANCE |access-date=18 November 2023 |via=[[YouTube]]}}</ref> RIK rejected the list on 18 November, stating that out of 6,093 collected signatures, only 4,937 were valid, and that KZMT had to collect the remaining 63 signatures until 20 November.<ref>{{Cite web |date=18 November 2023 |title=RIK: Koaliciji za mir i toleranciju nedostaje 63 potpisa za proglašenje liste |trans-title=RIK: The Coalition for Peace and Tolerance lacks 63 signatures to announce the list |url=https://www.tanjug.rs/izbori-2023/vesti/60058/rik-koaliciji-za-mir-i-toleranciju-nedostaje-63-potpisa-za-proglasenje-liste/vest |access-date=18 November 2023 |website=[[Tačno d.o.o.|Tanjug]] |language=sr}}</ref> On the same day, KZMT collected 436 more valid signatures and RIK confirmed their electoral list.<ref name="RIK_KZMT"/>

==== People's Party ====
After collecting more than 12,500 signatures, Narodna submitted its electoral list to RIK on 19 November. At a press conference in the building of RIK, Jeremić said that Narodna would campaign on rejecting the Ohrid Agreement, prohibiting [[lithium mining]], as well as "bringing back sovereignty over the national economy" (''vraćanje suvereniteta nad nacionalnom ekonomijom'').<ref name=":38">{{Cite web |date=19 November 2023 |title=Narodna stranka predala izbornu listu RIK-u |trans-title=The People's Party presented its electoral list to RIK |url=https://www.rtv.rs/sr_lat/izbori-2023/parlamentarni-izbori/narodna-stranka-predala-izbornu-listu-rik-u_1494663.html |access-date=19 November 2023 |website=[[Radio Television of Vojvodina]] |language=sr}}</ref> RIK confirmed their electoral list on 20 November.<ref name="RIK_NARODNA"/>

Narodna also emphasised its support for introducing [[military conscription]] to retain military neutrality, retaining close relations with Russia, and opposing sanctions against Russia, the accession of Serbia to the European Union, and the recognition of Kosovo.<ref>{{Cite web |date=18 November 2023 |title=Jeremić: Srbija mora biti neutralna, to podrazumeva uvođenje vojnog roka |trans-title=Jeremić: Serbia must be neutral, that implies the introduction of military conscription |url=https://www.euronews.rs/srbija/politika/105417/jeremic-srbija-mora-biti-neutralna-to-podrazumeva-uvodenje-vojnog-roka/vest |access-date=19 November 2023 |website=[[Euronews]] |language=sr}}</ref> Jeremić has said that Serbia should seek membership in the [[European Economic Area]] instead.<ref>{{Cite web |date=14 November 2023 |title=Vuk Jeremić: Srbija ne bi ušla u EU ni kada bi priznala "Kosovo" |trans-title=Vuk Jeremić: Serbia would not join the EU even if it recognized "Kosovo" |url=https://www.danas.rs/vesti/politika/izbori-2023/vuk-jeremic-srbija-ne-bi-usla-u-eu-ni-kada-bi-priznala-kosovo/ |access-date=19 November 2023 |website=[[Danas (newspaper)|Danas]] |language=sr}}</ref>

==== DJB–SDS ====
Initially, SDS was supposed to take part in the SPN alliance while DJB announced that they would contest the elections independently.<ref>{{Cite web |date=2 November 2023 |title=Tadić: SDS spremna da bude deo liste 'Srbija protiv nasilja' uz minimum uslova |trans-title=Tadić: SDS is ready to be part of the list of 'Serbia Against Violence' with minimum conditions |url=https://beta.rs/content/193451-tadic-sds-spremna-da-bude-deo-liste-srbija-protiv-nasilja-uz-minimum-uslova |access-date=2 November 2023 |website=[[Novinska agencija Beta]] |language=sr}}</ref> SDS was ultimately declined to join SPN, and shortly after in early November, DJB successfully negotiated with SDS and Ana Pejić's Stolen Babies movement to form a joint electoral alliance, mainly centering their opposition to the Ohrid Agreement.<ref>{{Cite web |date=3 November 2023 |title=Tadić: Aleksić nas obavestio da na listi 'Srbija protiv nasilja' ipak nema mesta za SDS |trans-title=Tadić: Aleksić informed us that there is no place for SDS on the list of 'Serbia Against Violence' |url=https://beta.rs/content/193513-tadic-aleksic-nas-obavestio-da-na-listi-srbija-protiv-nasilja-ipak-nema-mesta-za-sds |access-date=3 November 2023 |website=[[Novinska agencija Beta]] |language=sr}}</ref><ref>{{Cite web |date=6 November 2023 |title=SDS, DJB i pokret "Otete bebe" izlaze zajedno na izbore |trans-title=SDS, DJB, and movement "Stolen Babies" are taking part in the elections together |url=https://n1info.rs/vesti/izbori-2023/sds-djb-i-pokret-otete-bebe-izlaze-zajedno-na-izbore/ |access-date=6 November 2023 |website=[[N1 (TV channel)|N1]] |language=sr}}</ref> The coalition, named Good Morning Serbia, submitted its electoral list to RIK on 22 November.<ref>{{Cite web |date=22 November 2023 |title=Koalicija Tadića i Radulovića predala potpise RIK-u |trans-title=The coalition of Tadić and Radulović submitted their signatures to the RIK |url=https://n1info.rs/vesti/izbori-2023/koalicija-tadica-i-radulovica-predala-potpise-rik-u/ |access-date=23 November 2023 |website=[[N1 (TV channel)|N1]] |language=sr}}</ref> They collected over 11,500 signatures of support.<ref>{{Cite web |date=22 November 2023 |title=Dosta je bilo, SDS i udruženje "Otete bebe" predali RIK-u listu |trans-title=Enough is Enough, SDS and the association "Stolen Babies" submitted their list to RIK |url=https://www.euronews.rs/srbija/politika/105843/dosta-je-bilo-sds-i-udruzenje-otete-bebe-predali-rik-u-listu/vest |access-date=23 November 2023 |website=[[Euronews]] |language=sr}}</ref> RIK confirmed their electoral list on 23 November, with 10,534 valid signatures.<ref name="RIK_DJS"/>

== Opinion polls ==
{{main|Opinion polling for the 2023 Serbian parliamentary election}}
[[Opinion polling]] for the 2023 parliamentary election in Serbia was conducted by various monitoring and research organisations such as Demostat, NSPM, Agency Faktor Plus, Šta Srbija misli?/New Third Way, Stata Agency, and CRTA.<ref>Multiple sources: {{bulleted list|{{cite web |date=29 June 2022 |title=Istraživanje Demostata: spoljno-političke orijentacije građana Srbije |trans-title=Demostat research: foreign policy orientations of Serbian citizens |url=https://demostat.rs/upload/Prezentacija%2029062022%20Demostat.pdf |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20220921052046/https://demostat.rs/upload/Prezentacija%2029062022%20Demostat.pdf |archive-date=21 September 2022 |access-date=10 January 2023 |publisher=Demostat |language=sr |page=22}}|{{cite web |date=27 July 2022 |title=Srbija, leto 2022. – protivljenje uvođenju sankcija Rusiji porsalo sa 82,2 na 84 odsto. Članstvo srbije u NATO podržava 4,3 odsto, a protivi mu se 88,1 odsto |trans-title=Serbia, summer 2022 – opposition to the introduction of sanctions against Russia increased from 82.2 to 84 percent. Serbia's membership in NATO is supported by 4.3 percent, while 88.1 percent oppose it |url=http://www.nspm.rs/istrazivanja-javnog-mnjenja/srbija-leto-2022.-protivljenje-uvodjenju-sankcija-rusiji-poraslo-sa-822-na-84-odsto.html |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20221108050501/http://www.nspm.rs/istrazivanja-javnog-mnjenja/srbija-leto-2022.-protivljenje-uvodjenju-sankcija-rusiji-poraslo-sa-822-na-84-odsto.html |archive-date=8 November 2022 |access-date=10 January 2023 |publisher=[[Nova srpska politička misao]] |language=sr}}|{{cite web |date=25 October 2022 |title=SNS na 46,3 odsto, desnica u porastu: najnovije istraživanje "Faktor plusa" pokazalo i ovo: Neko treba da popuni prazninu nastalu u "proevropskoj" opoziciji! |trans-title=SNS at 46.3 percent, the right on the rise: the latest "Faktor Plus" opinion poll also showed this: Someone needs to fill the gap created in the "pro-European" opposition! |url=https://www.blic.rs/vesti/politika/sns-na-463-odsto-desnica-u-porastu-najnovije-istrazivanje-faktor-plusa-pokazalo-i-ovo/cpgpg4t |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20221106042406/https://www.blic.rs/vesti/politika/sns-na-463-odsto-desnica-u-porastu-najnovije-istrazivanje-faktor-plusa-pokazalo-i-ovo/cpgpg4t |archive-date=6 November 2022 |access-date=10 January 2023 |website=[[Blic]] |language=sr}}|{{cite web |title=Međunarodna politička situacija i javno mnjenje u Srbiji |trans-title=International political situation and public opinion in Serbia |url=https://istrazivanja.rs/medjunarodna-politicka-situacija-i-javno-mnjenje-u-srbiji/ |publisher=Šta Srbija misli? |access-date=22 February 2023 |language=sr |date=22 February 2023 |archive-date=22 February 2023 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20230222175343/https://istrazivanja.rs/medjunarodna-politicka-situacija-i-javno-mnjenje-u-srbiji/ |url-status=live }}|{{cite web |title=Istraživanje javnog mnjenja: Koliko bi građana glasalo za vlast, koliko za organizatore protests |trans-title=Public opinion poll: How many citizens would vote for the government, how many for the protest organisers |url=https://n1info.rs/vesti/istrazivanje-javnog-mnjenja-koliko-bi-gradjana-glasalo-za-vlast-koliko-za-organizatore-protesta/ |publisher=[[N1 (TV channel)|N1]] |access-date=19 September 2023 |language=sr |date=19 September 2023}}|{{Cite web |date=16 October 2023 |title=Stavovi građana Srbije i Beograda |trans-title=Stances of citizens of Serbia and Belgrade |url=https://crta.rs/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/CRTA-Istrazivanje-javnog-menjenja-Spetembar-2023.pdf |access-date=16 October 2023 |website=CRTA |pages=2, 9 |language=sr}}}}</ref> Stata Agency has also published scenario polls, featuring a SNS–SPS alliance, the Serbia Against Violence (SPN) coalition, and the "state-building opposition" before the official creation of SPN; Vukadinović of NSPM criticised Stata's scenario polls, saying that the coalition "Serbia Against Violence is not exactly a fiction, then, for now, only a projection and, possibly, the desire of some media and political factors. It is difficult to compare something that actually exists with something that could possibly be" (''Srbija protiv nasilja ako ne baš fikcija, onda, za sada, samo projekcija i, eventualno, želja nekih medijskih i političkih faktora. Teško je porediti nešto što realno postoji sa nečim što bi, eventualno, tek moglo biti''). Anđelković also said that "public's pulse is very fluid when the elections are still relatively far away" (''pulsa javnosti vrlo fluidna kada su izbori još relativno daleko'').<ref name=":23">{{Cite web |last=Valtner |first=Lidija |date=20 September 2023 |title=Zašto istraživanja javnog mnjenja sada treba uzimati sa dozom sumnje? |trans-title=Why should public opinion polls be taken with a grain of salt now? |url=https://www.danas.rs/vesti/politika/istrazivanje-javnog-mnjenja-rejting/ |access-date=14 October 2023 |website=[[Danas (newspaper)|Danas]] |language=sr}}</ref> Besides Stata, CRTA has also published a scenario poll in October 2023.<ref>{{Cite web |date=18 October 2023 |title=Proevropski ili nacionalni: Koji blok je širi? |trans-title=Pro-European or the national: which bloc is wider? |url=https://nova.rs/emisije/proevropski-ili-nacionalni-koji-blok-je-siri/ |access-date=18 October 2023 |website=[[NOVA portal]] |language=sr}}</ref>

The Bureau of Social Research (BIRODI) has criticised opinion polling in which "information about the name of the agency that conducted the opinion poll, the individual who ordered the opinion poll, the number of respondents, the time when the opinion poll was carried out, as well as the question that were asked to the respondents" (''ko je naručilac istraživanja, ko je sproveo istraživanje, u kojem periodu i sa kojom tehnikom su prikupljeni podaci, u kojem uzorku, sa kojom uzoračkom greškom'') is not present, and has called news agencies to not publish those opinion polls. BIRODI stated these organisations "give the opportunity to use opinion polls for propaganda purposes" (''daje mogućnost da se istraživanja javnog mnjena koriste u propagandne svrhe'') and noted that the elements lead to the "deprofessionalisation of a public opinion researcher" (''deprofesionalizacije profesije istraživača javnog mnjenja'').<ref name=":24">{{Cite web |date=26 July 2023 |title=BIRODI: Mediji da ne objavljuju istraživanja javnog mnjenja ako se ne zna naručilac istraživanja |trans-title=BIRODI: The media should not publish public opinion surveys if the person who commissioned the survey is not known |url=https://www.danas.rs/vesti/drustvo/birodi-mediji-da-ne-objavljuju-istrazivanja-javnog-mnjenja-ako-se-ne-zna-narucilac-istrazivanja/ |access-date=14 October 2023 |website=[[Danas (newspaper)|Danas]] |language=sr}}</ref> Srećko Mihailović of Demostat has also stated that most opinion polls in Serbia are "biased and unprofessional" (''pristrasna i neprofesionalna''), claiming that "clients are political parties and the government, and researchers manipulate the ratings of parties" (''naručioci su političke stranke i vlast, a istraživači manipulišu i sa rejtinzima stranaka'') in opinion polls.<ref>{{Cite web |date=7 July 2023 |title=Srećko Mihailović: Istraživanja javnog mnjenja u Srbiji su uglavnom neprofesionalna i pristrasna |trans-title=Srećko Mihailović: Public opinion surveys in Serbia are mostly unprofessional and biased |url=https://www.danas.rs/vesti/drustvo/srecko-mihailovic-istrazivanja-javnog-mnjenja-u-srbiji-su-uglavnom-neprofesionalna-i-pristrasna/ |access-date=14 October 2023 |website=[[Danas (newspaper)|Danas]] |language=sr}}</ref> The [[World Association for Public Opinion Research]], an international professional association of opinion poll researchers, has listed Serbia as a country where there is a denial of the right to public opinion research, stating that "there is pressure from the government, politicians, and some media" (''na njih vrši pritisak od strane vlade, političara ali i pojedinih medija'').<ref>{{Cite web |last=Živanović |first=Katarina |date=20 April 2022 |title=Gavrilović: Istraživači prolaze "toplog zeca" kada objave rezultate koji "žuljaju" vlast |trans-title=Gavrilović: Researchers go through a "hot rabbit" when they publish results that "scald" the government |url=https://www.danas.rs/vesti/drustvo/gavrilovic-istrazivaci-prolaze-toplog-zeca-kada-objave-rezultate-koji-zuljaju-vlast/ |access-date=14 October 2023 |website=[[Danas (newspaper)|Danas]] |language=sr}}</ref>
