== Conduct ==
On election day, 17 December, voting stations were opened from 07:00 to 20:00.<ref name="RIK_rokovi">{{cite web |date=4 November 2023 |title=RIK: Određeni rokovi za izborne radnje |trans-title=RIK: Deadlines for electoral actions have been set |url=https://n1info.rs/vesti/izbori-2023/rik-odredjeni-rokovi-za-izborne-radnje/ |access-date=9 November 2023 |website=[[N1 (TV channel)|N1]] |language=sr}}</ref> Monitoring and non-governmental organisations, such as [[CeSID]] and CRTA, reported that the election day was marked with [[electoral fraud]].<ref name=":48">{{Cite web |date=17 December 2023 |title=CeSID dosad zabeležio više od 50 nepravilnosti na izborima |trans-title=So far, CeSID recorded more than 50 irregularities in the elections |url=https://n1info.rs/vesti/izbori-2023/cesid-dosad-zabelazio-vise-od-50-nepravilsnosti-na-izborima/ |access-date=18 December 2023 |website=[[N1 (TV channel)|N1]] |language=sr}}</ref><ref name=":58">{{Cite news |date=18 December 2023 |title=Serbia's ruling populists claim sweeping victory in election amid vote-rigging accusations |url=https://www.theguardian.com/world/2023/dec/18/serbia-election-results-populist-party-victory-vote-rigging-accusations |access-date=18 December 2023 |work=[[The Guardian]] |issn=0261-3077}}</ref><ref>{{Cite news |last1=Kirby |first1=Paul |last2=Delauney |first2=Guy |date=17 December 2023 |title=Serbia election: Vucic claims big election victory for ruling party |url=https://www.bbc.com/news/world-europe-67742032 |access-date=18 December 2023 |work=[[BBC News]]}}</ref><ref>{{Cite news |last=Vasović |first=Aleksandar |date=18 December 2023 |title=Serbia's ruling SNS set to win election, Vucic declares victory |url=https://www.reuters.com/world/europe/serbians-vote-snap-election-ruling-party-set-secure-another-term-2023-12-17/ |access-date=18 December 2023 |work=[[Reuters]]}}</ref> By 9:00, CeSID reported over 50 irregularities, this included irregularities such as non-compliance of procedures by members of election committees and voters photographing or recording their ballot papers, while Kreni-Promeni reported instances of irregularities, including the [[Bulgarian train]] vote-rigging method at voting stations in [[New Belgrade]].<ref name=":48" /> Nedeljkov from CRTA also reported that in [[Odžaci]] CRTA observers were physically attacked and that their cars sustained damage from the attackers. In Odžaci, CRTA observers reported an instance of a Bulgarian train.<ref name=":49">{{Cite web |date=17 December 2023 |title=Nedeljkov: Napadnuti posmatrači Crte i uništeno im vozilo u Odžacima |trans-title=Nedeljkov: CRTA observers attacked and their vehicle destroyed in Odžaci |url=https://n1info.rs/vesti/izbori-2023/nedeljkov-napadnuti-posmatraci-crte-i-unisteno-im-vozilo-u-odzacima/ |access-date=18 December 2023 |website=[[N1 (TV channel)|N1]] |language=sr}}</ref> Throughout the rest of the election day, CeSID continued to report more irregularities and intimidation.<ref>{{Cite web |date=17 December 2023 |title=Porodično glasanje, pritisak na birače: CeSID objavio nepravilnosti od 14 do 17 časova |trans-title=Family voting, pressure on voters: CeSID announced irregularities from 14:00 to 17:00 |url=https://n1info.rs/vesti/izbori-2023/porodicno-glasanje-pritisak-na-birace-cesid-objavio-nepravilnosti-od-14-do-17-casova/ |access-date=18 December 2023 |website=[[N1 (TV channel)|N1]] |language=sr}}</ref> Parandilović from SPN also published a video in which two [[Priboj]] councillor candidates were spotted rigging election ballots.<ref>{{Cite web |date=17 December 2023 |title=Parandilović: Odbornik SNS u kafani u Priboju prekraja izbornu volju građana |trans-title=Parandilović: Members of SNS in a pub in Priboj are destroying the electoral will of the citizens |url=https://n1info.rs/vesti/parandilovic-odbornik-sns-u-kafani-u-priboju-prekraja-izbornu-volju-gradjana-foto/ |access-date=18 December 2023 |website=[[N1 (TV channel)|N1]] |language=sr}}</ref>

Voters from [[Republika Srpska]] were also driven to the [[Štark Arena]] in Belgrade.<ref>{{Cite web |last=Opačić |first=Ana |date=17 December 2023 |title=Birači iz Republike Srpske organizovano u Areni, odakle se preusmeravaju gde da glasaju |trans-title=Voters from Republika Srpska are organised in the Arena, from where they are redirected to where to vote |url=https://n1info.rs/vesti/izbori-2023/audio-video-biraci-iz-republike-srpske-organizovano-u-areni-odakle-se-preusmeravaju-gde-da-glasaju/ |access-date=18 December 2023 |website=[[N1 (TV channel)|N1]] |language=sr}}</ref> Despite Štark Arena not being a voting station, voters from Republika Srpska confirmed that the Arena was used illegally as a voting station and as a redirect station towards official voting stations in Belgrade.<ref>{{Cite web |date=17 December 2023 |title=Došla ova televizija N: Obezbeđenje objašnjava proceduru za glasanje u Areni za ljude iz BiH |trans-title="This television N has arrived": Security explains the procedure for voting in the Arena for people from Bosnia and Herzegovina |url=https://n1info.rs/vesti/izbori-2023/video-dosla-ova-televizija-n-obezbedjenje-objasnjava-proceduru-za-glasanje-u-areni-za-ljude-iz-bih/ |access-date=18 December 2023 |website=[[N1 (TV channel)|N1]] |language=sr}}</ref> The security at the Štark Arena did not allow members of RIK to enter the building.<ref>{{Cite web |date=17 December 2023 |title=Pripadnici obezbeđenja u Areni izbacili članove RIK-a |trans-title=The members of the security in the Arena kicked out the members of the RIK |url=https://n1info.rs/vesti/izbori-2023/statisti-statisti-pripadnici-obezbedjenja-u-areni-izbacili-clanove-rik-a/ |access-date=18 December 2023 |website=[[N1 (TV channel)|N1]] |language=sr}}</ref> Brnabić said that she did not see what was irregular or illegal with the Štark Arena serving as a redirect station for voters from Republika Srpska.<ref>{{Cite web |date=17 December 2023 |title=Brnabić se oglasila povodom glasača iz Republike Srpske u Areni |trans-title=Brnabić spoke about the voters from Republika Srpska in the Arena |url=https://n1info.rs/vesti/izbori-2023/brnabic-se-oglasila-povodom-glasaca-iz-republike-srpske-u-areni/ |access-date=18 December 2023 |website=[[N1 (TV channel)|N1]] |language=sr}}</ref> Miodrag Jovanović, a professor at the Faculty of Law, said that in regards to the Arena and the phantom voters{{Efn|Phantom voters are a type of voters that exist in the voters list but do not reside at the listed location, thus cannot legally vote in the municipality or a city that is listed in the list.<ref>{{cite web |url=https://n1info.rs/vesti/izbori-2023/da-li-fantomi-zive-medju-nama-ako-ih-niko-nije-video-ni-cuo-zasto-ih-drzava-zove-na-glasanje/ |title=Da li fantomi žive među nama? Ako ih niko nije video ni čuo, zašto ih država zove na glasanje |trans-title=Do phantoms live among us? If no one has ever heard about them, why is the country calling them to vote |last=Bulajić |first=Žana |date=7 December 2023 |access-date=21 June 2024 |website=[[N1 (TV channel)|N1]] |lang=sr |archive-date=21 June 2024 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240621220838/https://n1info.rs/vesti/izbori-2023/da-li-fantomi-zive-medju-nama-ako-ih-niko-nije-video-ni-cuo-zasto-ih-drzava-zove-na-glasanje/ |url-status=live }}</ref>}} (''fantomski glasači''), "it is illegal for someone to have a residence where he does not live" (''zabranjeno da neko ima prebivalište tamo gde ne živi'').<ref>{{Cite web |last=Kuzmanović |first=Aleksandra |date=17 December 2023 |title="Zabranjeno da neko ima prebivalište tamo gde ne živi": Profesor o biračima iz RS u Areni |trans-title="It is forbidden for someone to have a residence where he does not live": Professor on voters from RS in Arena |url=https://n1info.rs/vesti/izbori-2023/zabranjeno-da-neko-ima-prebivaliste-tamo-gde-ne-zivi-profesor-o-biracima-iz-rs-u-areni/ |access-date=18 December 2023 |website=[[N1 (TV channel)|N1]] |language=sr}}</ref>

In its report, ODIHR concluded that SNS had a "systematic advantage which created unfair conditions in the elections" and that Vučić heavily dominated the election campaign, despite not being a candidate in it. According to ODIHR, there was abuse of public funds, and the media monitoring body, Regulatory Body for Electronic Media, was also not efficient during the election campaign, and that despite the elections being well organised, they were organised in a "societal and political divided ambience". ODIHR said that the campaign was polarised and met with negative campaigning and [[fearmongering]].<ref name=":57">{{Cite web |date=18 December 2023 |title=ODIHR: Ozbiljne neregularnosti na izborima, predsednik doneo prednost jednoj listi |trans-title=ODIHR: Serious irregularities in the elections, the president favoured only one list |url=https://n1info.rs/vesti/izbori-2023/izbori-rezultati-2023-odihr-srbija/ |access-date=18 December 2023 |website=[[N1 (TV channel)|N1]] |language=sr}}</ref> The [[Federal Foreign Office]] of Germany said that abuse of public funds, fearmongering of voters, and vote buying is "unacceptable for a country with the status of a candidate for EU membership".<ref>{{Cite web |date=18 December 2023 |title=Nemačko ministarstvo o izborima u Srbiji: Neprihvatljivo za zemlju sa statusom kandidata za EU |trans-title=The German Ministry on the elections in Serbia: Unacceptable for a country with EU candidate status |url=https://n1info.rs/vesti/izbori-2023/nemacko-ministarstvo-o-izborima-u-srbiji-neprihvatljivo-za-zemlju-sa-statusom-kandidata-za-eu/ |access-date=18 December 2023 |website=[[N1 (TV channel)|N1]] |language=sr}}</ref>

{{Ill|Stefan Schennach|de|Stefan Schennach}}, the chief of the delegation of PACE that monitored the elections, said that "the elections were not fair" and that he had seen "ballots that were printed by a photocopier".<ref>{{Cite web |date=19 December 2023 |title=Šef posmatračke delegacije: Istina je šokantna, video sam listiće napravljene u kopirnici |trans-title=Head of the observation delegation: The truth is shocking, I saw ballots made in the copy shop |url=https://n1info.rs/vesti/izbori-2023/sef-delegacije-parlamentarne-skupstine-se-istina-je-sokantna-video-sam-listice-napravljene-u-kopirnici/ |access-date=20 December 2023 |website=[[N1 (TV channel)|N1]] |language=sr}}</ref> In a joint statement, [[Josep Borrell]] and [[Olivér Várhelyi]], on behalf of the European Commission, said that Serbia's "electoral process requires tangible improvement and further reform".<ref>{{Cite news |last1=Psaledakis |first1=Daphne |last2=Singh |first2=Kanishka |date=20 December 2023 |title=EU, US urge Serbia to address concerns about electoral process |url=https://www.reuters.com/world/europe/eu-us-urge-serbia-address-concerns-about-electoral-process-2023-12-19/ |access-date=20 December 2023 |work=[[Reuters]]}}</ref> Political scientist [[Florian Bieber]] said that "irregularities appeared to be more widespread than in previous [elections]".<ref>{{Cite news |last=Bayer |first=Lili |date=18 December 2023 |title=Serbia's elections held under 'unjust conditions', say international observers |url=https://www.theguardian.com/world/2023/dec/18/serbias-elections-under-unjust-conditions-say-international-observers |access-date=20 December 2023 |work=[[The Guardian]] |issn=0261-3077}}</ref> [[Matthew Miller (spokesperson)|Matthew Miller]], the spokesperson of the [[United States Department of State]], called for the government of Serbia to investigate the irregularities that occurred.<ref>{{Cite web |date=19 December 2023 |title=SAD: Pozivamo Srbiju da istraži navode o neregularnostima na izborima |trans-title=USA: We call on Serbia to investigate allegations of irregularities in the elections |url=https://n1info.rs/vesti/izbori-2023/sad-pozivamo-srbiju-da-istrazi-navode-o-neregularnostima-na-izborima/ |access-date=20 December 2023 |website=[[N1 (TV channel)|N1]] |language=sr}}</ref> United States senators [[Jeanne Shaheen]] and [[Pete Ricketts]] also called for the government to "urgently consider whether elections should be repeated in certain regions", saying that the elections were not free and fair.<ref>{{Cite web |date=20 December 2023 |title=Američki senatori: Izbori u Srbiji ni slobodni ni fer |trans-title=American senators: Elections in Serbia are neither free nor fair |url=https://n1info.rs/vesti/izbori-2023/americki-senatori-izbori-u-srbiji-ni-slobodni-ni-fer/ |access-date=20 December 2023 |website=[[N1 (TV channel)|N1]] |language=sr}}</ref> [[Andreas Schieder]], who monitored the elections on behalf of the European Parliament, criticised Brnabić, saying that "the government should work on solving numerous claims about pressure on voters, vote buying, violating voting secrecy, biased media, and the president's involvement in the campaign".<ref>{{Cite web |date=22 December 2023 |title=Šider: Brnabić širi dezinformacije o meni, napada posmatrače umesto da se pozabavi nepravilnostima |trans-title=Schieder: Brnabić is spreading misinformation about me and is attacking observers instead of dealing with irregularities |url=https://n1info.rs/vesti/izbori-2023/sider-brnabic-siri-dezinformacije-o-meni-napada-posmatrace-umesto-da-se-pozabavi-nepravilnostima/ |access-date=23 December 2023 |website=[[N1 (TV channel)|N1]] |language=sr}}</ref>

Vučić and SNS denied all of the electoral fraud allegations.<ref name=":58" /> Brnabić accused the opposition and CRTA of "destabilising Serbia and its constitutional order" (''destabilizuju zemlju i uruše ustavni poredak'') and verbally attacked Schennach and Schieder due to them criticising the conduct of the election.<ref>{{Cite web |date=22 December 2023 |title=Brnabić: Opozicija, CRTA i druge NVO pokušavaju da destabilizuju zemlju |trans-title=Brnabić: The opposition, CRTA and other NGOs are trying to destabilize the country |url=https://www.tanjug.rs/izbori-2023/vesti/65942/brnabic-opozicija-crta-i-druge-nvo-pokusavaju-da-destabilizuju-zemlju/vest |access-date=23 December 2023 |website=[[Tačno d.o.o.|Tanjug]] |language=sr}}</ref><ref>{{Cite web |date=22 December 2023 |title=Evropski posmatrači o kritikama vlasti u Beogradu: Ovo pokazuje da smo pogodili tačku |trans-title=European observers on criticism of the authorities in Belgrade: This shows that we have hit the spot |url=https://n1info.rs/vesti/izbori-2023/evropski-posmatraci-o-kritikama-vlasti-u-beogradu-ovo-pokazuje-da-smo-pogodili-tacku/ |access-date=23 December 2023 |website=[[N1 (TV channel)|N1]] |language=sr}}</ref>

== Results ==
There were 6,500,666 citizens in total who had the right to vote in the parliamentary election.<ref>{{Cite web |date=15 December 2023 |title=RIK: Na vanrednim parlamentarnim izborima pravo glasa ima 6.500.666 birača |trans-title=RIK: In the extraordinary parliamentary elections, 6,500,666 voters have the right to vote |url=https://n1info.rs/vesti/izbori-2023/rik-na-vanrednim-parlamentarnim-izborima-pravo-glasa-ima-6-500-666-biraca/ |access-date=15 December 2023 |website=[[N1 (TV channel)|N1]] |language=sr}}</ref> Out of 8,273 voting stations in total, voters abroad could have voted at 81 voting stations in 35 different countries.<ref name=":41">{{Cite web |date=27 November 2023 |title=Cesid objavio gde može da se glasa u inostranstvu: 81 biračko mesto u 35 zemalja širom sveta |trans-title=Cesid announced where you can vote abroad: 81 polling stations in 35 countries around the world |url=https://www.danas.rs/vesti/politika/izbori-2023/cesid-glasanje-u-inistranstvu/ |access-date=27 November 2023 |website=[[Danas (newspaper)|Danas]] |language=sr}}</ref><ref>{{Cite web |title=Počelo štampanje glasačkih listića; Dimitrijević: Rekordan broj mesta za glasanje u inostranstvu |trans-title=Printing of ballots has begun, Dimitrijević: Record number of places to vote abroad |url=https://www.rts.rs/lat/vesti/izbori-2023/5323145/stampanje-glasackih-listica-rik-.html |access-date=6 December 2023 |website=[[Radio Television of Serbia]] |language=sr}}</ref> 32,216 dual citizens registered to take part in the elections abroad.<ref name=":41" /> In Canada, Portugal, the United Kingdom, and the United States, voting occurred on 16 December from 07:00 to 20:00.<ref name="RIK_27Nov"/> Elections were repeated at 30 voting stations in 19 different municipalities on 30 December.<ref>{{Cite web |date=20 December 2023 |title=Na kojim će se sve biračkim mestima ponoviti glasanje 30. decembra |trans-title=At which voting stations will the voting be repeated on December 30 |url=https://n1info.rs/vesti/izbori-2023/na-kojim-ce-se-sve-birackim-mestima-ponoviti-glasanje-30-decembra/ |access-date=21 December 2023 |website=[[N1 (TV channel)|N1]] |language=sr}}</ref>

After the voting stations were closed, CeSID/Ipsos and CRTA were the first to report their projections of the results.<ref>{{Cite web |date=17 December 2023 |title=IPSOS/CeSID: Projekcija rezultata parlamentarnih izbora |trans-title=IPSOS/CeSID: Projection of parliamentary election results |url=https://n1info.rs/vesti/izbori-2023/najnovije-vesti-izbori-2023-rezultati/ |access-date=18 December 2023 |website=[[N1 (TV channel)|N1]] |language=sr}}</ref><ref>{{Cite web |date=17 December 2023 |title=CRTA objavila rezultate na osnovu 95 odsto obrađenog uzorka |trans-title=CRTA published results based on 95 percent of the processed sample |url=https://n1info.rs/vesti/izbori-2023/crta-koalicija-oko-sns-osvojila-46-9-odsto/ |access-date=18 December 2023 |website=[[N1 (TV channel)|N1]] |language=sr}}</ref> According to the 18 December projection from CeSID/Ipsos, SNS won 46% of popular vote and 128 seats in the National Assembly, successfully returning its parliamentary majority, while SPN placed second, with 23.6% of popular vote and 65 seats in the National Assembly. According to CeSID/Ipsos, SPS only won 6% of popular vote and 18 seats in the National Assembly, this being the worst result of SPS since the [[2007 Serbian parliamentary election|2007 parliamentary election]], while NADA won 4.9% of popular vote. In a surprise move, Nestorović's MI–GIN also crossed the threshold, winning 13 seats in total. Out of the minority lists, VMSZ won 6 seats, SPP–DSHV won 3 seats, SDAS won 2 seats, and SDAS and Russian Party won one seat respectively.<ref name=":50">{{Cite web |date=18 December 2023 |title=CeSID i IPSOS obradili 97,2 odsto uzorka – SNS-u 128 mandata, SPN-u 65 |trans-title=CeSID and IPSOS processed 97.2 percent of the sample – SNS 128 mandates, SPN 65 |url=https://n1info.rs/vesti/izbori-2023/cesid-i-ipsos-obradili-972-odsto-uzorka-sns-u-128-mandata-spn-u-65/ |access-date=18 December 2023 |website=[[N1 (TV channel)|N1]] |language=sr}}</ref> The NO coalition of Dveri and SSZ failed to cross the threshold, winning only 2.8% of popular vote.<ref>{{Cite web |date=18 December 2023 |title=Poslednji podaci RIK-a i PIK-a: SNS blizu 50 odsto, Dveri i Zavetnici ispod cenzusa |trans-title=Latest data from RIK and PIK: SNS close to 50 percent, Dveri and Oathkeepers are below the threshold |url=https://n1info.rs/vesti/izbori-2023/poslednji-podaci-rik-a-i-pik-a-sns-blizu-50-odsto-dveri-i-zavetnici-ispod-cenzusa/ |access-date=18 December 2023 |website=[[N1 (TV channel)|N1]] |language=sr}}</ref> SNS received the most votes abroad.<ref>{{Cite web |date=21 December 2023 |title=RIK: SNS osvojio najviše glasova u inostranstvu, sledi "Srbija protiv nasilja" |trans-title=RIK: SNS won the most votes abroad, followed by Serbia Against Violence |url=https://www.rts.rs/lat/vesti/izbori-2023/5332440/rik-glasanje-inostranstvo-rezultati.html |access-date=21 December 2023 |website=[[Radio Television of Serbia]] |language=sr}}</ref>

RIK broadcast the results live, with the results being updated every 5 minutes.<ref>{{Cite web |date=17 December 2023 |title=Vladimir Dimitrijević: Izborni rezultati moći će uživo da se prate |trans-title=Vladimir Dimitrijević: The election results will be able to be followed live |url=https://www.tanjug.rs/izbori-2023/vesti/65155/vladimir-dimitrijevic-izborni-rezultati-moci-ce-uzivo-da-se-prate/vest |access-date=18 December 2023 |website=[[Tačno d.o.o.|Tanjug]] |language=sr}}</ref> RIK published the final results on 12 January.<ref>{{Cite news |date=12 January 2024 |title=RIK proglasio konačne rezultate parlamentarnih izbora u Srbiji |trans-title=REC announced the final results of the parliamentary elections in Serbia |url=https://www.slobodnaevropa.org/a/srbija-rik-rezultati-izbora/32772231.html |access-date=22 June 2024 |work=[[Radio Free Europe]] |language=sr}}</ref> After the publishing of the overall report on the election, RIK awarded the candidates the seats of the National Assembly in less than 10 days.<ref name="RIK_rokovi" />

== Reactions ==
SNS proclaimed victory after the voting stations were closed.<ref>{{Cite web |date=17 December 2023 |title=Brnabić: "Srbija ne sme da stane" ima 47,1 posto, imaćemo više od 125 poslanika |trans-title=Brnabić: "Serbia must not stop" has 47.1 percent, we will have more than 125 deputies |url=https://n1info.rs/vesti/izbori-2023/brnabic-srbija-ne-sme-da-stane-ima-471-posto-na-osnovu-uzorka-od-50-procenata/ |access-date=18 December 2023 |website=[[N1 (TV channel)|N1]] |language=sr}}</ref> SNS was congratulated by Dačić and [[Milorad Dodik]], the president of Republika Srpska, and [[Katalin Novák]], the president of Hungary.<ref name=":51">{{Cite web |date=17 December 2023 |title=Dačić: Potrebno je naći novog lidera SPS |trans-title=Dacic: It is necessary to find a new SPS leader |url=https://n1info.rs/vesti/izbori-2023/dacic-potrebno-je-naci-novog-lidera-sps/ |access-date=18 December 2023 |website=[[N1 (TV channel)|N1]] |language=sr}}</ref><ref>{{Cite web |date=18 December 2023 |title=Dodik čestitao Vučiću: Ponosan sam na sve iz RS koji su glasali |trans-title=Dodik congratulated Vučić: I am proud of everyone from RS who voted |url=https://n1info.rs/vesti/izbori-2023/dodik-cestitao-vucicu-ponosan-sam-na-sve-iz-rs-koji-su-glasali/ |access-date=18 December 2023 |website=[[N1 (TV channel)|N1]] |language=sr}}</ref><ref>{{Cite web |date=18 December 2023 |title=Mađarska predsednica čestitala Vučiću i SNS na "velikoj izbornoj pobedi" |trans-title=The Hungarian president congratulated Vučić and SNS on the "great election victory" |url=https://www.tanjug.rs/izbori-2023/vesti/65230/madarska-predsednica-cestitala-vucicu-i-sns-na-velikoj-izbornoj-pobedi/vest |access-date=18 December 2023 |website=[[Tačno d.o.o.|Tanjug]] |language=sr}}</ref> Vučić alleged that a "an important country intervened in the election process of Serbia in the most brutal way" (''jedne važne zemlje u izborni proces Srbije na najbrutalniji način'').<ref>{{Cite web |date=21 December 2023 |title=Vučić: Sastavljamo važno pismo o najbrutalnijem mešanju jedne važne zemlje u izbore u Srbiji |trans-title=Vučić: We are writing an important letter about the most brutal interference of an important country in the elections in Serbia |url=https://n1info.rs/vesti/vucic-sastavljamo-vazno-pismo-o-najbrutalnijem-mesanju-jedne-vazne-zemlje-u-izbore-u-srbiji/ |access-date=21 December 2023 |website=[[N1 (TV channel)|N1]] |language=sr}}</ref>

Nestorović of MI–GIN said that "even though no one gave us a chance, we became one of the four or five strongest parties" (''iako im niko nije davao šanse, ušli u krug četiri, pet najjačih partija''); he rejected cooperating with SNS or SPN after the elections.<ref>{{Cite web |date=17 December 2023 |title=Nestorović za N1: Nećemo sarađivati ni sa jednima ni sa drugima |trans-title=Nestorović for N1: We will not cooperate with any of them |url=https://n1info.rs/vesti/izbori-2023/nestorovic-niko-nam-nije-davao-sanse-ali-smo-postigli-veliki-uspeh/ |access-date=18 December 2023 |website=[[N1 (TV channel)|N1]] |language=sr}}</ref> ''Danas'' newspaper described Nestorović as "the biggest surprise" (''najveće iznaneđenje'') of the 2023 elections.<ref>{{Cite web |date=18 December 2023 |title=Izbori u Srbiji, dan posle: Najveće iznenađenje Nestorović |trans-title=Elections in Serbia, the day after: Nestorović's biggest surprise |url=https://www.danas.rs/vesti/politika/izbori-2023/izbori-u-srbiji-dan-posle-najvece-iznenadjenje-nestorovic/ |access-date=18 December 2023 |website=[[Danas (newspaper)|Danas]] |language=sr}}</ref> At a SPS press conference, Dačić was dissatisfied with the result.<ref name=":51" /> Pásztor said that VMSZ "achieved the election result that we wanted" (''rezultat kakav smo želeli'') and they were ready to join the next SNS-led government.<ref>{{Cite web |date=18 December 2023 |title=Pastor: Rezultat kakav smo želeli, koalicija samo sa SNS |trans-title=Pastor: We got the result we wanted, coalition only with SNS |url=https://n1info.rs/vesti/izbori-2023/pastor-rezultat-kakav-smo-zeleli-koalicija-samo-sa-sns/ |access-date=18 December 2023 |website=[[N1 (TV channel)|N1]] |language=sr}}</ref>

Miloš Bešić, a professor at the Faculty of Political Sciences, said that the society in Serbia "is even more divided after the elections" (''društvo podeljenije nego pre izbora'') and argued that "the failure of right-wing parties is one of the main impressions of the voting results" (''neuspeh desnice jedan od glavnih utisaka rezultata glasanja''). Bešić also said that the attacks of SNS on SPS during the election campaign was also shown during the election day, due to the decrease in support of SPS and an increase in support of SNS. He, however, noted that both SNS and SPS combined won fewer votes than in the 2022 election.<ref name=":56">{{Cite web |date=17 December 2023 |title=Bešić: Naše društvo podeljenije nego pre izbora, neuspeh desnice jedan od glavnih utisaka nakon glasanja |trans-title=Bešić: Our society is more divided than before the election, the failure of the right wing one of the main impressions after the vote |url=https://n1info.rs/vesti/izbori-2023/besic-nase-drustvo-podeljenije-nego-pre-izbora-neuspeh-desnice-jedan-od-glavnih-utisaka-nakon-glasanja/ |access-date=18 December 2023 |website=[[N1 (TV channel)|N1]] |language=sr}}</ref>

== Aftermath ==
Due to failing to gain parliamentary representation, Obradović of Dveri and all members of the presidency of Narodna, including president Jeremić, resigned from their positions.<ref>{{Cite web |date=23 December 2023 |title=Boško Obradović podneo ostavku na mesto predsednika Dveri |trans-title=Boško Obradović resigns as president of Dveri |url=https://www.euronews.rs/srbija/politika/109062/bosko-obradovic-podneo-ostavku-na-mesto-predsednika-dveri/vest |access-date=23 December 2023 |website=[[Euronews]] |language=sr}}</ref><ref>{{Cite web |date=23 December 2023 |title=Svi članovi Predsedništva Narodne stranke podneli ostavke |trans-title=All members of the presidency of the People's Party resigned from their positions |url=https://n1info.rs/vesti/izbori-2023/svi-clanovi-predsednistva-narodne-stranke-podneli-ostavke/ |access-date=23 December 2023 |website=[[N1 (TV channel)|N1]] |language=sr}}</ref>

The [[Economist Intelligence Unit]] (EIU) and ''Danas'' newspaper reported in early December that on 22 September, Vučić signed an agreement with the [[European Commission]] on the production of lithium batteries in Serbia. The government of Serbia previously cancelled the [[Rio Tinto (corporation)|Rio Tinto]] lithium mine project in January 2022, amidst the [[2021–2022 Serbian environmental protests|environmental protests]], but the EIU reported that in the September 2023 agreement "the government [of Serbia] has not given up on a plan to allow the mining of lithium at Jadar". The agreement also includes a construction of another factory in [[Ćuprija]]. EIU stated that due to the 2023 parliamentary election, "the government is likely to stall the plans, reviving them only once the December election is over".<ref name=":47">{{Cite web |last=Howey |first=William |date=5 December 2023 |title=Serbia revives lithium mining plans with EU agreement |url=https://services.eiu.com/serbia-revives-lithium-mining-plans-with-eu-agreement/ |access-date=9 December 2023 |website=[[Economist Intelligence Unit]]}}</ref> In June 2024, ''[[Financial Times]]'' published an article regarding the topic, revealing that Serbia would "give green light to Rio Tinto" and its Project Jadar.<ref>{{Cite web |last1=Dunai |first1=Marton |last2=Russell |first2=Alec |date=16 June 2024 |title=Serbia set to give green light to Rio Tinto lithium mine |url=https://www.ft.com/content/2bd0d74e-ff22-442e-8be1-1250fe4bf826 |access-date=22 June 2024 |website=[[Financial Times]]}}</ref> ''[[Neue Zürcher Zeitung]]'' revealed the same.<ref>{{Cite web |last=Dedović |first=Dragoslav |date=19 June 2024 |title=Vučićev poljubac za Rio Tinto |trans-title=Vučić's kiss for Rio Tinto |url=https://www.dw.com/sr/vu%C4%8Di%C4%87ev-poljubac-za-rio-tinto/a-69411559 |access-date=22 June 2024 |website=[[Deutsche Welle]] |language=sr}}</ref> In July 2024, the government revived the Jadar project, which resulted in a [[2024 Serbian environmental protests|series of environmental protests]].<ref>{{Cite web |date=2024-07-16 |title=Vlada Srbije ponovo otvorila vrata Rio Tintu za iskopavanje litijuma, oštre osude ekoloških organizacija |trans-title=The Government of Serbia reopened the door to Rio Tinto for lithium mining, harsh condemnation of environmental organisations |url=https://www.glasamerike.net/a/srbija-zivotna-sredina-vlada-uredba-rio-tinto-litijum-jadar-ekologija/7700059.html |access-date=2024-07-30 |website=[[Voice of America]] |language=sr}}</ref><ref>{{Cite news |date=29 July 2024 |title=Rio Tinto u Srbiji: Demonstracije protiv rudnika litijuma, najava radikalizacije protesta |trans-title=Rio Tinto in Serbia: Demonstrations against lithium mines, announcement of radicalisation of protests |url=https://www.bbc.com/serbian/lat/srbija-69227364 |access-date=30 July 2024 |work=[[BBC News]] |language=sr}}</ref>

=== Protests ===
{{Further|2023 Serbian election protests}}
Following the elections on 17 December, SPN began organising protests outside the RIK building.<ref>{{cite web |date=18 December 2023 |title=Protesti opozicije pred zgradom RIK-a, traže poništavanje izbora u Beogradu |trans-title=Protest of the opposition in front of the RIK building, they are demanding the annulling of the elections in Belgrade |url=https://balkans.aljazeera.net/news/balkan/liveblog/2023/12/18/rik-na-osnovu-7-847-birackih-mesta-srbija-ne-sme-da-stane-4684-odsto-glasova |access-date=18 December 2023 |website=[[Al Jazeera Balkans]] |language=sr}}</ref> At the 18 December protest, Aleksić and Tepić announced that they would go on a [[hunger strike]] until the results of the Belgrade City Assembly elections are annulled.<ref>{{Cite web |date=18 December 2023 |title=Marinika Tepić i Miroslav Aleksić najavili štrajk glađu do poništenja beogradskih izbora |trans-title=Marinika Tepić and Miroslav Aleksić announced a hunger strike until the annulment of the Belgrade elections |url=https://www.danas.rs/vesti/politika/izbori-2023/marinika-tepic-i-miroslav-aleksic-najavili-strajk-gladju-do-ponistenja-beogradskih-izbora/ |access-date=18 December 2023 |website=[[Danas (newspaper)|Danas]] |language=sr}}</ref> SPN expanded their demands on 20 December by demanding the annulment of all 17 December election results.<ref>{{Cite web |date=20 December 2023 |title=Aleksić: Tražićemo poništavanje izbora na svim nivoima |trans-title=Aleksić: We will ask for the annulment of the elections at all levels |url=https://n1info.rs/vesti/izbori-2023/aleksic-trazicemo-ponistavanje-izbora-na-svim-nivoima/ |access-date=21 December 2023 |website=[[N1 (TV channel)|N1]] |language=sr}}</ref> Alongside SPN, NADA, Narodna, SDS, and Dveri also expressed their support for the annulment of 17 December election results and the scheduling of a new ones.<ref>{{Cite web |last=Milenković |first=Mirjana R. |date=21 December 2023 |title=Koje stranke opozicije još podržavaju ponavljanje izbora? |trans-title=Which opposition parties still support repeating the elections? |url=https://www.danas.rs/vesti/politika/izbori-2023/koje-stranke-opozicije-podrzavaju-ponavljanje-izbora/ |access-date=21 December 2023 |website=[[Danas (newspaper)|Danas]] |language=sr}}</ref> On 21 December, members of the National Assembly [[Jelena Milošević]] and [[Danijela Grujić]] joined Aleksić and Tepić in their hunger strike.<ref>{{Cite web |date=21 December 2023 |title="Pojačaćemo borbu još više": Štrajku glađu pridružuju se još dve poslanice |trans-title="We will strengthen the fight even more": two more MPs join the hunger strike |url=https://n1info.rs/vesti/izbori-2023/pojacacemo-borbu-jos-vise-strajku-gladju-pridruzuju-se-jos-dve-poslanice/ |access-date=21 December 2023 |website=[[N1 (TV channel)|N1]] |language=sr}}</ref> A day later, [[Janko Veselinović (lawyer)|Janko Veselinović]] and [[Željko Veselinović]] also began their hunger strike, while on 23 December MPs-elect [[Branko Miljuš (politician)|Branko Miljuš]] and [[Dušan Nikezić]] began their hunger strike.<ref>{{Cite web |date=22 December 2023 |title=U štrajk glađu stupaju i Janko Veselinović i Željko Veselinović |trans-title=Janko Veselinović and Željko Veselinović also go on hunger strike |url=https://n1info.rs/vesti/izbori-2023/u-strajk-gladju-stupaju-i-janko-veselinovic-i-zeljko-veselinovic/ |access-date=23 December 2023 |website=[[N1 (TV channel)|N1]] |language=sr}}</ref><ref>{{Cite web |date=23 December 2023 |title=Još jedan protest ispred RIK-a, u nedelju ističe rok za poništavanje izbora, u suprotnom – blokade |trans-title=Another protest in front of the RIK, the deadline for annulment of the election expires on Sunday, otherwise – blockades |url=https://www.glasamerike.net/a/balkan-srbija-izbori-protest-republicka-izborna-komisija-strajk-gladju/7410092.html |access-date=24 December 2023 |website=[[Voice of America]] |language=sr}}</ref>

After an attempt from councillors to enter the City Assembly of Belgrade, a [[riot]] occurred which resulted in an arrest of 38 demonstrators.<ref name=":05">{{Cite web |date=24 December 2023 === Government formation ===
{{Further|Cabinet of Miloš Vučević}}
On several occasions, Dačić expressed his support for continuing to work with SNS after the 2023 election.<ref name=":07">{{Cite web |date=21 October 2023 |title=Dačićeva čestitka SNS-u: Saradnja i posle pobede na decembarskim izborima |trans-title=Dačić's congratulations to SNS: Cooperation even after the victory in the December elections |url=https://n1info.rs/vesti/dacic-cestitao-sns-15-godina-od-osnivanja/ |access-date=23 October 2023 |website=[[N1 (TV channel)|N1]] |language=sr}}</ref><ref name=":111">{{Cite web |date=29 November 2023 |title=Ivica Dačić: Najbolje rešenje za Srbiju – Vučić predsednik, Dačić premijer; Sve podseća na drugi krug izbora 2000. godine |trans-title=Ivica Dačić: The best solution for Serbia – President Vučić, Prime Minister Dačić; Everything is reminiscent of the second round of the 2000 election |url=https://insajder.net/teme/ivica-dacic-najbolje-resenje-za-srbiju-vucic-predsednik-dacic-premijer-sve-podseca-na-drugi-krug-izbora-2000-godine |access-date=2 December 2023 |website=[[Insajder]] |language=sr}}</ref> In October, Dačić had said: "I am convinced that we will continue cooperation even after the victory in the December elections, in the interest of Serbia, and a better future for all the citizens of our country, as well as the Serbian people as a whole" (''Uveren sam da ćemo takvu saradnju nastaviti i posle pobede na decembarskim izborima, u interesu Srbije i bolje budućnosti svih građana naše zemlje, kao i srpskog naroda u celini'').<ref name=":07" /> In a November interview with ''Insajder'', Dačić said that the goal of SPS is "to win a parliamentary majority, together with SNS, because we alone cannot have a majority" (''Naš politički cilj je da osvojimo većinu, zajedno sa SNS-om, jer mi sami ne možemo da imamo većinu'') and that "the best solution for Serbia is [...] that Vučić should be president [...] and Dacić should be prime minister" (''najbolje rešenje za Srbiju'' [...] ''Vučić da bude predsednik'' [...] [''i''] ''Dačić premijer'').<ref name=":111" /> Dačić later said, in regards to SNS forming a government with SPS, that "[SPS] wants [to be in the government], but if they do not want us, then there is no problem" (''Mi hoćemo, ako oni ne žele, nikakav problem nije''); he has also criticised opposition parties and described them as "a big fraud called [[Democratic Opposition of Serbia|DOS]]" (''velika prevara koju on naziva DOS-om'').<ref>{{Cite web |date=2 December 2023 |title=Dačić: Ako SNS ne želi, SPS ne mora da bude u vlasti, ali od nas nema pouzdanijih |trans-title=Dacic: If SNS doesn't want to, SPS doesn't have to be in power, but there are none more reliable than us |url=https://www.rtv.rs/sr_lat/izbori-2023/parlamentarni-izbori/dacic-ako-sns-ne-zeli-sps-ne-mora-da-bude-u-vlasti-ali-od-nas-nema-pouzdanijih_1498336.html |access-date=2 December 2023 |website=[[Radio Television of Vojvodina]] |language=sr}}</ref> Other SPS politicians, like Paunović and [[Toma Fila]], expressed their support for continuing to work with SNS after the elections.<ref>{{Cite web |date=30 October 2023 |title=Snežana Paunović: SPS odlučila da na izbore ide sa dosadašnjim partnerima, posle izbora sa SNS |trans-title=Snežana Paunović: SPS decided to go to the elections with its previous partners, after the elections with the SNS |url=https://www.tanjug.rs/srbija/politika/56752/snezana-paunovic-sps-odlucila-da-na-izbore-ide-sa-dosadasnjim-partnerima-posle-izbora-sa-sns/vest |access-date=2 December 2023 |website=[[Tačno d.o.o.|Tanjug]] |language=sr}}</ref><ref>{{Cite web |date=27 November 2023 |title=Toma Fila: SPS će posle izbora biti u koaliciji sa SNS-om |trans-title=Toma Fila: SPS will be in a coalition with SNS after the elections |url=https://www.danas.rs/vesti/politika/izbori-2023/toma-fila-sps-ce-posle-izbora-biti-u-koaliciji-sa-sns-om/ |access-date=2 December 2023 |website=[[Danas (newspaper)|Danas]] |language=sr}}</ref>

Despite taking part with SNS in the Belgrade City assembly election, Vučić said that the next government would not include SRS due to programme differences, naming European Union as an example.<ref>{{Cite news |date=1 November 2023 |title=Vučić kaže da Srpska napredna stranka neće formirati vladu sa radikalima |trans-title=Vučić says that the Serbian Progressive Party will not form a government with Radicals |url=https://www.slobodnaevropa.org/a/vucic-seselj-koalicija-srbija-vlada-radikali/32666309.html |access-date=2 December 2023 |work=[[Radio Free Europe]] |language=sr}}</ref> Vučić also expressed doubts in SPS during the campaign period, while Brnabić criticised SPS officials such as Ružić, her former cabinet minister.<ref>{{Cite web |last=Savić |first=Danilo |date=3 December 2023 |title=Vučiću se komplikuje situacija pred izbore i panika je sve veća: Naprednjaci imaju samo jednog sigurnog saveznika |trans-title=The situation before the elections is getting complicated for Vučić and the panic is growing: the Progressives have only one reliable ally |url=https://nova.rs/vesti/politika/vucicu-se-komplikuje-situacija-pred-izbore-i-panika-je-sve-veca-naprednjaci-imaju-samo-jednog-sigurnog-saveznika/ |access-date=4 December 2023 |website=[[NOVA portal]] |language=sr}}</ref><ref>{{Cite web |date=5 December 2023 |title="Logične trzavice" između SNS i SPS: Pa tako Brnabić poredi Ružića s Đilasom |trans-title="Logical conflicts" between SNS and SPS: That's how Brnabić compares Ružić to Đilas |url=https://n1info.rs/vesti/izbori-2023/logicne-trzavice-izmedju-sns-i-sps-pa-tako-brnabic-poredi-ruzica-s-djilasom/ |access-date=6 December 2023 |website=[[N1 (TV channel)|N1]] |language=sr}}</ref> Vučević also said that "there are no guarantees that SPS will ... switch to the other side" (''nemamo garancije da SPS neće promeniti stranu'').<ref>{{Cite web |date=6 December 2023 |title=Miloš Vučević za Euronews Srbija: Građani biraju između Vučića i Đilasa, nemamo garancije da SPS neće promeniti stranu |trans-title=Miloš Vučević for Euronews Serbia: Citizens will choose between Vučić and Đilas, we have no guarantee that the SPS will not change sides |url=https://www.euronews.rs/srbija/politika/107222/milos-vucevic-za-euronews-srbija-gradani-biraju-izmedu-vucica-i-dilasa-nemamo-garancije-da-sps-nece-promeniti-stranu/vest |access-date=7 December 2023 |website=[[Euronews]] |language=sr}}</ref> Dušan Spasojević, a Faculty of Political Sciences professor, said that the "attacks on SPS are aimed to win back part of the voters who voted for the Socialists in the last elections, and perhaps to take over part of their voting base" (''Napadi na SPS imaju za cilj da povrate deo birača koji je na prošlim izborima glasao za socijaliste, a možda i da preuzmu deo njihove baze'').<ref>{{Cite web |last=Slavković |first=Stefan |date=4 December 2023 |title=Ko to tamo u SPS-u peva protiv Vučića: Predizborna varničenja partnera iz vlasti |trans-title=Who is that in the SPS singing against Vučić: Pre-election sparks of partners from the government |url=https://www.nin.rs/politika/vesti/41728/ko-to-tamo-u-sps-u-peva-protiv-vucica-predizborna-varnicenja-partnera-iz-vlasti/vest |access-date=7 December 2023 |website=[[NIN (magazine)|NIN]] |language=sr}}</ref> Popović of the Centre for Practical Politics argued the same.<ref>{{Cite web |last=Jelovac |first=Jelena |date=6 December 2023 |title=Ivica Dačić se pere, a Vučić nastavlja da ga ponižava na svakom koraku |trans-title=Ivica Dačić washes himself, and Vučić continues to humiliate him at every step |url=https://nova.rs/vesti/politika/ivica-dacic-se-pere-a-vucic-nastavlja-da-ga-ponizava-na-svakom-koraku/ |access-date=7 December 2023 |website=[[NOVA portal]] |language=sr}}</ref>

The constitutive session of the [[14th National Assembly of Serbia]] took place on 6 February.<ref>{{Cite news |date=6 February 2024 |title=Skupština Srbije konstituisana uz zvižduke, opozicija položila zakletvu u holu |trans-title=The National Assembly of Serbia was constituted with whistles, the opposition took the oath in the hall |url=https://www.slobodnaevropa.org/a/konstitutivna-sednica-novog-saziva-skupstine-srbije/32807299.html |access-date=22 June 2024 |work=[[Radio Free Europe]] |language=sr}}</ref> A month later, Brnabić was elected president of the National Assembly.<ref>{{Cite web |date=19 March 2024 |title=Ana Brnabić izabrana za predsednicu Skupštine Srbije |trans-title=Ana Brnabić was elected as the President of the National Assembly of Serbia |url=https://www.bbc.com/serbian/lat/srbija-68608274 |access-date=22 June 2024 |website=[[BBC News]] |language=sr}}</ref> After several months of negotiations, Vučević was given the mandate to form a government, after which he formed a government on 2 May. Besides SNS and SPS, his cabinet also included Đurđević Stamenkovski of SSZ that failed to gain representation in the National Assembly.<ref name=":60">{{Cite web |last=Milovančević |first=Vojislav |date=2 May 2024 |title=Izglasana nova Vlada Srbije: Ovo su ministri koji će je činiti |trans-title=The new Government of Serbia was voted in: These are the ministers who will make it up |url=https://nova.rs/vesti/politika/vlada-srbije-clanovi/ |access-date=22 June 2024 |website=[[NOVA portal]] |language=sr}}</ref>
